1b1(phal chen): / 'phags pa sangs rgyas ngal ba che zhes bya ba/ 
1b2(phal chen): ma da/ nu gsu ga/ de nas byang chub
1b3(phal chen):
2a1(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing ni tsam zhig tu bsam
2a2(phal chen): gyis mi khyab/ sang sa rgyas bcom ldan 'das nams kyi sngon gyi smon
2a3(phal chen): lam dang / 'byung ba rnam par dag pa ni ji tsam zhig tu bsam gyis mi khyad
2b1(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i gdung ni ji tsam zhig tu bsam gyis mi khyags
2b2(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas skye ba na ji tsam zhig tu bsam gyis mi khyab/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan
2b3(phal chen): 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshe/ gas pa'i skun ji tsam zhig tu bsam rgya// sa mi khyag sangs rgyas brtse
2b4(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung ni ji tsam zhig tu bsam gyis mi khyab/ sangs rgyas bcom
2b5(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes ni ji tsam zhig tu bsam gyis mi khyag sangs rgyas bcom
3a1(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa ni ji tsam zhig tu bsam gyis mi
3a2(phal chen): khyab/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chags pa mi mnga' ba'i rnam par spyod pa ni ji tsam zhig tu bsam
3a3(phal chen): gyis mi khyab// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi do rnam par thar pa ni ji tsam zhig tu
3a4(phal chen): bsam gyis mi khyab snyam pa dang nga / de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis byang chu ba sems dpa' de dag gi sems
3a5(phal chen): thugs kyis thugasu chud nas/ byang chub sems dpa' udat+pa la'i snying po// sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis byin tu
3a6(phal chen): brlab so// sangs rgyas kyi ye shes kyi byin dang ldan par mdzad do// de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'od kyis snang bar mdzad// sangs
3b1(phal chen): rgyas kyi gzi brjid kyis yongasu rgyas par mdzad do// sangs rgyas kyi mi 'jig pa la rab tu bzhago/ sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi dbyings la 'jug pa
3b2(phal chen): khong du chud par mdzad// sangs rgyas kyi bdag nyid che ba nyid dang / rdzu 'phrul gyi yul rab tu rtogs par mdzad do// chags pa med pa'i rgyud
3b3(phal chen): 'byam klas pa la rab tu bzhag go// sangs rgyas thams cad gcig nas gcig tu rgyud pa'i rigs rab tu rtogs par mdzad do// sangs
3b4(phal chen): rgyas kyi tshul gyi gnas brjod du med pa// la rab tu bzhag pa mdzad do// de nas byang chub sems dpa' ud la'i snying po chos kyi
3b5(phal chen): dbyings la 'jug pa rig cing khong du chud pas/ chags pa med pa'i dbyingasu bsgrubs pa'i yid dang / chos thaMd la bsgribs pa med par
3b6(phal chen): gaunas pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dang / kun tu bzang po'i smon lam dang ldan pa'i yang dag par 'jug pa dang / sangs rgyas
3b7(phal chen): thams cad kyi rje su song ba'i sangs rgyas blta ba dang / snying rje chen pos lta ba'i sems can thams cad yongasu spongs pa'i go cha chen po
4a1(phal chen): dang / byang chub sems dpa'i yi dam dang / spyod pa'i dkyil 'khor rgyun chad pa med pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi ye shes mngon par sgrub
4a2(phal chen): bskad cig gi cha shas la rnam par spyod pa dang / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi sgo mthong ba mi zad pa dang / tha dad pa yang dag par shes pa'i rnam pa/ gzus
4a3(phal chen): thams cad kyis snang bar byas pa dang ldan pas sangs rgyas kyi mthus byang chub sems dpa' pad+mo'i snying po la 'di skad ces smras// kye rgyal ba'i sras sangs rgyas
4a4(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams ni tshad med pa la rnam par spyod pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni rnam par 'phrul
4a5(phal chen): ba chen po la rnam par spyod pa'o// kye rgyal kha'i sras sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa thams cad la sku'i
4a6(phal chen): mtshan nyid thams cad rab tu brnyes pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba ni ting 'dzin dang dgongs pas sbyar ba'o// 
4a7(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa bzhi ni brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa shin tu ston pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom
4a8(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams ni/ sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la bsam gyis mi khyab par rnam par spyod pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas
4b1(phal chen): kyi gsung dang dbyangs ni tshad med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi dbyings thugs chud pa ni brjod du med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi/ 
4b2(phal chen): khyu mchog gi mthu byung ba ni/ thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis chos kyi dbyings thugs chud cing bstan pa ni bsgribs
4b3(phal chen): pa med pa'i mthar thug pa'o//  rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi dbyings mtha' dang dpung med pa'i sangs rgyas kyi chos rnam pa bcu ste/ 
4b4(phal chen): gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi ga zugs kyi sku rnam par dag pa ni rtog pa med par rgyud tham/ sa cad du byang bas mtha' dang dpung med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom
4b5(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi chags pa'i spyan ni/ chos thams cad ma nyam pa nyid kyi spyan mngon par sangs rgyas pas mtha' dang dpung med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi
4b6(phal chen): chags pa med pa'i snyan ni/ 'gro ba thams cad kyi sgra bsgribs pa med par thugasu chud pas mtha' dang dpung med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shangs kyi skye mched ni/ sangs rgyas kyi ma
4b7(phal chen): thams cad kyi pha rol tu phyin pa brnyes pas mtha' dang dpung med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi ljags shin tu yangs pa ni/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad du gsung gi dbyangs rjesu 'gro/ 
4b8(phal chen): ngas mtha' dang dpung med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sku'i chos nyid ni/ sems can thams cad ma lus pa'i sems kyi rnam pa de bzhin gshegs pa mthong ba rnam par dmigs/ 
5a1(phal chen): pas mtha' dang dpung med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi thugs kyi phrin las ni/ chos kyi sku dang tha mi dad cing / dus gsum chags pa med par thugs chud cing
5a2(phal chen): rnam par dag pas mtha' dang dpung med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rnam par thar pa bsgribs pa mi mnga' ba la rnam par spyod pa ni/ sangs rgyas kyi go 'phang
5a3(phal chen): dang rnam par 'phrul pa dang / cho 'phrul mi zad pa yang dag par ston pas mtha' dang dpung med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad rnam par dag pa ni/ 
5a4(phal chen): brjod du med pa'i rgyan byin gyis brlabs pas/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing nye bar nyon mongs pa med pa yang dag par bstan te/ bas ma pa ji lta ba bzhin du rnam par dmigs par mdzad pas mtha' dang / 
5a5(phal chen): dpung med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi byang chub sa/ mas dpa'i spyod pa'i khyad par dang / smon lam thams/ cad yongasu rdzogs pa ni/ rnam par rol pa'i ye shes kyi chos so
5a6(phal chen): su rdzogs te/ chos thams cad rdzogs par byang chub par bya ba la mtha' dang dpung med pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs
5a7(phal chen): rgyas rnams kyi chos kyi dbyings mtha' dang dpung med pa'i sangs rgyas kyi chos rnamaso// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi skad cig gcig la
5a8(phal chen): ye shes kyis mngon par bsgrubs pa yang dag par bstan pa'o// bcu gang zhe na/ skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du dga' ldan gyi gnas nas 'pho ba yongasasu bstan pa dang / sa
5b1(phal chen): cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du byang chub sems dpa'i tshe yongasu bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du mngon par 'byung ba yongs su bstan pa dang / 
5b2(phal chen): skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad byang chub kyi shing drung du bzhugs shing mngon par 'tshang brgya pa yongs su bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du/ 
5b3(phal chen): chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba yongasu bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du 'dul ba'i sems can yongasu smin pa'i tshul ji lta ba bzhin du dus la bab par shes
5b4(phal chen): pas/ sangs rgyas bsnyen bkur ba yongasu bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad sems can ji ltar 'dul ba'i tshul bzhin du de bzhin gshegs
5b5(phal chen): pa brjod du med pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi sku sna tshogs rnam par dmigs pa yongasu bstan pa dang / skad cig gci ga la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du rgyan sna tshogs dang / 
5b6(phal chen): rgyan brjod du med pas de bzhin gshegs pa'i khyu mchog gi mthu phyung ba dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i mdzod yongasu bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du
5b7(phal chen): rnam par dag pa gcig ma yin pa thams cad yongasasu bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du 'das pa dang // ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas skye
5b8(phal chen): ba thams cad du dbang po dang / brtson 'grus rnam pa tha dad byung ba dang / mos pa dang / spyod pa rnam pa tha dad pa byung ba la dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas kyi rgyud du mngon par 'tshang rgya ba yongasasu bsdu
6a1(phal chen): pa ste kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi skad cig la ye shes mngon par sgrub pa yang dag par bstan pa'o// kye rgyal
6a2(phal chen): ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi dus las mi 'da' ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams mngon par 'tshang rgya ba ni
6a3(phal chen): de'i dus las mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi dge ba rnam par smin pa dang / rnam par ma smin pa mnyam pa nyid ni de'i dus las mi 'da' bas dus
6a4(phal chen): la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis yongasu smin pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams lung bstan pa ni/ de'i dus las mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa
6a5(phal chen): yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis sems can gyi bsam pa'i rgyud du cho 'phrul yongasu bstan ba ni de'i dus las mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs
6a6(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis sems can mos pa ji lta bu dang ldan pa'i tshul bzhin du sku yongasu bstan pa ni dus las mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan
6a7(phal chen): 'das rnams btang snyomasu bzhugs pa ni/ de'i dus las mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams yul dang grong dang grong rdal du gshegs pa ni/ 
6a8(phal chen): de'i dus la mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams dad pa ji lta bu dang ldan pa'i tshul bzhin du sems can yong su 'dzin pa ni/ de'i dus las
6b1(phal chen): mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can kun nas nyon mongs pa dang ldan zhing gdul dka' ba la gzhan la ltos pa mi mnga' bar 'dul ba ni/ 
6b2(phal chen): de'i dus las mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa bsam gyis mi khyab pas rnam par 'phrul pa bstan pa de'i dus
6b3(phal chen): las mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi dus las mi 'da' ba'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ 
6b4(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sang+yas kyi yul dpe me dad cing bsam gyis mi khyab ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'jig/ rten gyi khams thams cad ma lus par dkyil mo dkrung gcig gis
6b5(phal chen): rgyas par dgang ba dang / dus gcig tu sangs rgyas thams cad yongasu bstan pa dang / 'od zer gcig gis 'dzi/ ga rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad snang bar bya ba dang / 
6b6(phal chen): gzugs gcig gi lus dang / gzugs thams cad yongasu bstan pa dang / gnas gcig na bzhugs kyang 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad ma lus par byon pa'i skur 'gyur ba dang / ye shes gcig
6b7(phal chen): rtogs pas chos thams cad la bsgribs pa med par 'gyur ba dang / thugs gcig bskyed pas chos kyi dbyings thams cad ma lus par rgyas par 'gengs pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi che ba nyid tshad
6b8(phal chen): med pa dang ldan pa'i gshegs stabs gcig gis de kho na nyid yang dag par bstan pa dang / dus gsum thams cad sangs rgyas kyi go 'phang gis rgyas par 'gengs pa dang / 'gro ba thams cad
7a1(phal chen): dang ma 'dres par bzhugs shing / 'das pa dang / mthon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams dang mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis rgyud kyi tshul gyi gcig pa
7a2(phal chen): ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi yul dpe med cing bsam gyis mi khyab pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ 
7a3(phal chen): bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis brlabs mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes te/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'jug pa med pa'i chos thams cad la 'jug pas/ smon lam mngon par sgrub pa
7a4(phal chen): ye shes dang / lus med pa la lus mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang / chos thams cad mi gnyis pa la mngon dpar 'tshang rgya ba mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang / sems
7a5(phal chen): can gyi mthar thug par bdag med pa la sems can 'dul ba mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang / chos thams can mtshan ma med pa la/ mtshan ma sna tshogs mngon par sgrub
7a6(phal chen): pa'i ye shes dang / 'jig rten gyi khams kyi yul ma skyes pa la 'jig rten gyi khams 'du ba dang / 'jig pa mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang / yul thams cad mngon par 'du bya
7a7(phal chen): ba med pa la las kyi rnam par smin pa mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang / chos thams cad brjod du med pa la chos kyi dbyingasu gsung mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang / chos thams
7a8(phal chen): cad kun nas nyon mongs pa dang / rnam par byang bas 'jug pa med pa la kun nas nyon mongs pa dang / rnam par byang ba mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang / chos thams cad ma skyes pa la skye
7b1(phal chen): ba dang / 'jig pa'i mtshan nyid rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mdzan/ 
7b2(phal chen): par sgrub pa'i ye shes so// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshad med pa'i khongasu chud ba dag ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan
7b3(phal chen): 'das rnams kyi sku ni dus gsum thams cad kyi rjesu 'brang ba'i khongasu chud pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can thams cad 'dul bar mdzad pa ni/ cho 'phrul chen
7b4(phal chen): gsum gyi khongasu chud pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'a ngas rnams tshig rab tu dbye ba thams cad la mkhas pa ni// sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi gzungs thams cad kyi khongasu chud pa
7b5(phal chen): yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi/ 'khor lo thams cad ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa bzhir khongasu chud ba yin
7b6(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can thams cad yongasu mi gtong ba ni/ thugs rje chen po'i khongasu chud pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams rtag tu mnyam par bzhag
7b7(phal chen): pa ni/ dus thams cad du sems can thams cad la rnam par gzigs pa'i khongasu chud pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba ni/ sems can
7b8(phal chen): rnam par gdul ba thams cad khongasu chud pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chags pa mi mnga' bar spyod pa ni chos kyi dbyings thams cad khongasu chung ba yin/ sangs
8a1(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi skad cig gcig tu ni 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas skye ba thams cad khongasu chud pa yin/ sangs rgyas
8a2(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi nyi ma gcig tu ni/ dus gsum gyi bskal pa'i grangs khongasu chud bar bstan pa thams cad khongasu chud pa yin/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas
8a3(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshad med pa'i khongasu chud pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par bka' ba rnams
8a4(phal chen): te/ bcu gang zhe na/ bdud kyi dkrugs ma rab tu 'joms zhing rnam par 'thor ba ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das na mas kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o// mu sta
8a5(phal chen): can gzhan dang / phas kyi rgol ba tshar bcad pa ni/ sa/ ngas rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i// chos bzod par dka' ba'o// 'dul ba'i sems can thams
8a6(phal chen): cad rab tu tshim par mdzad pa ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o// sems can 'dul ba'i dbang gis 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad
8a7(phal chen): du gshegs pa ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o// chos kyi dbyings thugasu chud pa'i ye shes ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
8a8(phal chen): kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o// 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad ma lus par skus khyab cing / sangs rgyas kyi sku rnam par phye ba sna tshogs thams cad du mi gnyis pa ni/ 
8b1(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o// gsung gi yan lag thams cad la sems can mos par bya ba dang / thos par bya ba dang / gdul bar bya
8b2(phal chen): ba don yod par tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa thogs pa med pas bstan pa'i tshul du tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa bzhi 'byung ba ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya
8b3(phal chen): ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi ba spu'i bu ga gcig nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed
8b4(phal chen): bsam gyis mi khyab cing thogs pa med pa'i tshul du 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyithabs kyis 'byung zhing / de bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi sku'i ba
8b5(phal chen): spu'i bu ga thams cad nas 'byung ba ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka'aba'o// de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par
8b6(phal chen): rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rdul shin tu phra ba gcig la sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed yongasu ston cing / sangs rgyas kyi rgyan dang / rang bzhin gyi lha
8b7(phal chen): lhub dang / chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba rgyun mi 'chad cing / sems can rnam par 'dul ba thogs pa med la 'jig rten gyi khams de dag tu gtogs pa rnams la'ang mi bde ba dang / gnod pa/ 
8b8(phal chen): med kyang rdul shin tu phra ba de yang yangs par ma byas/ 'jig rten gyi khams de dag kyang chung bar ma byas par ji ltar gnas pa'i chos kyi dbyings kyang thugs chud pa'i ye shes mnga' ba ni/ 
9a1(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgyargyu che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o// mun pa med pa'i khams de bzhin gshegs pas mngon par sangs rgyas te/ 
9a2(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la mun pa med cing bsgribs pa mi mnga' la/ sems can pha rol gyi bsgribs pa sna tshogs kyi gnas par sel na/ de la bcom ldan 'das de bzhin ga
9a3(phal chen): pa'i stobs bcu dang ldan pa ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos la bzod par dka' ba ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas
9a4(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod padaka' ba'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che
9a5(phal chen): pa rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing / na tu dag pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas pa com ldan 'das rnams kyi yang dag par bsgrubs pa
9a6(phal chen): bdag nyid che ba ni/ sngon gyi mtha' nas rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing rnam par dag pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang
9a7(phal chen): da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas kyi rgyud du rigs dang ldan par 'byung ba'i bdag nyid che ba ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs rnam par dag pas/ rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu
9a8(phal chen): rnam par dag pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni rnam par shes pa la mi gnas pa ste/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni/ phyi ma'i mtha'i mur
9b1(phal chen): thugs par gnas pas/ rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni ngas gsum la mi gnas par rnam par spyod cing chos
9b2(phal chen): thams cad la rten pa yang dag par bcom pas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni/ rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o// sangs
9b3(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dngos po rnam pa tha dad pa la rnam par bzhag pa gcig gis len pa med pas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni/ rnam pa thams cad
9b4(phal chen): du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sngon gyi mtha' dang / phyi ma'i mthar chos kyi dbyings la gnas pas mnyam pa'i
9b5(phal chen): bsod nams mi zad pa dang ldan pas/ mi zad pa'i bsod/ nams mnga' ba ste/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das/ rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni/ rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma
9b6(phal chen): tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sku gzugs dang / kha dog mtha' yas pas/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad na/ sems can 'dul
9b7(phal chen): ba'i dus dang dbang gis chags pa med par bzhugs pas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni/ rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o// 
9b8(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mi 'jigs pa bzhi brnyes pas bag tsha ba mi mnga' bar bzhugs shing khyu mchog dang seng ge'i nga ro 'byin te/ rgol ba'i nang na stag lta bu'i mthu dang
10a1(phal chen): ldan la/ chos thams cad bstan pa la thugs sgron ma lta bu mnga' bas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni/ rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma thob
10a2(phal chen): med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni yongasu mya ngan las 'das nas bskal pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa zhig yon yang mtshan gyi tshig thos
10a3(phal chen): btsam gyis bzhugs pa dang 'dra bar sems can rnams kyi yon shin tu sbyong zhing / mya ngan las 'das nas de srid kyi yun ring po 'das kyang / sangs rgyas la bskyed pa'i yon zad par mi
10a4(phal chen): 'gyur bas/ sangs rgyas kyi bdag nyid che ba ni/ rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag dpa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams 'jig rten
10a5(phal chen): gyi khams brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa dag na ba zhugs shing / 'jig rten gyi khams rgyang ring po na ba/ zhugs kyang / 'jig rten gyi khams 'di na gnas pa'i
10a6(phal chen): sems can rnams kyis rjes su dran par byas na/ sku mngon par ston pa mdzad pas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni/ rnam pa thams cad kha na ma tho ba med
10a7(phal chen): cing shin tu rnam par dag pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni/ rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par
10a8(phal chen): dag pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rnam par dag pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs
10b1(phal chen): rgyas kyi tshangs pa'i spyod pa rnam par dag pa la/ sngon gyi smon lam gyis shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chags pa med pa'i tshul khrims kyis shin tu
10b2(phal chen): rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/ sems can thams cad kyi nyon mongs pa sel bas/ shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
10b3(phal chen): rnams ni/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing gis shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'khor gyis shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
10b4(phal chen): ni rigs rna bar dag pas/ shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni gzugs kyi sku'i mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po rnam par dag pas/ shin tu rnam
10b5(phal chen): par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnam sa ni/ chos kyi sku rnyog pa med pas/ shin tu ni/ ma par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnas
10b6(phal chen): ni thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi phung po bsgribs pa med pas shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/ sangs rgyas kyi rnam par thar pa thams cad la
10b7(phal chen): mthu chen po brnyes shing / pha rol tu phyin pa dam pa brnyes pas shin tu rnam par dag pa yin te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rnam
10b8(phal chen): par dag pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mdzad pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du 'byung zhing dus thams cad du gnas pa
11a1(phal chen): ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas rje su dran pa'i thob pa'i sems can rnams la dus thams cad du/ sangs rgyas bstan pa dang / sems can sems cad shes dang
11a2(phal chen): ldan pa rnams la/ dus thams cad du chos bstan pa dang / sems can sangs rgyas la dad pa'i sems dang ldan pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba dus thams cad du bskyed pa dang / chos kyi skyon med
11a3(phal chen): par 'das pa'i sems can rnams dus thams cad du ye shes khong du chud par bya ba dang / 'gro ba thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa dus thams cad du rgyun mi 'chad pa dang / de bzhin
11a4(phal chen): gshegs pa rnams 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du dus thams cad du chags pa mi mnga' bar gshegs pa dang / sems can thams cad la thugs rje chen po dus
11a5(phal chen): thams cad du mi gtong ba dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi sprul pa dus thams cad du thogs pa med pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
11a6(phal chen): kyi sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa sna tshogs dus thams cad du thogs pa med pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams chos kyi dbyings gnas pa'i sangs rgyas dus thams cad du
11a7(phal chen): 'byung ba ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mdzad pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du 'byung zhing / dus thams cad du gnas
11a8(phal chen): pa'o/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'i tshul rnams ste/ bcwa
11b1(phal chen): ga she na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i sras ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/ sangs rgyas kyi phrin las chang
11b2(phal chen): med pa brnyes pas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zang pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi spyan gyi yul mnga' bas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom
11b3(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams ni dge ba'i rtsa ba tshad med pa/ bsam gyis mi khyab pa mnga' bas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/ chos kyi char mngon par
11b4(phal chen): 'bebs pas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o// sangs rgya ngas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi yon tan dang / legs pa mang po mnga' bas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad
11b5(phal chen): pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sngon gyi// mtha'i thams cad mkhyen pa'i smon lam dang khyad par/ mnga' bas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o// sangs rgyas
11b6(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams ni phyi ma'i mtha'i mur 'gro ba thams cad sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun mi 'chad par sgrub pas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
11b7(phal chen): ni sems can gyi rigs thams cad ma lus pa'i sems dang spyod pa la ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni thams cad mkhyen pa'i bsod nams zil/ 
11b8(phal chen): gyis mi non pas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi ye shes rgya mtsho mi
12a1(phal chen): zad pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi tshul rnams te/ bcu gang she na/ 'di lta ste/ pha rol tu phyin pa
12a2(phal chen): thams cad kyis mngon par byung ba 'di ni sangs bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no// 'di lta ste/ chos thams cad la mi mkhyen pa gang yang mi mnga' ba 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom
12a3(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no// 'di lta ste/ thams cad kyang thugs rje chen po dang ldan pa 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no// 'di lta ste/ thams cad
12a4(phal chen): kyang stobs bcu tshad med pa dang ldan pa 'di ni/ sangs rgyasabacom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no// 'di lta ste/ thams cad kyang bla na med pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu bskor
12a5(phal chen): ba 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul/ yin no// 'di lta ste/ thams cad kyang sems can 'dul ba yang dag par zhugs pa 'di ni/ sangs rgyas pa
12a6(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no// 'di lta ste/ thams cad kyang 'gro ba thams cad kyi don du mngon par sangs rgyas pa 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no// 'di
12a7(phal chen): lta ste/ 'dul ba'i sems can rnams 'dul ba la thogs pa mi mnga' ba 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no// 'di lta ste/ mi gnyis par yang dag par
12a8(phal chen): spyod pa'i mtshan nyid kyi chos la rab tu gzhol ba 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no// 'di lta ste ji ltar yongasu smin par gyur pa dang / dul bar gyur pa'i sems
12b1(phal chen): can rnams la/ sangs rgyas kyi yul mu med pas/ sangs rgyas kyi yongasu mya ngan las 'da' ba ston pa 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan rnams kyi tshul yin te/ kye rtul ba'i sras bcu po de dag
12b2(phal chen): ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi tshulo// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi chos mtha' yas pa shin
12b3(phal chen): tubastan pa'i sgo rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can gyi khams shin tu bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni
12b4(phal chen): sems can gyi spyod pa sna tshogs shin tu bstan pa'i sgor ma tha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can thams cad kyi las dang / rnam par smin pa shin tu
12b5(phal chen): bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'a/ ngas rnams ni sems can thams cad la gdams ngag dang / man ngag shin tu bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas
12b6(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can mtha' yas pa rnam par sbyong ba'i nan tan gyi sgor mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad la gdams
12b7(phal chen): ngag dang / man ngag gis yongasu gzhog pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni byang chub sems dpa'i khyad par gyi smon lam rnam pa tha dad pas 'byung ba shin tu bstan
12b8(phal chen): pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad ma lus pa'i 'du ba dang / 'jig pa shin tu bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom
13a1(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnam par dag pa ni byang chub sems dpa'i bsam pa dang / mos pa ji lta bzhin du yongasu bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan
13a2(phal chen): 'das rnams kyi 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa ni bskal pa yangs pa de dang de dag tu bstan cing
13a3(phal chen): brjod pa dang / yongasu bshad pas/ sangs rgyas kyi ye shes thams cad khong du chud par bya ba'i sgor mtha' yas pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis
13a4(phal chen): rgyas kyi chos mtha' yas pa shin tu bstan pa'i sgo'o// kye rgyal ba 'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las sems can rnams la sgrub
13a5(phal chen): pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sku yongs su bstan pa ni/ sems can rnams la sang / sa rgyas kyi phrin las sgrub bo// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
13a6(phal chen): rnams kyi gsung yang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las sgrub bo// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams len pa mdzad pa yang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las sgrub bo// sangs
13a7(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams len pa mi mdzad pa yang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las sgrub po// sa dang / chu dang / me dang / rlung gis kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sem/ 
13a8(phal chen): can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las sgrub po// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni byin gyi rlabs kyi yul dang mangs dmigs pa thams cad yul du mdzad pas kyang / sems can rnams la
13b1(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi phrin las sgrub po// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mtshan kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las sgrub bo// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/ zhing la ri/ 
13b2(phal chen): par mdzad pas kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las sgrub po// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnam par dag pas kyang / sems can rnams la sangs rgyas
13b3(phal chen): kyi phrin las sgrub bo// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams mi gsung bar bzhugs pa yang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las sgrub ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas
13b4(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las sems can rnam dasal sgrub pa'o// / bam po drug cu rtsa bzhi pa// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas ba
13b5(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos te/ cu gang zhe na/ smon lam chen po la rab tu brtan zhing chu/ na lam zhig pa mi mnga' bas ji skad du gsung ba de ltar
13b6(phal chen): mdzad cing gnyis su mi gsung ba 'di ni/ sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos dang po'o// phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa'i skal ba thams cad du/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la yon tan thams
13b7(phal chen): cad yongs su rdzogs par mdzad par rab tu brtson zhing sgyid lug pa mi mnga' ba 'di ni/ sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos gnyis pa'o// sems can 'dul bar 'gyur ba gcig cig gzigs kyang
13b8(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med par gshegs shing 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du gshegs pa la thags thogs med pa 'di ni/ sems can gyi gtso bo'i
14a1(phal chen): chos gsum pa'o// zhe sdang ba'i sems can rnams la thugs rje chen pos snyoms pa dang / dang pa'i sems can rnams la thugs rje chen pos snyoms pa 'di ni/ sems can
14a2(phal chen): gyi gtso bo'i chos bzhi pa'o// gang gi tshe bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu yang dag par zhugs nas bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par sangs rgyas
14a3(phal chen): kyi bar du de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas su 'gyur ro snyam du/ byang chub kyi sems ma nyams pa 'di ni/ sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos lnga
14a4(phal chen): pa'o/ dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad yang dag par sgrub cing thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du yongasu sngo bas 'jug gi/ 'jig rten pa'i rgyud la ma yin pa 'di ni/ sems
14a5(phal chen): can gyi gtso bo'i chos drug pa'o// sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rjes su sngon/ sangs rgyas kyis spyad pa'i sems/ su lus kyi las dang / ngag gi las dang / yid kyi las
14a6(phal chen): kyis slob cing nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi spyod pas thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du yong su sngo ba med pas/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par sangs rgyas pa 'di/ 
14a7(phal chen): ni/ sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos bdun pa'o// byang chub sems dpa'i sems rnam par dag cing / 'od gsal la dngas pa/ thams cad du snang zhing kun tu 'od 'byung ba/ sangs
14a8(phal chen): rgyas kyi chos thams cad la sdang zhing thams cad du snyoms pas thams cad mkhyen pa nyid yongasu rdzogs par byed pa 'di ni/ sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos brgyad pa'o// 'jig rten pa'i bde
14b1(phal chen): pa thams cad yongasu spangs te/ 'jig rten pa'i dga' ba thams cad la ma chags pa dang / 'jig rten thams cad kyis gos pa med pa'i sman la thams cad du mnyam pa nyid kyis 'jig rten thams
14b2(phal chen): cad bde ba thams cad dang ldan par byas te/ sdug bsngal dang / spros pa thams cad rab tu 'jom pa 'di ni/ sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos dgu pa'o// sdug bsngal gyi mi bde ba thams cad
14b3(phal chen): nyamasu bab ste/ 'gro ba thams cad kyi don du dka' thub kyis shin tu gdungs kyang bla bar sems bskyed pas/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rigs yongasu bsrung ba dang ldan pa dang / stobs bcu
14b4(phal chen): sa'i bar du/ sangs rgyas kyi yul la mos pas mthar thug pa 'di ni/ sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos bcu pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom
14b5(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos so// / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas/ bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rnam par spyod
14b6(phal chen): pa chags pa med pa rnams ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du gshegs pas chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod
14b7(phal chen): pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/ 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad na bzhugs pas chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom
14b8(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad na bzhugs pa dang / bzhengs pa dang / bzhud pas chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
15a1(phal chen): ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du chos ston pas chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams
15a2(phal chen): ma lus pa thams cad kyi dga' ldan gyi gnas na bzhugs kyang / chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi sngon
15a3(phal chen): gyi mtha' dang / phyi ma'i mtha' dang / da ltar byung ba'i mtha' la chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad tsam gyi
15a4(phal chen): 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor na bzhugs kyang chags pa mi mnga' nga bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can ma lus pa thams cad kyi sems dang spro
15a5(phal chen): pa la gzigs shing thugs kyi skad cig gcig la/ cho 'phrul/ chen po gsum gyis/ sems can rnam par 'dul ya/ nga chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas
15a6(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sku gcig gis kyang tshad med bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i sangs rgyas kyi rnam par spyod pa chen por rnam par spyod kyang chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin// sangs rgyas
15a7(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can gyi khams 'byam klas pa ma lus pa thams cad du/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos ma lus pa thams cad kyi mthar thug pa bsam gyis mi khyab par ston cing
15a8(phal chen): gsung yang / chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rnam par spyod pa chags pa med pa'o// 
15b1(phal chen): rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis ng+yas kyi rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sku/ mtshan dang
15b2(phal chen): dpe byad bzang po sna tshogs kyis rnam par brgyan pa ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sku'i rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gsung yan lag gi/ 
15b3(phal chen): mchog dam pa drug cu dang ldan zhing yan lag lnga brgyas yongasu bzung ba dang / rgyan brgya stong du mas rab tu brgyan pa dang / dbyangs kyi yan lag mtha' yas mu med pas rnam par dag pa dang / sangs rgyas
15b4(phal chen): kyi chos kyi don dang / tshig dang / yi ge brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pas rab tu tshim par mdzad pa dang / bag tsha ba mi mnga' bas seng ge'i nga ro chen po sgrogs pa dang / 'jigs pa
15b5(phal chen): med pa chen pos bsnyengs pa mi mnga' bar gyur pa dang / chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad du sems can thams cadal grags cing bstsal te khong du chud par 'gyur ba dang / sems
15b6(phal chen): can bsam pa tha dad pa dang / dbang po tha dad pa rnam pa sna tshogs 'dul bar nye bar gnas pa 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gsung gi rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// sangs rgyas
15b7(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi thugs kyi phrin las ni stobs bcus brgyan pa/ sangs rgyas kyi ting nge 'dzin chen po thams cad kyi me tog shin tu rgyas pa/ sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad
15b8(phal chen): kyi rgyan gyis shin tu brgyan cing bsrubs pas chags pa med pa'i spyod yul dang ldan pa/ chos kyi dbyings kyi gzhi la rab tu rten pa/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi chos gting med pa rab tu brnyes
16a1(phal chen): ba chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi rgyan tu gyur pa/ dus gsum gyi chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi sems can kun gyi sems dang spyod pa thams cad skad cigag ci
16a2(phal chen): dang ldan pa'i shes rab kyi rab tu mkhyen pa ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi thugs kyi rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'od zer bye ba
16a3(phal chen): brjod du med pa rab tu 'gyed pa mdzad de/ 'od zer de dag re re la yang 'od zer gyi 'khor gyi dra ba brjod du med pa dang ldan pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'byam klas pa thams cad ma lus par snang bar
16a4(phal chen): byed cing / 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyud thams cad mun pa med dpar ston pa sangs rgyas skye ba dang mi 'bral bas/ sangs rgyas kyi phrin las phyir mi ldog cing don yod pa/ sangs
16a5(phal chen): rgyas skye ba brjod du med pas gnas pa med pa rang bzhin rnam par dag cing kun tu snyoms par 'byung ba ste/ 'di ni sa/ ngas rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi 'od zer gyi rgyan mchog
16a6(phal chen): dam pa bla na med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams bzhad mo 'dzum par ston na/ zhal gyi sgo nas 'od zer kha dog sna tshogs kha dog du ma dang ldan pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong brjod
16a7(phal chen): du med pa phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad snang bar byed pa/ sems can gyi khams tshad med grangs med bsam gyis mi khyab pa rnam par ston pa/ bla na med pa yang
16a8(phal chen): dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu rnam pa gzhan du mi 'gyur bar lung ston pa/ 'gro ba thams cad du shin tu gsal ba 'byung ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bzhad mo 'dzum
16b1(phal chen): pa bstan pa'i rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi sku ni tshad med pa ste/ bsgribs pa med pas rnam par dag pa chos thams cad chags pa med pa
16b2(phal chen): nyid kyi mthar thug pa/ mtha' dang dpung med pa'i chos kyi dbyings la gnas pa/ 'jig rten thams cad dang ma 'dres pa/ 'jig rten thams cad dang 'ji ba med pa/ 'jig rten thams cad kyi
16b3(phal chen): de kho na nyid la yang dag par zhugs pa/ 'jig rten thams cad las gyen du 'phags pa/ 'jig rten las 'das pa'i chos kyis yang dag par spyod pa/ tshig gi lam dang bral ba/ brjod du
16b4(phal chen): med pa'i mthar phyin pa/ phung po dang / khams dang / skye mched dadang bral ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi sku'i rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med
16b5(phal chen): pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'od tshad med pa mnga' ba ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa tha mas cad du 'od ma 'dres shing rgyan du ma dang ldan pa kha dog sna
16b6(phal chen): tshogs brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rgyan dang ldan pa/ 'od kyi snang ba kun tu thogs pa med cing thams cad du chags pa med pa 'od kyi dkyil 'khor bsgribs pa med pa tshad med pa'i mdzod du gya
16b7(phal chen): papa'od thams cad kyi 'byung gnas su gyur pa ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi 'od kyi rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// sangs bcom ldan 'das rnams ni kha dog mtha'
16b8(phal chen): yas pa mnga' ba ste/ kha dog yid du 'ong ba mnga' ba'o// kha dog 'od gsal ba mnga' ba'o// kha dog tshad med pa mnga' ba'o// sems can gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad kyi bsam pa dang mos pa
17a1(phal chen): bzhin du rnam par dmigs pa'i kha dog mnga' ba'o// de ma yin pa'i kha dog gzhan khams gsum du gtogs pa thams cad zil gyis gnon pa'i kha dog mnga' ba'o// kha dog
17a2(phal chen): thams cad kyi pha rol tu phyin pa brnyes pas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni kha dog bla na med pa mnga' ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi kha dog rgyan mchog dam pa
17a3(phal chen): bla na med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dge bas shin tu rnam par dag pa ste/ 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rigs dge ba rin po che'i
17a4(phal chen): 'byung gnasu gyur pa la shin tu byung ba'o// chos nyid kyi rnam dpa thams cad du khyad par yod pa dang / khyad par med pa de'i spyod pas rnam par dag pa'i rgyan gyi ye shes skye ba thams
17a5(phal chen): cad nang du gtogs pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i rig sa bsgribs pa med pa'i rgyud rnam par dag pas 'jig rten gyi mi snyan pa thams cad kyis mi snyan pa brjod du med pa
17a6(phal chen): ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rigs dang rgyud rnam par dag pa'i rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni byams pa chen po
17a7(phal chen): mthu dang / rang bzhin gyi rgyan mnga' ba ste/ shin tu dang ba yongasu rtog pa'i rnyog pa mi mnga' ba sku'i phrin las yongasu gsal ba/ blta bas mi skyo ba thugs shin tu rnam par bsal ba/ thugs rje
17a8(phal chen): chen po mnga' ba 'gro ba thams cad skyob pa yon gyi gnas kyi dam pa bla na med pa yongasu 'dzin pa'i nang na thugs brtse ba can phan par mdzad pa/ sems can thams cad kyi don du ye shes chen po
17b1(phal chen): byin gyis brlabs te/ bsod nams chen pos yongasu 'phags pa 'gro ba thams cad kyi bsod nams kyi zhing du gyur pa/ sems can rnams kyi yon tan dang / ye shes kyi phung po thams cad rnam par
17b2(phal chen): bar mdzad pa ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi byams pa chen po dang / thugs rje chen po'i mthar thug pa'i bsod nams kyi rgyan mchog das pa bla na med pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ 
17b3(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen po
17b4(phal chen): mnga' sgyur ba'i chos rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas pa bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos thams cad la mnga' ba dang // chos thams cad la snang bar mdzad pa'i mnga' sgyur bas/ tshig
17b5(phal chen): dang yi ge mtha' yas pa la thogs pa mi mnga' ba'i spon sa pa mnga' ba dang / chos thams cad ma lus par yod su brjod pas mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan
17b6(phal chen): 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sgyur ba'i chos dang po'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can ji ltar yongasu smin pa dang / smon lam ji ltar btab pa'i tshul
17b7(phal chen): bzhin du 'dul ba la thogs pa mi mnga' bas mnga' che ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sgyur ba'i chos gnyis pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams
17b8(phal chen): ma lus pa thams cad sems can gcig la'ang gnod pa med par rnam pa drug tu rab tu bskyod pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams rgyan rnam par bkod pa grangs med tshad med pa dang ldan pa/ nam mkha'i
18a1(phal chen): dbyings kyi mthas gtugs pa thams cad gcig nas gcig tu 'phang ba dang / gcig nas cig tu gzhug pa dang / gcig nas gcig tu bsdu ba dang / gcig nas gcig tu bsre ba 'jig
18a2(phal chen): rten gyi khams gzhan dang / gzhan dag gzhan dang gzhan gyi phyogs su rab tu bzhag kyang / sems can gyi khams rnams 'khor cing rmongs par mi 'gyur la the tsom du mi 'gyur bar mdzad pas/ 
18a3(phal chen): mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sgyur ba'i chos gsum pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad byin gyis
18a4(phal chen): rlob pa'i ye shes kyis 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyan phan tshun du byin gyis brlab pa dang / thugs skad cig gis la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rgyan yang dag par bstan pa/ 
18a5(phal chen): dang / bskal pa grangs med par brjod kyang yi ge shin tu bstan pa zad mi shes pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad rgyan thams cad kyis rnam par brgyan pa
18a6(phal chen): dang / mi mthun pa med cing nye bar nyon mongs pa med pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing gcig tu yongasu 'du bar sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnam par dag pa thams cad byin gyis brlab pa la mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni// 
18a7(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sbyar ba'i chos bzhi pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi 'dul ba'i sems can gzigs na sems
18a8(phal chen): can gcig gi don du bskal ba brjod du med pa'i yang brjod med par skyil mo krung gcig gis bzhugs na yang de bzhin gshegs pa'i skul mi bde ba mi mnga' zhing thugs la mi bde ba mi mnga' ste/ gang zag de yang
18b1(phal chen): mi bsrel bas 'dul ba'i dus las mi 'da' ba dang / gang zag gcig la ji lta ba bzhin du rim pa rim pas 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa'i sku tshe la mnga' ba/ 
18b2(phal chen): byin gyis brlabs ste/ bzhugs kyang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams la skyo ba mi mnga' ba ste/ de ltar sems can gyi khams thams cad mthar gyis rim pas/ sangs rgyas kyis 'dul ba'i gang
18b3(phal chen): zag gi don du yongasu skyong ba mdzad pa la mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sbyar ba'i chos lnga pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/ 'jig rten gyi
18b4(phal chen): khams ma lus pa thams cad du yang dag par gzhol ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i bzhud pas 'jig rten gyi khams tham/ sa cad du bzhud pa la thags thogs mi mnga' ba dang / phyogs bcu'i
18b5(phal chen): chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi 'jig rten gyi kham/ sa kyi rgyud rgya mtsho 'byam klas pa dang / phyogs kyi dra ba'i rgyu de thams cad du thugs skad cig gcig dang ldan pas bzhud
18b6(phal chen): par byin gyis rlob cing chos kyi dbyings shin tu bstan pa khong du chud par bya bas/ chos kyi 'khor lo thogs pa med pa rab tu bskor ba la mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
18b7(phal chen): kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sbyar ba'i chos drug pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'dul ba'i sems can gyi khams thams cad kyi don du thugs skad cig re re la bla na med pa yang dag par
18b8(phal chen): rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya bar mnga' che ba ste/ de la chos thams cad mngon par sangs rgyas pa'ang gang yang med la mngon par sangs rgyas pa'ang med de/ mngon par 'tshang rgya bar
19a1(phal chen): 'gyur ba med kyang / slob pa'i sa la gnas shing mngon par 'tshang rgya bar yang mi brjod pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad kyang bsgribs pa med par rtogs par thug su chud pas
19a2(phal chen): sems can thams cad 'dul ba'i don du ye shes tshad med pa'i tshul gyis/ sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa chen po'i yul yongasu rgyun mi gcod pa 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
19a3(phal chen): kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sbyar ba'i chos bdun pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi spyan gyi skye mched kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las gang sgrub pa de snyan gyi skye mched kyis yongasu grub pa
19a4(phal chen): mdzad do// snyan gyi skye mched kyis sangs rgyas kyi phrin las gang bsgrub pa de shangs kyi skye mched kyis yongasu grub par mdzad do// shangs kyi skye mched kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las gang
19a5(phal chen): sgrub pa de ljags kyi skye mched kyis yongasu grub par mdzad do// ljags kyi skye mched kyis/ sangs rgyas kyi phrin las gang sgrub pa de ni sku'i skye mched kyis yongasu grub par mdzad do// 
19a6(phal chen): sku'i skye mched kyis sangs rgyas kyi phrin las gang sgrub pa de thugs kyi skye mched kyis yongasu grub par mdzad do// thugs kyi skye mched kyis sangs rgyas kyi phrin las gang sgrub pa de 'jig rten gyi khams
19a7(phal chen): ma lus pa thams cad kyi dmigs pa 'jig rten pa dang / 'jig rten las 'das pa sna tshogs rnam par phye ba thams cad du grub par mdzad do// de bzhin du dmigs pa thams cad re re yang snrel zhing
19a8(phal chen): sgrub pas sangs rgyas kyi phrin las sgrub pa la mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sbyar ba'i chos brkyang ba'o// sangs rgyas
19b1(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams ni rang gi sku'i baspu'i bu gcig gi nang du sems can gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad gzung bar mdzad cing khongasu chud par mdzad pa dang / sems can re re shing yang lus sangs
19b2(phal chen): rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa tsam du yangs par mdzad kyang / sems can de dag la gnod pa dang / mi bde bar mi 'gyur ba dang / de dag du yang sems can re re zhing 'jig rten gyi khams gcig nas ga
19b3(phal chen): tu brgyad pas bskal pa grangs med pazang par gnas par bya ba dang / 'jig rten gyi khams grangs med par gom pa gcig gis phyin pas 'jig rten gyi khams de dag du sangs rgyas byung ba rnams
19b4(phal chen): kyi spyan sngar 'gro bar bya ba dang / sangs rgyas de dag byung ba'i tshe yang brjod du med pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyud dang gling de dag na sems can gyi gtso bos brjod du med pa'i yang
19b5(phal chen): brjod du med pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bar bya ba dang / ba spu'i bu ga de nas sangs rgyas gcig nas gcig tu ba rgyud pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa 'byung bar bya
19b6(phal chen): ba dang / sems can gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa 'byung bar bya ba dang / chos kyi 'khor lo gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med
19b7(phal chen): pa bskor bar bya ba dang / chos kyi dbyings gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa shin tu bstan par bya ba dang 'das pa gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa brjod/ 
19b8(phal chen): du med pa dang / ma 'ongs pa gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa brjod du med pa dang / da ltar byung ba gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa brjod du med pa yongs su brjod par bya ba dang / nam mkha'i
20a1(phal chen): dgyes mtha' nga dadrung med par bstan bkun marnams med par sems can thams cad 'o shrI gro dang / skye ba'i skyem ched thams cad du dod pa'i sangs stoH
20a2(phal chen): chen po bgegs med pa thams cad 'byung bar bya ba la mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sgyur ba'i chos dgu pa'o// sas
20a3(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad du d+mo'i rgyan chen pos brgyan pa'i seng ge'i khri pad+mo'i snying po can la de bzhin gshegs pa gcig gi chos kyi dbyis
20a4(phal chen): tshad med pa thams cad du khyab pa'i skus byang chub tu ma rngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas te/ sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa thams cad yongasu bstan pa mdzad pa
20a5(phal chen): dang / de bzhin gshegs pa gcig gi ji lta bar 'jigarten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi sems can gyi gtso bo thams cad kyang de bzhin du dgongs pa
20a6(phal chen): skad cig ma re re'i byin gyis brlabs kyis brlabs pa dang / dgongs pa skad cig la ji lta ba bzhin du dgongs pa skad cig thams cad la'ang pad+mo'i rgyud kyis yongasu dag par mngon par 'tshang rgya
20a7(phal chen): pabar bya ba dang / de bzhin du chos kyi dbyings thams cad ma lus pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa rnam par dag pa rgyan sna tshogs dang ldan pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams dmigs
20a8(phal chen): pa rnam pa sna tshogs dang ldan pa'i zhing rnam par dag pa 'byam klas pa brjod du med pa mtshan nyid tha dad pa'i rgyud tshad med cing 'byam klas pa dus kyi rgyad grangs med pa dang ldan pa/ bstan
20b1(phal chen): pam 'dres pa dang ldan pa/ blo chang med pa dang / nos pa shin tu yangs pa dang ldan pa// mtshan nyid sna tshogs kyi gnas med pa/ mtshan nyid bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang ldan pa/ 
20b2(phal chen): tshad med pa thams cad dgongs pa skad cig ma las dgongs pa skad cig ma gcig gis thams cad yongasu bstan kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'ongs rnams ched du/ 
20b3(phal chen): sgrub pa mi mdzad pa la mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sbyar ba'i chos bcu pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras ba
20b4(phal chen): bide dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sgyur dba'i chos so// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni// 
20b5(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi chos yongasu rdzogs pa tshad med pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na mtshan re re shing bas
20b6(phal chen): nams brgya pa'i mtshan yongs su dag par 'gyur ba 'di ni yongasu rdzogs pa dang po ste/ des sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o// sangs
20b7(phal chen): rgyas kyi chos rnams yongasu rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o// dge ba'i rtsab thams cad yongs su rdzogs pas sargyas
20b8(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o// yon tan thams cad kyi 'byung gnas phun sum tshogs pa'i spyod pa yongasu dag pa rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom
21a1(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o// sems can yongs su smin par bya ba dang / 'dul ba yongs su rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan
21a2(phal chen): 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshong rgya'o// sangs rgyas kyi mnga' 'gro ba thams cad kyis zil gyis mnon pa yongs su rdzogs pas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'dra/ 
21a3(phal chen): rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o// zhing yongs su dag par bya ba yongs su rdzogs pas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o// 
21a4(phal chen): thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes yongasu rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o// mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po dang / 
21a5(phal chen): gzugs kyi sku blta na don yod par yongs su rdzogs pa/ sa/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o// de bzhin gshegs pa
21a6(phal chen): thams cad dang mnyam pa nyid yongs su rdzogs pas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya ste sangs rgyas kyi drin las thams cad yongs su
21a7(phal chen): par mdzad nas/ yongs su mya ngan las 'da'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi chos yongs su rdzogs pa tshad med/ 
21a8(phal chen): bsam gyis mi khyab pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi thabs mkhas pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
21b1(phal chen): rnams ni chos thams cad byin gyis brlabs pa med cing stos pa thams cad med par yang / thugs su chud la dge ba'i sgra nas sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyang shin tu
21b2(phal chen): cing brjod de/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa dang po'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos thams cad la gru
21b3(phal chen): pa med cing phan tshun du mkhyen pa med do// ma bcings ma grol ba dang / gzung ba med cing bsags pa med de yongs su rdzogs pa med per yang thugs su chud la sangs rgyas kyi cho
21b4(phal chen): thams cad la mnga' dam pa yang brnyes te/ sangs da rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams chos thams cadu la mnga' sbyar ba de yang yang dag pa de kho na nyid mnor
21b5(phal chen): rnam pa gzhan du mi 'gyur ba dang / chos thams cad/ khrodag gi med cing yongs su 'dzin pa med la de kho na nyid kyi mtha' las rnam par mi 'dra' yang sangs
21b6(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mnga' chen pos chos kyi dbyings thams cad snang ba la'ang rab tu mkhyen pa 'ang na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas
21b7(phal chen): kyi thabs mkhas pa gnyis pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mtshan ma'i mtha' thams cad mi mnga' ste/ mtshan ma thams cad dang mi 'grogs shing / mtshan
21b8(phal chen): ma'i mngon par shes pa thams cad dang / ma 'dres la de'i rang bzhin du ngo bo nyid med pa dang / ji ltar ngo bo nyid med pa'i sgra'i tshul thams cad thugs su chud kyang gzugs kyi mtshan
22a1(phal chen): ma'i sku gzugs rnam par dag pa grangs med pa dang / zhing gi mtshan ma dang / rnam par spyod pa'i mtshan ma zad mi shes pa rnam pa sna tshogs yang dag par bstan
22a2(phal chen): cing bshad pa'i ye shes kyi phung po mun pa med pa 'gro ba thams cad kyi sgron ma chen por gyur pas mun pa med pa'i snang ba ston pa 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnam
22a3(phal chen): kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa gsum pa'o// chags pa med pa'i mtha' ni sngon gyi mtha' yang ma yin/ phyi ma'i mtha' yang ma yin/ da ltar byung ba yang ma yin te/ chos
22a4(phal chen): kyi dbyings su gnas pa ni 'das pa dang / ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba yang ma yin pas/ de bzhin nyid kyi mtshan nyid kyis 'byung ba med kyang sangs rgyas 'byung/ 
22a5(phal chen): ba rnams kyi rigs tshad med pa'i phyir shin tu bstan pa brjo/  du med pas 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar/ byung ba'i sangs rgyas bskye ba yang rab tu brjod cing kun tu/ 
22a6(phal chen): gzigs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi yul gyis de bzhin du gzigs pa 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa bzhi pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan
22a7(phal chen): 'das rnams kyi sku'i phrin las dang / gsung gi phrin las dang / thugs kyi phrin las kyi mngon par 'du mdzad pa yang mi mnga' la yongs su blang ba mi mnga' bas bzhugs shing rnam pa/ 
22a8(phal chen): phye ba med pa'i mthar thugs pa ste/ dor ba med pa'i chos kyi gnas kyi pha rol tu phyin la bgrang ba'i tshul las rnam par 'das kyang tshul grangs med pa'i mdzod du gyur cing / bgrang ba dang / 
22b1(phal chen): mngon par sgrub pa mtha' yas pa dang / 'jig rten pa dang 'jig rten las 'das pa rnam pa sna tshogs tha dad pa'i grangs kyi tshul thugs su chud pa ye shes bsgribs pa med pas gzigs/ 
22b2(phal chen): pa rnam te/ chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi sems can gdul ba rnam par dmigs pa la rdzu 'phrul sna tshogs tshad med mu med par mngon par sgrub pa mdzad pa 'di ni sangs rgyas
22b3(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa lnga pa'o// chos thams cad lta ba med pas tha mi dad pa dang / bye brag med pa dang / 'byung ba med pa dang / mtshan nyid med
22b4(phal chen): pa dang / sna tshogs med pa dang / blang ba med pa dang / dor da pa med pa dang / rang bzhin med par rab tu mkhyend kyang chos kyi rgyud shin tu nges pa yang dag par sgrub cing
22b5(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi tshul dang 'gal ba med pa dang / rang bzhin me/ da pa yang yang dag par gzigs pas thams ca nga mkhyen pa thams cad gzigs pa mkhyen par bya ba tham
22b6(phal chen): cad ma lus par gzigs pas chos la mnga' sbyar ba thams cad kyang rab tu ston la/ de bzhin nyid kyi rang bzhin las kyang mi nyams pa 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
22b7(phal chen): kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa drug pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni thugs su chud pa'i rnam pa gcig gis gzhan dang gzhan mkhyen par bya ba/ chos de'i skyon med
22b8(phal chen): las rnam par ma 'das pa gnas pa med pa/ dge ba'i rtsa ba rnam par dag pa mnyam pa nyid kyi chos skyon med pas dus thams cad du gnas pa rab tu mkhyen te/ de la yang nyi ma gcig gam/ rmab
23a1(phal chen): phyed dam/ lo gcig gam/ lo brla 'am bskal pa 'jig pa dang / 'du bas rjes su bsnyag pa dang / phyir phyogs pa mi mnga' brar dus tshad med pa dang / nyi ma
23a2(phal chen): gcig dang / yud tsam gcig gi dus dang / snga dro nas nyi ma phyed kyi dus dang / phyi dro nas snga dro'i du dus dang / nyi ma gung nas phyi dro'i dus dang / nyi ma 'grang ba'i dus dang / nyi ma bdun dang / 
23a3(phal chen): zla ba phyed kyi dus dang / zla ba dang / lo dang / lo brgya'i dus dang / bskal pa gcig gi dus dang / tshod med grangs med pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i dus nas/ phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thub
23a4(phal chen): pa'i dus su chos bstan pa dang / chos kyi 'khor lo the/ gas pa med cing phyir mi ldog/ rgyun chad par mi 'gyur/ bral bar mi 'gyur/ bar chad par mi 'gyur
23a5(phal chen): med par mi 'gyur/ 'jig par mi 'gyur/ g.yo bar mi 'gyur/ ring du mi 'gyur/ 'khor de na gnas pa nyid du yang rgyun chang par mi 'gyur te/ 'di ni sangs
23a6(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa bdun pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad rtag tu ngus
23a7(phal chen): la bab par bzhugs pa ste/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mi 'jigs pa tshad med pa mnga' ba'o// tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa grangs med pa mnga' ba'o// 
23a8(phal chen): thadad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa tshad med pa mnga' nga'o// tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa zadang mi shes pa mnga' ba'o// tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa thogs pa med/ 
23b1(phal chen): bamanga' ba'o// tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa mtha' yas pa mnga' ba'o// thun mong ma yin pa'i tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa mnga' ba'o// tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa
23b2(phal chen): mthar thug pa med pa mnga' ba'o// tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa de kho na dang ldan pa mnga' ba'o// tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa tshig gi tshul thams cad rab tu rtogs pa rag
23b3(phal chen): ba'o// chos thams cad tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa mnga' ba'o// bsdam pa dang mos pa dang / dbang po ji lta bzhin du/ chos kyi tshul dang / rnam grangs tshul ji ltar rnam
23b4(phal chen): par bkod pa bzhin dus mtshams med par ston te/ mdo sde bye ba khrag khrig brjod du med pa'i yang brjod pa me dad pa rnams mdo sdeng dang de la thog ma dang / tha ma dang / dbu
23b5(phal chen): gi tshul gyis yang dag par ston te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thangs mkhas pa brgyad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
23b6(phal chen): rnams ni ming med kyang / ming dang rigs su byung ba'i chos thams cad tshig dang / yi ges shin tu dbyangs pa'i dbyings mngon par sangs rgyas pa ste/ ming 'das pa ma yin pa dang / 
23b7(phal chen): ming ma 'ongs pa ma yin pa dang / ming da ltar byung ba ma yin pa dang / ming sems can ma yin pa dang / ming zhing ma yin pa dang / ming chos ma yin pa dang / ming yon tan ma yin pa dang / 
23b8(phal chen): ming byang chub sems dpa' ma yin pa dang / ming sangs rgyas ma yin pa dang / ming grangs ma yin pa dang / ming grangs med pa ma yin pa dang / ming skye ba ma yin pa dang / ming
24a1(phal chen): pa ma yin pa dang / ming med pa ma yin pa dang / ming yod pa ma yin pa dang / ming gcig pa ma yin pa dang / ming tha dad pa ma yin pa dang / ming thams cad ma yin pa
24a2(phal chen): dadang / chos thams cad rang bzhin gyis brjod du med pa dang / phyogs med pa dang / brda med pa dang / tshig gi lam med pa dang / sgra dang bral ba/ sgra'i rnam pa thams cad mi 'byung ba yongs su
24a3(phal chen): bsgrubs pa med pa/ byas pa dang rnam par byas pa med pa/ rnam pa gcig ma yin pa/ rnam pa mang po ma yin pa yang thugs su chud la brjod pa dang / sprad pa thams cad la yang pha rol tu phyin pa
24a4(phal chen): mchog brnyes pa dag ste/ rnam par rtog pa'i yul mi ma dnga' bdag go// mngon par 'du mdzad pa med pa la ra rab tu brtson pa dag go// rtog pa dang kun tu rtog pa dang yongs su
24a5(phal chen): rtog pa 'gag pa dag go// spyod pa thams cad la mi gnas par spyod pa dag ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyu kyi thabs mkhas pa dgu pa'o// 
24a6(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos thams cad kyi gzugs ma skyes pa rab tu mkhyen pa ste/ tshor ba'i spros pa med pa dang / 'du shes kyi grangs med pa dang / 'du byed kun/ 
24a7(phal chen): tu rgyu ba med pa dang / rnam par shes pa nye bar len pa med pa dang / rang bzhin gyis zhi bar rab tu mkhyen te/ chos thams cad skye mched kyi rgyud med pa dang / khams rnams mi dmigs pa
24a8(phal chen): dang / chos thams cad mi 'jigs pa dang / chos thams cad bskyed du med cing rang bzhin gyis nam mkha' lta bu dang / chos thams cad dben pa dang / las med pa dang / rnam par smin
24b1(phal chen): ba med pa dang / stong bas 'byung ba med pa dang / mgrub pa dang / mabyung ba dang / grangs kyi mi brjod pa dang / yod pa ma yin pa dang / med pa ma yin pa dang / ma skyes pa dang / ma 'gags pa
24b2(phal chen): dang / kun nas nyon mongs pa med pa dang / rnam par byang ba med pa dang / skyon med pa dang / gnas med pa dang / yongs su gnas pa med pa dang / yongs su smin par byas pa med pa dang / 
24b3(phal chen): rnam par btul ba med pa dang / sems can med pa dang / sems can med pa ma yin pa dang / srog med pa dang / srog med pa ma yin pa dang / rkyen med pa dang / rkyen med pa ma yin pa dang / 
24b4(phal chen): rten pa med pa dang / rten pa med pa ma yin par chos thams cad thugs su chud kyang chos kyi dbyings thams cad shin tu bstan pa la pha rol tu phyin pa'i dam pa brnyes pa
24b5(phal chen): dag ste/ nges pa dang ma nges pa dang / log par nges pa'i phung po gsum rnam par dgod pa rnams la stobs bcus thugs su chud pa'i ye shes mi 'jigs pa bzhis
24b6(phal chen): rnam par dag pa'i sangs rgyas kyi yul chen po dang ldan pas seng ge'i sgra sgrog pa 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa bcu pa ste/ kye
24b7(phal chen): rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan
24b8(phal chen): 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgya chen po tshad med pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa rnams te/ de dag ni sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi brlabs ma gtogs par lha dang bcas pa'i 'ji/ 
25a1(phal chen): rten dang / 'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyis 'jug par mi nus pa'o// bcu gang zhe na
25a2(phal chen): phyogs bcu'i nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mthas gtugs pa'i chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyi 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du dga' ldan du skye ba bstan pa dang / byang / 
25a3(phal chen): chub sems dpa'i spyod pa mu med pa dag la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad de/ kha dog tshad med pa gzi brjid tshad me dra pa/ snang ba tshad med pa/ dadrangs chad med pa
25a4(phal chen): dbyangs kyi yan lag rnam par dag pa tshad med pa// gsung brjod pas rnam par dmig pa tshad med pa ting nge// 'dzin tshad med pa la spyod pa/ shes rab dang / ye she
25a5(phal chen): yul tshad med pa mang ba rnams lha dang bcas pa'i 'ji ga rten la phan 'dogs pa mdzad de/ bdud dang bcas pa/ tshangs pa dang bcas pa/ dge sbyong dang bram ze'i
25a6(phal chen): skye dgu dang bcas pa/ lha dang mi dang lha ma yin du bcas pa'i 'jig rten la phan 'dogs pa mdzad do// byams pa chen po'i spyod yul thogs pa med pa dang / thabs thugs rje chen
25a7(phal chen): po'i sgo'i mthar thug pas sems can la phan 'dogs pa mdzad do// bsod nams kyi stobs dang / mnga' phun sum tshogs pa dang / dbang po rnam par sbyang pa dang / cang shes kyi
25a8(phal chen): sems yongasu dag pas kyang sems can rnams la phan 'dogs pa mdzad do// theg pa sna tshogs rnam par dag pas kyang sems can rnams la phan 'dogs pa mdzad do// theg
25b1(phal chen): ba chen po yongs su rdzogs par bya bas kyang sems can rnams la phan 'dogs par mdzad do// 'gro ba thams cad gdon pas kyang sems can rnams la phan 'dogs pa mdzad de// 
25b2(phal chen): 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las dang po'o// dga' ldan gyi pho brang nas 'phos pa med kyang yum gyi skur gshegs shing / byang chub se/ 
25b3(phal chen): dpa'i sku tha ma skye bar bstan pa/ sgyu ma lta bur yongs su spyod pa sprul pa lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin gyi mthar thug pa/ mig yor lta bur rnam par dmigs pa/ nam mkha'i yul chad med
25b4(phal chen): par ldab pa/ bzhed pa bzhin du skye yang chags pa mi mang dab / smig rgyu ba lta bur bstan pa/ nyon mongs pa med dpa'i chos la yang dag par gzhol ba/ gnas med ci
25b5(phal chen): ye shes la gnas pa/ rang bzhin gyis 'dod chags dang bral bas rnam par dag pa/ rgyan shin tu rgya ma ba'i mdzod kyis sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// 
25b6(phal chen): khang pa brtsegs pa rin po che las byas pa'i pho brang chen po rin po che'i rgyan mang po ldan pa na bzhugs pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// rdzu 'phrul gyis kyang
25b7(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// yid la bya ba byin gyis brlabs chen pos kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// rnam par 'phrul ba'i mdzod chen po ya
25b8(phal chen): dag par bstan pas kyang / sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// ye shes kyi nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor chen pos kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// yum sku skyed pa'i snyun
26a1(phal chen): bzhugs pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// sangs rgyas kyi yul gyi spyod yul chen po brnyes pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzang // sa @/ 
26a2(phal chen): rgyus kyi byin gyis 'jig rten byin du brlabs pa mtha' yas pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// ting nge 'dzin chen po grangs med pa la rnam par spyod cing snyoms par 'jug pas
26a3(phal chen): kyang sengs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// ting nge 'dzin las bzhengs pa de dang de dag gis kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// spyod pa'i thog ma la yongs su mya ngan las 'das
26a4(phal chen): pa chen po'o mthar thugs pa'i bar du thog ma dang / dbus da dang tha ma'i tshul gyis kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las ma dzad ngo // sa 'di la gnyis su med pa thams cad mthar
26a5(phal chen): phyin par byas nas tha mar 'jig rten gyi grangs kyis skye bayongs su ston te/ skye bas kyang 'jig rten thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// gzhon nur gyur
26a6(phal chen): pas kyang 'jig rten thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// byang chub sems dpar gyur pas kyang 'jig rten thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// mngon par
26a7(phal chen): 'byung bas kyang 'jig rten thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// mngon par 'tshang rgya bas kyang 'jig rten thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// chos kyi 'khor lo/ 
26a8(phal chen): bskor bas kyang 'jig rten thams cad sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// thabs mkhas/ pa sna tshogs kyis kyang 'jig rten sna tshogs 'jig rten tshad med pa 'jig rten tu mtha' yas
26b1(phal chen): ba/ phyogs kyi dra nga'i rgyud dang / rigs thams cad kyi 'jig rten ma lus pa thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// zhing gi rgyang ma lus pa'i 'jig rten du sangs rgyas kyi phrin
26b2(phal chen): las mdzad do// las kyi rnam par smin pa ma lus pa'i 'jig rten du sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// sems can gyi rgyud ma lus pa'i 'jig rten du sangs rgyas kyi phrin las
26b3(phal chen): mdzad do// skye ba dang shi 'pho ba'i rgyud ma lus pa'i 'jig rten du sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do// sprul pa chen po'i rgyud dang / sangs rgyas kyi rigs dang / chos dran pa'i sgo 'tsha
26b4(phal chen): los kyang / sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad de/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las gnyis pa'o// dge bar spyod pa'i las rnam
26b5(phal chen): par dag cing / gdung rabs thams cad du ye shes kyi tshul rnam par dag pas sku tshe'i rgyud kyi tshul dang ldan pa/ sems can thams cad gdul ba thug su chung ba/ da
26b6(phal chen): ba'i rtsa ba thams cad yongs su rdzogs par mdzad cing btsun mo'i 'khor gyi nang na bzhugs pa ston kyang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi 'dod chags dang bral ba'i tshul gyi gnas la bzhugs pa
26b7(phal chen): rnams sgra dang / tshig thams cad dang bral bar brtags pas dngos po thams cad dngos po med pa las byung bar khong du chud par bya ba dang / dngos po thams cad shes pa la gzung bar bya ba
26b8(phal chen): dang / tshul khrims thams cad thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi mthar thug par yongs su rdzogs par bya ba dang / snying rje chen pos 'gro ba mu med pa la rnam par blta bar bya ba dang / byams
27a1(phal chen): pa chen pos sems can med pa'i yul la rab tu rtog par bya ba dang / dga' ba chen pos 'jig rten brjod du med par khong du chud par bya ba dang / btang snyoms chen pos sems/ 
27a2(phal chen): la dbang sgyur ba la gnas par bya ba dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i yon tan gyis rang yongs su rgyas par byed par bya ba dang / chos kyi dbyings kyi lus ma lus par mngon par sgrub par bya ba dang / 
27a3(phal chen): thams cad du gnas med pa'i lus yongs su rdzogs par bya ba dang / 'khor thams cad rnam par dag par nan tan du byed par bya ba dang / chos bstan pa rnam par brjod pa rab tu brjod par bya ba dang / 
27a4(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi dngos po la smod par bya ba dang / 'gro ba thams cad kyi nyes pa la rtog par bya ba mdzad cing spyod pa dang // dge ba'i rtsa bas rnam par smin pa yang dag par bstan pa
27a5(phal chen): dang / ji ltar bkod pa'i tshul du sems can gdul ba dang / yongasu ma smin pa'i sems can yongs su smin par bya ba dang / yongs su smin pa rnams tshul bzhin du
27a6(phal chen): gdul ba dang / grangs med pa'i thabs mkhas pa mngon par sgrub pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi phrin las phyir mi ldog pa yongs su bstan pa dang / sgo sna tshogs nas chos kyi spyod pa rab tu brjod pa
27a7(phal chen): dang sems can rnams kyi bsam pa sna tshogs rnam par snang ba dang / thugs rje chen po las byung ba'i chos kyi sprin gyis mngon par spang ba dang / thams cad la skyob pa'i byams pa chen po
27a8(phal chen): bskyed pa'i cho 'phrul gsum gyis yongs su brlan pa dang / sangs rgyas thams cad mthong ba dang / rnam par dmigs pa'i btsun mo'i 'khor gyi nang du bstan pa yan cad du 'jig rten mtha
27b1(phal chen): dang dpung med par sangs rgyas kyi phrin las yongs su bstan pa mdzad cing / ye shes mthu chen po thogs pa med pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi mngon par mkhyen pa bsgribs pa med par bsdun
27b2(phal chen): pa dang / chos rnam pa gsum gyis thabs mkhas pa dang ldan pa'i phrin las kyi mtha' dang / sku'i phrin las kyi mtha' shin tu rnam par dag pa dang / gsung gi phrin las ye shes nyams
27b3(phal chen): pa med pas rnam par dag po dang / thugs kyi phrin las kyi mtha' zab cing chags pa med pa'i mthar thugs pa'i thabs la mkhas pas sems can rnams kyi don mdzad de/ 'di ni sangs
27b4(phal chen): rgyas rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las gsum pa'o// / bam po drug cu lnga pa// rnam par rgyal ba chen po mnga' ba rnams ni btsun mo'i 'khor
27b5(phal chen): rgyan rnam par phye ba tshad med pa dang ldan pa/ yid du 'ong ba spangs te mngon par 'byung ba'i spyod pa yongs su bstan pas sems can rnams 'jig rten gyi gnas las bskyod pa dang // 
27b6(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi mngon par zhen pa rnam par bzlog pa dang / 'jig rten du gtogs pa thams cad mi rtag par shes par bya ba dang / 'jig rten gyi tshul la mngon par zhen pa rnam par bzlog pa dang / 'jig
27b7(phal chen): rten gyi dga' ba la sred pa yongs su bcang ba dang / 'jig rten nyon mongs pa byang shing nub pa la yang dag par spyod par bya ba dang / sems can gyi don rjes su dran par bya ba'i phyir/ mngon par
27b8(phal chen): 'byung ba'i don la rab tu gzhal ba dang / khyim pa'i tshul yongs su spang ba bstan pa dang / nyon mongs pa med pa'i chos kyi sbyor ba la yang dag par gnas par bya ba dang / sngon gyi sngon la/ 
28a1(phal chen): yongs su rdzogs par bya ba dang / yon tan gyi dkyil 'khor tshad med pa yongs su snang bar bya ba dang / ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor chen po brnyes pas sems can rnams kyi
28a2(phal chen): mi shes pa'i sgrib pa rab tu bsal ba dang / bdag nyid bsod nams kyi zhing bla na med par gyur par 'gro ba thams cad la bstan pa dang / dge ba'i rtsab thams cad sangs rgyas la bskyed pa'i // 
28a3(phal chen): ba'i rtsa ba'i nang du 'dus par 'gro ba thams cad la yang dag par brjod pa dang / bdag nyid kyis ye shes kyi don gzigs par bstan pa dang / sems can rnams rnam par dag pa'i sgor brjod/ 
28a4(phal chen): pa dang / sems can rnams kha na ma tho ba med pa'i sgorasgrub pa dang / 'jig rten thams cad du 'byung ba'i sgo rab tu bstan pa dang / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi rgyal
28a5(phal chen): mtshan yang dag par bsgreng ba mdzad cing mngon par 'byung / ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnam/ sa kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las bzhi pa'o// don gcig ma
28a6(phal chen): yin pa mkhyen pa dang ldan pa thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi mthar thug pa rnams ni/ chos thams cad mngon par 'tshang rgya bar bya'o zhes/ byang chub kyi shing drung du byon te/ byang chub
28a7(phal chen): tu mngon par 'tshang rgya bas kyang bdud kyi dpung thams cad rab tu bzhom pa dang / sku'i byin gyis brlabs kyi mdzod kyi chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad du rgyas par dgang ba'i phyir/ 
28a8(phal chen): byin gyis brlabs zad mi shes pa'i mthar thug pas mtha' rnam par spangs pa spyod pa tshad med pa rab tu brnyes pa thams cad mkhyen pa'i yul gyis rnam par rol pa'i ye shes kyi don
28b1(phal chen): dang ldan pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i yon tan yang dag par sgrub pa yongs su rdzogs pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du gdan rnam par bkram pas yongs su rgyas pa/ 
28b2(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi zhing ma lus pa thams cad du/ byang chub sems dpa' rnam par dmigs pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i stong ngangs pathob pa rnams kyis nal du lta ba/ byang chub sems dpa'
28b3(phal chen): thams cad kyi rnam pa dang / smon lam khyad par can dang ldan pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad kyis yang dag par bsam pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo zab mo rab tu
28b4(phal chen): skor ba sangs rgyas kyi yul tshad med pa bsams pas/ byang chub sems dpa' brjod du med pa'i 'byung gan das su gyur pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyad pa sna tshogs
28b5(phal chen): spyod pa la yang dag par gzhol ba'i byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rnam par dag pa mnga' ba 'ji garten gyi khams thams cad sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis byin du rlob
