28b6(phal chen): pa'i yul mnga' ba/ dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed pa'i sems can gyis rnam par dmigs pa dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad tha mi dad pa dang ldan pa 'byung ba'i sa byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa mtha' yas pa'i mthu'i
28b7(phal chen): gnas la yon tan gyi khyad par thams cad rab tu brnyes pas bzhugs pa 'jig rten gyi rnam pa thams cad ma lus pa'i mthar thug pa/ sems can gyi rnam pa thams cad dang / zhing gi rnam pa thams cad dang / chos
28b8(phal chen): kyi rnam pa thams cad dang / byang chub sems dpa'i rnam pa thams cad dang / yongs su smin par bya ba'i rnam pa thams cad dang / dus kyi rnam pa thams cad dang / 'dul ba'i rnam pa thams cad dang / sangs
29a1(phal chen): rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul ba'i rnam pa thams cad ma lus par mthar thug pa'i rnams 'gro ba ma lus pa thams cad du mos pa ji lta ba bzhin du rnam par 'tshang rgya bas/ sangs rgyas
29a2(phal chen): kyi phrin las mdzad de/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las lnga pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba mdzad pa phyir mi ldog
29a3(phal chen): pa'i tshul gyis phyir mi ldog pa'i 'khor lo dang / 'jig rten thams cad kyis khong du chud par 'gyur ba'i tshul gyis tshad med pa'i 'khor lo dang / mi 'jigs pa'i seng ge'i nga ro chen po'i tshul gyis thams cad
29a4(phal chen): ma lus par mngon par sangs rgyas pa'i 'khor lo dang / chos kyi mdzod mun pa med pa'i spos snang bar byed pa'i tshul gyis chos thams cad mkhyen pa'i mdzod kyi 'khor lo dang / 
29a5(phal chen): ye shes nam mkha'i dbyings ltar tshad med pa'i tshul gyis chag sa pa med pa'i 'khor lo dang / chos thams cad kyi dngos po med pa'i rang bzhin rab tu rtogs par bya ba'i tshul gyis bsgrings
29a6(phal chen): nga med pa'i 'khor lo dang / sems can thams cad kyi chos kyi mig rnam par sbyong ba'i tshul gyis 'jig rten thams cad kyi sgron ma'i 'khor lo dang / 'jig rten thams cad du rgyas par 'gengs pa'i tshul gyis
29a7(phal chen): thams cad mkhyen pa'i chos brjod pa'i 'khor lo dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad dang mi 'gal ba'i tshul gyis/ sangs rgyas thams cad 'dab 'dres par gyur pa'i 'khor lo dang / de dag la sogs
29a8(phal chen): pa rnam pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong du chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bas sems can thams cad kyi sems dang spyod pa'i rnam pa la chos kyi 'khor lo bskor te/ de ltar chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bas kyang / 
29b1(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sangs rgyas kyi phrin las bsam gyis mi khyab pa mdzad de/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sangs rgyas kyi phrin las drug pa'o// sangs rgyas / 
29b2(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams ni grong dang / grong khyer dang / grong rdal dang / rgyal po'i gnas su gshegs pas kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad de mi'i rgyal po'i gnas dang / lha'i
29b3(phal chen): rgyal po'i gnas dang / klu'i rgyal po'i gnas dang / gnod sbyin gyi rgyal po'i gnas dang / dri za'i rgyal po'i gnas dang / lha ma yin gyi rgyal po'i gnas dang / na mkha' lding gi rgyal po
29b4(phal chen): gnas dang / mi 'am ci'i rgyal po'i gnas dang / lto 'phye chen po'i rgyal po'i gnas dang / srin po'i rgyu dal po'i gnas dang / sha za'i rgyal po'i gnas dag tu
29b5(phal chen): gshegs kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/ sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad de/ 'di lta ste tshwa nga khyer gyi sgor byon na/ sa g.yo ba dang / 'od zer snang ba dang / 
29b6(phal chen): long ba rnams mig 'thob pa dang / 'on pa rnams sgra thos par 'gyur ba dang / smyos pa rnams dran pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dang / gos med pa rnams gos 'thob par 'gyur ba dang / sdug bsngal ba rnams
29b7(phal chen): bde ba 'thob pa dang / rol mo'i cha spyad ma dkrol ma brdungs par sgra yid du 'ong ba rang 'byin pa dang / rgyan snod na 'dug pa dang / gnas nas ma phog pa dang / ma bskyod ma dkrol bar bskyod
29b8(phal chen): cing dkrol ba'i sgra 'byung ba dang / bya sna tshogs mang po'i sgra skad yid du 'ong ba 'byung ba dang / lta na gtang mo bri zhing mi 'thun pa med pa'i sku mthong bas kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnam
30a1(phal chen): sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do// mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po bstan pas kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can rnams la
30a2(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad de/ yongs su gzigs pa dang / rnam par gzigs pa dang / brkyang ba dang bskum pas kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// gshegs
30a3(phal chen): pa dang slar bzhud pa dang / bzhengs pa dang / 'chag pa dang / bzhugs pa dang / gzigs pas kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// chos bstan pa dang / mi gsung
30a4(phal chen): bar bzhugs pas kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi// phrin las mdzad do// rdzu 'phrul gyi cho 'phrul dang // / yongs su bstan pa'i cho 'phrul dang / rjes su bstan pa'i
30a5(phal chen): cho 'phrul gyis kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams 'jig rten gyi khams kyi yul sems can bsam pa sna tshogs rgya mtsho dang ldan pa/ 'jig rten gyi spyod pa thams cad
30a6(phal chen): rgyu zhing 'byung ba dang ldan pa/ dge ba'i rtsa ba chen pos shin tu bstan pa/ sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa dang ldan pa/ sngon 'grogs 'grogs pa byang chub sems dpa' dang gnas pa'i sems can rnams la
30a7(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams ni sku gzugs blta na mi ngoms pa'o zhes bya bar gzhol ba dang / sangs rgyas rnams skye bar dkon no zhes bya bar yid
30a8(phal chen): ches par byed pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa mthong zhing / de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung thos pa ni bsod nams kyi chos dkar po'i 'byung gnas su gyur pa'o zhes sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa yid la
30b1(phal chen): byeng pa dang / 'jig rten thams cad rnam par dag pa ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa skye ba yin no zhes bya bar khong du chud par byed pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi yon tan bsngags pa ni mtha' yas pa'o zhes bya/ 
30b2(phal chen): bar yang dag par lta ba dang / mabyon pa'i sangs rgyas 'byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs yang dag par sgrub pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba dang / mos pa'i tshul thams cad kyis/ sarba/ 
30b3(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams mnyes par byed pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa rnams ni yon tan mtha' yas pa'o zhes khong du chud par byed pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa ni sems can thams
30b4(phal chen): cad la mngon du gyur par rtog pa dang / de bzhin gsheg/ rnas pa ni sems can gyi rigs bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i gnasu gyur par sems pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa ni
30b5(phal chen): zhing thams cad ni snang bar khong du chud pa dang / de lta bu'i dge/ ba'i rtsa ba thams cad 'byung bas/ 'jig rten thams cad na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can
30b6(phal chen): rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// ngang par byas pa dang / phyag 'tshal ba dang / thal mo sbyar ba byas pa dang / rjes su bstod pa dang / spyan drangs pa dang / mchod pa dang / mngon du
30b7(phal chen): mthong ba dang / 'dzum pa byas pa dang / sangs rgyas la dga' ba'i sems kyis mos par byas pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba'i sgo nas kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can rnams la
30b8(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// sangs rgyas rjes su dran par gyur pas kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// sangs rgyas
31a1(phal chen): mthong bar 'dod par bya bas kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku kha dog dang / 
31a2(phal chen): dbyibs kyi rnam pa tshad med pa bstan pas kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung thos par
31a3(phal chen): bya bas kyang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad de/ de dag la sogs pa/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las
31a4(phal chen): rnam pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong brjod du med pa dag 'jig rten dgyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du sems can tham/ sa cad kyi bsam pa dang / mthu dang 'dul ba ji lta ba'i
31a5(phal chen): tshul las mi 'da' bar 'byung ngo // de ltar sangs rgyas kyi phrin las 'jig rten thams cad kyi sems can kun gyi sems dang spyod pa dang / bsam pa la gnas pa dge ba rgya
31a6(phal chen): che ba tshad med pa dag phyir mi ldog pa'i yul dang snying rje chen pos rab tu bskul ba dang / sngon gyi smon lam gyis yongs su spro ba med pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mkhyen pa'i stobs pa
31a7(phal chen): shugs kyis 'jig rten thams cad du 'byung ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las bdun pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dgon pa la
31a8(phal chen): bzhugs sam/ zhi bar bzhugs sam/ dben par bzhugs sam/ sangs rgyas kyi rnam par spyod pa la bzhugs sam/ ting nge 'dzin chen po'i gnas la bzhugs sam/ gcig pu dgyes
31b1(phal chen): par bzhugs sam/ sku mi snang bar bzhugs sam/ ye shes zang mo'i gnas la bzhugs sam/ sangs rgyas kyi yul gyi stobs tshad med pa la bzhugs sam/ sgra'i yongs su spyod nga mi mchong
31b2(phal chen): bar bzhugs kyang rung ste/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las gzhan gyis mi tshugs pa'i ye shes dang / smon lam gyi tshul gyis mos pa bzhin du 'dul ba'i sems can
31b3(phal chen): rnams la rgyun mi 'chad par 'byung ste/ sangs rgyas lha yongs su tshol bas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun mi 'chad do// sangs rgyas klu yongs su tshol bas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun
31b4(phal chen): mi 'tshang ngo // sangs rgyas gnod sbyin yongs su tshol ba dang / sangs rgyas mi'am ci yongs su tshol ba dang / sangs rgyas lto 'phye chen po yongs su tshol ba dang / sangs rgyas srin sa
31b5(phal chen): yongs su tshol ba dang / sangs rgyas mi dang mi ma yin pa/ yongs su tshol ba dang / sangs rgyas nyan thos dngasangs rgyas rang sangs rgyas dang / sangs rgyas byang chub sem
31b6(phal chen): dpa' yongs su tshol bas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun mi 'chang ngo // chos ston pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun mi 'chang ngo // sangs rgyas gcig brjod pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las
31b7(phal chen): rgyun mi 'chad do// sangs rgyas thams cad brjod pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun mi 'chang ngo // byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa'i khyad par dang / smon lam thams cad gcig tu brjod pas
31b8(phal chen): kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun mi 'chang ngo // byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa gcig rnam par phye ste/ spyod pa tha dad pa brjod pas kyang / sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun mi 'chad do// 'jig
32a1(phal chen): rten gyi yul sangs rgyas kyi yul du brjod pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun mi 'chang ngo // sangs rgyas kyi yul 'jig rten gyi yul du brjod pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyan/ 
32a2(phal chen): mi 'chang ngo // yul ma yin pa sangs rgyas kyi yul du brjod pas kyang / sangs rgyas kyi phrin la rgyun mi 'chang ngo // nyin mtshan dang / yud du yan man dang / zla ba dang / lo 'grangs par
32a3(phal chen): bzhugs pa dang / yongs su bzhugs pa nas de bzhin du bskal ba brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i bar du bzhugs pas kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can rnams
32a4(phal chen): la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad de/ 'di ni sangs rgyas pa com ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las brgyad pa 'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams
32a5(phal chen): la 'byung gnas lta bu sems can thams cad kyi bsam pa kun la rnam par sbyong ba lta bu/ sangs rgyas rnams la dang / pa lta bu/ sems khong du chud par bya ba la shin tu mos pa lta bu/ 
32a6(phal chen): dbang po rnams la sgrub pa lta bu/ sems can skye dgu thams cad la 'dul ba lta bu/ 'gro ba thams cad la mos pa lta bu/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la 'byung ba lta bu/ byang chub tu zhug/ 
32a7(phal chen): pa rnams la stsal ba lta bu/ gzhan gyi dring mi 'jog pa rnams la ye shes snang ba lta bu dag ste/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten mi rtag par ston pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi drin las/ 
32a8(phal chen): rgyun chad par brjod pa dang / phrin las mdzad pa'i mthar thug par bstan pa dang / chos kyi rgyud rnams pa med pa'i dngos por brjod pa dang / srid pa'i tshul rtsa ba nas chad par brjod pa dang / sems can
32b1(phal chen): thams cad skyo bar bya bar bstan pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi rjes su 'gro ba'i sems su 'thun par bya ba dang / sku tsho'i mtha' lta bur sems can rnams kyis shes par bya ba dang / sems can rnams kyis
32b2(phal chen): 'jig rten thams cad du dga' bar bya ba med par bstan pa dang / sems can rnams la ma byon pa'i sangs rgyas gcig nas gcig tu brgyad pa mnyes par gyis shig par bstan pa dang / 
32b3(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams chos kyi 'khor lo skor ba bstan tu mi rung bar khong du chud par bya ba dang / 'jig rten rnams kyi rtsol ba bsgred pa dang / sangs rgyas la dmigs par brtson pa
32b4(phal chen): sems la dgod pa dang / yun du dran pa rnam par dag pas de bzhin gshegs pa mthong ba'i rnam par rtog pa bsti dad pa dang / skyo ba'i dbang po phyir bzlog cing / yongs su dag
32b5(phal chen): par mdzad pa dang / sangs rgyas la mos pa bskyed pa dang skyo bar gyur pa'i sems la byin gyis brlab par bya ba dang / sangs rgyas la dmigs pa'i skyen 'jig rten gyi
32b6(phal chen): khams ma lus pa thams cad du phyin par dgongs pa mdzad pa dang / sku thams cad bshig ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku gdung gis sems can rnams yongasu gzung ba mdzad pa dang / 'jig rte/ 
32b7(phal chen): rnam par 'khrugs pa dang / dregaso shing myos pa'i sems can rnams sdom pa la dgod pa mdzad cing yongs su mya ngan las 'da' bar ston pas kyang / sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun mi 'chad te/ 'a
32b8(phal chen): ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las dgu pa'o// de bzhin gshegs pa rnams mya ngan las 'da' ba'i tshe/ 'jig rten thams cad na sems can rnams smre sngags 'don ci
33a1(phal chen): dra ba dang / mya ngan byed pa dang / mchi ma 'byin pa dang / yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas zhe 'am/ thugs rje chen po zhe'am/ ded dpon n+dan pa na'am/ ngan par bzhed bzugs pa
33a2(phal chen): ba can zhe'am/ lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten gyi sems can thams cad kyi skyabs su gyur pa/ mgon du gyur pa/ rten du gyur pa/ bla na med pa bsod nams kyi zhing nub par gyur to zhe 'am/ sangs rgyas bcom
33a3(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams ni 'byung bar da/ 'o zhes rnam pa de lta bur smre sngags 'don pa dang / mya ngan byed pa dang / sangs rgyas mthong ba rjes su dran pa'i sems can rnams kyi bsam pa dang / yid la bya ba de dang de dag
33a4(phal chen): gi sgor/ sangs rgyas kyi phrin las tshad med pa rgyun mi 'chad do// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams yongs su mya ngan las 'dra' ba'i tshe/ 'di lta ste/ sems can rnams kyi sems dang par bya
33a5(phal chen): ba'i dbang dang / sems can rnams dad pas mchod par bya ba'i// dbang dang / sems can rnams lhag pa'i bsam pa rnam/ par sbyong bar bya ba'i dbang dang / sems can rnams yongasu smin
33a6(phal chen): par bya ba'i dbang dang / sems can rnams yongs su sbyang bar bya ba'i dbang dang / sems can rnams 'dul ba'i dbang dang / sems can rnams bsod nams kyi tshogs yongs su rdzogs pa
33a7(phal chen): bya ba'i dbang dang / sems can rnams de bzhin gshegs pa la mchod pas dmigs par bya ba'i dbang dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i mchod rten dam pa sna tshogs su brgyan pas/ phyogs dang yul sna/ 
33a8(phal chen): tshogs su sems can rnams kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba bsags par bya ba'i dbang gis sems can rnams kyi bsam pa dang / mos pa ji lta ba bzhin du sku gdung dang / ring bsrel byin gyis rlob ste/ lha dang
33b1(phal chen): klu dang / gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang / lha ma yin dang / nam mkha' lding dang / mi 'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po dang / mi'i gnas thams cad du 'dul ba dang / mos pa'i tshul ji lta ba bzhin du sku/ 
33b2(phal chen): gdung dang / ring bsrel byin gyis rlong ngo // rang gi sku rnam par phye ste/ sku gdung dang ring bsrel tshang med pa grangs med pa/ dpag tu med pa/ bsam gyis mi khyab pa brjod du med pa'i yang
33b3(phal chen): brjod du med pa byin gyis rlob bo// de bzhin gshegs pa'i mchod rten gyis sangs rgyas kyi sku gdung 'jig rten thams cad du rnam par phye ba de'i yul dang / phyogs kyi klu'i gnas dang / gnod
33b4(phal chen): sbyin dang / dri za dang / lha ma yin dang / nam mkha' lding / dang / mi 'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po'i gnas dang / mi'i gnas dang / srin po'i gnas dag tu/ sku gdung dang ring
33b5(phal chen): bsrel mchod par byed par 'gyur bas/ sku gdung gi ring bsrel da nga / dbu dang phyag sen gyi mchod rten dang / sangs/ rgyas bzhugs pa'i mchod rten la 'gro ba thams cad nges par
33b6(phal chen): sangs rgyas dran par 'gyur te/ chos la rab tu rten par 'gyur ro// dge 'dun la dad pa rab tu 'thob par 'gyur ro// yul dang phyogs kyi gnas de dang de dag tu 'ang rgyun mi 'chang bar sangs rgyas mchod pa
33b7(phal chen): la brtson pa'i bsam pas sbyin pa yongasu gtong bar 'gyur ro// bsod nams byed par 'gyur ro// mtho ris de dang de yongs su dag pa rab tu 'thob par 'gyur ro// rigs dang rgyud kyi bang
33b8(phal chen): nyid che ba rab tu 'thob par 'gyur ro// longs spyod chen po dang 'khor rnam par dag pa rab tu 'thob par 'gyur ro// lha dang mi'i phun sum tshogs pa nyams su myong bar 'gyur ro// log par
34a1(phal chen): ltung ba med pa'i lam yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas 'byung ba don yod pa rab tu sgrub par 'gyur ro// chos dkar po la gnas pa yongasu rdzogs par byed par
34a2(phal chen): 'gyur ro// khams gsum pa las 'byung ba'i lam yongs su sbyong bar 'gyur ro// theg pa gang la dad pa'i smon lam gyis nges par 'byung bar 'gyur ro// de bzhin gshegs pa de dang de dag la
34a3(phal chen): drin du gzo ba rab tu 'thob par 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams la brten pa dang / skyabs btsal ba dang / mgon btsal ba dang / dpung gnyen btsal ba'i sems bskyed par 'gyur
34a4(phal chen): ro// de ltar sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni yod su mya ngan las 'das kyang yon bsam gyis mi khyab rab sbyong ba/ bsod nams zad mi shes pa'i yon gyi gnas
34a5(phal chen): ngag ste/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig/ rten du byung na/ de ltar sems can rnams kyi dge ba'i/ rtsa ba rnam pa mang po rab tu bsags pas bsod nams kyi chogs
34a6(phal chen): rab tu rdzogs par 'gyur te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las bcu pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi
34a7(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgya chen po tshad med pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa rnams so// de dag ni sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs ma gtogs par lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten gyis tshang gzung bar mi nus pa'o// 
34a8(phal chen): 'das pa dang / ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyis 'jug par mi nus pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gnyis
34b1(phal chen): su med par myong cing ngos po rnam pa gnyis su med pa'i chos kyi dbang phyug gi chos rnams te/ bcu gang nen 'di lta ste/ sangs rgyas ma ldan 'das rnams ni/ lung bstan pa thams cad ston pa la/ 
34b2(phal chen): gnyis su med par spyod do// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/ sems can sangs rgyas kyi rjes su dran pa la bston pa rnams kyi sems dang bsam pa brjod du med pa 'byam klas pa rnams la
34b3(phal chen): gnyis su med par spyod do// sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad kyi don ma lus par mngon par sangs rgyas pas gnyis su med pa'i sku rnam par dmigs par mdzad do// 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / 
34b4(phal chen): da ltar byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la rang bzhin pa/ nyis su med par thugs su chung ba mnga' ba'o// 'byung ba/ dang / 'byung ba'i mtha' gnyis su med pa dang / sngon gyi mtha' dang / 
34b5(phal chen): phyi ma'i mtha' dang / da ltar byung ba'i mtha' gnyis su med par thu/ gas su chud pa mnga' ba'o// sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cang gnyis su med pas dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams
34b6(phal chen): cad gcig par rab tu mkhyen cing ston pa thugs su chud par mnga' ba'o// sangs rgyas gcig dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gsung gnyis su med par thugs su chud pa mnga' ba'o// de bzhin gshegs pa
34b7(phal chen): thams cad kyis thugs su chud pa dang / 'dul ba mdzad pa'i rnam par dmigs pa gnyis su med par thugs su chud pa mnga' ba'o// 'jig rten gyi chos thams cad/ sangs rgyas kyi chos gnyis su med par
34b8(phal chen): thugs su chung ba mnga' ba'o// 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad dge ba'i rtsa ba gcig ste/ gnyis su med par thugs su chud par mnga'o// kye
35a1(phal chen): rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gnyis su med par spyod cing / dngos po gnyis su med pa'i chos kyi dbang phyug gi chos so// kye rgyal ba'i sras/ 
35a2(phal chen): bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa bzhugs pa/ chos thams cad la rab tu bzhugs pa rnams so// bcu gang zhe na sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni
35a3(phal chen): chos kyi dbyings gnas pa'i ye shes thugs su chud ba la bzhugs pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni thugs rje chen po mi nyam pa la bzhugs pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
35a4(phal chen): ni smon lam ji lta ba bzhin du 'byung ba la bzhugs pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'dul ba'i sems can yo/ dngas su mi gtong ba la bzhugs pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan
35a5(phal chen): 'das rnams ni dngos po med pa la gnas pa'i chos nyid la bzhu/ gas pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku skal ba mnyam pa tha mi dad cing don yod
35a6(phal chen): pa la bzhugs pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni rtog tu mnyam par gzhag pa'i thugs la bzhugs pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos thams cad nyams pa med par
35a7(phal chen): gzhol ba la bzhugs pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chags pa med pa'i thugs kyis rnam par spyod pa la bzhugs pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos thams cad kyi
35a8(phal chen): mnyam pa nyid la 'jug pas grub pa med pa'i yang dag pa'i mtha'i mtshan nyid la bzhugs pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa bzhugs pa
35b1(phal chen): chos thams cad la bzhugs pa rnams so// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos thams cad ma lus par mngon par mkhyen pa rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na 'dis/ 
35b2(phal chen): ste/ chos kyi dbyis ma lus pa thams cad kyi 'das pa 'grangs pa mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang / ma 'ongs pa 'grangs pa mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang / da ltar byung ba 'gras/ 
35b3(phal chen): pa mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang / tshig gi lam mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang / 'jig rten gyi rgyud mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang / sems can gyi
35b4(phal chen): bsam pa dang / shes pa mtha' dag thams cad mngon par ma khye dan pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba chung dadu dang / 'bring dang / chen po dang / rnam pa sna tshogs rnam par
35b5(phal chen): gnas pa'i mtshan nyid kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams la bsam pa/ tshad med pa yongs su mi btang bas/ sangs rgyas kyi ya shes 'bar bar bya ba dang / yongs su rdzogs par bya ba
35b6(phal chen): mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang / chos thams cad 'tshang rgya ba'i mkhyen pa mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang / 'jig rten gyi rgyud thams cad rnam par dbye ba'i ye shes
35b7(phal chen): gzigs pa mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang / chos kyi dbyings kyi gzhi mig 'phrul gyi rnam pa lta bur dbye ba thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni
35b8(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos thams cad ma lus par mngon par mkhyen pa'o// / bam po drug cu rtsa drug pa kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni// 
36a1(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi stongs chen po/ stobs dam pa/ stobs tshad med pa/ stobs bdag nyid che ba/ stobs thub pa med pa/ stongs mi nyam pa/ 
36a2(phal chen): stobs snying po dang ldan pa/ stobs mi shigs pa/ stobs 'jig rten thams cad kyis bsam gyis mi khyab pa/ stobs sems can thams cad kyis mi 'phrogs pa/ sangs rgyas kyi rgyal
36a3(phal chen): mtshan stobs po che dpa' bo chen po'i stobs ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ sangs rgyas kyi sku ni pha rol gyi gnod pa thams cad kyis mi shigs mi chong pa'o// 'jig rten gyi yul thams
36a4(phal chen): cad kyis sku tshe'i dbang po nyams par mi nus pa'o// 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi bskal pa'i me'i gdung bas 'tshig par mi nus pa'o// 'jig rten gyi khams
36a5(phal chen): thams cad 'jig par gtogs pa'i chu'i phung por 'grongs par mi 'gyur ba'o// bdud thams cad dang / bdud/ kyi sde thams cad dang / lha thams cad kyi dpung dang / klu
36a6(phal chen): dang gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang lha ma yin dang / nam mkha' lding dang / mi 'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po dang / mi dang mi ma yin pa thams cad kyi dpung dang / sha za dang / srin po thams cad kyi
36a7(phal chen): dang / sems can ma lus pa thams cad kyi dpung gis brgal bar dka' ba'o// rdo rje ri rab kyi tshil gyi char pa dang / khor yug gi'i chen po tsam dang / stong gsum gyi stong chen po tsam gyi rdo rje'i char/ 
36a8(phal chen): babakyang / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi bsdugacig kyang 'gul bar mi 'gyur/ g.yo bar mi 'gyur te/ bag changa'i shas mi
36b1(phal chen): mnga' ba'o// bzhugs sam/ bzhengs sam/ bzung dam/ gzims kyang d+hA n+te/ snong lam 'gyur ba med de// de bzhin gshegs pa gang na bzhugs pa'i yul de dang / ro'ag la rab tu yang / 
36b2(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa dgyes na kun tu 'bab par mi 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas kyi zhabs 'bring rnams la yang gnod par mi 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas kyis byin gyis brlabs pa'i sems can rnam
36b3(phal chen): la yang gnod par mi 'gyur zhing mi g.yon/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku lta la smos kyang ci dgos te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu bo che chen po'i stobs sangs rgyas kyi
36b4(phal chen): spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos dang po'o// gzhan yang sang ngas rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams dgyes na/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyis klas pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams
36b5(phal chen): thams cad ri rab kyi ri dang bcas pa/ khor yug dang khor/ yug chen po'i ri dang bcas pa/ rgya mtsho dang ri dang nags/ tshol thibs po dang / sems can gnas pa'i gnas tha dad
36b6(phal chen): pa kun dang bcas pa/ de lta bu'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa'i ba spu'i bu ga gcig tu btsud de/ phyi ma'i mtha'i bsgral pa'i mur drug par bzhag kyang de bzhin gshegs
36b7(phal chen): pa'i byin gyi brlabs ma gtogs par sems can rnams kyis shes par mi nus so// de bzhin gshegs pa de dag ni de snyed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams sku'i ba spu'i khung bu gcig gis bzung / 
36b8(phal chen): ste/ phyi ma'i mtha'i bskal pa'i mur thug par bsnams shing / gshegs sam/ bzhugs sam/ bzhengs sam/ gzims kyang rung ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i thugs skad kyi
37a1(phal chen): tsam yang skyob mi mnga'o// chad cing drab par mi 'gyur ro// mthu nga stobs la yongs su nyam par 'gyur ba mi mnga'o// spyod lam rnam par 'gyur ba mi mnga'o// 
37a2(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras 'di lta ste dper na/ na mkha' ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad 'dzin kyang skyo ba med do// dub par med do// gnod pa med do// med par mi
37a3(phal chen): 'gyur ro// mi g.yo mi 'byung / mi 'jig go// de bzhin du sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyang baspu'i khung bu gcig du 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad bsnams kyang / de'i rgyus
37a4(phal chen): thugs skad cig tsam du yang mi bde ba'i sku nyams mi 'byung ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu bo che chen po'i stobs/ sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan
37a5(phal chen): gyi chos gnyis pa'o// gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom/ ldan 'das rnams gshegs stabs gcig tu bzhud/ pas sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med
37a6(phal chen): pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams yongs su 'da' zhing thugs bskyed pa gcig gis bskal pa tha dad pa'i rim pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rdul
37a7(phal chen): shin tu phra ba snyed 'byung bar mdzad do// de lta bur gshegs pas bskal pa 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed du gshegs shing / 'jig rten gyi khams thams
37a8(phal chen): cad kyi sems kyi rgyud ji snyed pa'i skal par bzhung ngo de/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams tsam du 'khor kun tu rgya che zhing yangs pa'i 'khor yug
37b1(phal chen): chen par rnga rje'i ri dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rnam pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa la bsgres pa snyed kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyang de la bsgres pa de snyed ba spu'i khung bu gcig tu srung de/ 
37b2(phal chen): spu'i khung bu gcig tu ji lta ba bzhin du sku'i ba spu'i khung bu thams cad du btsud de/ ba spu'i khung bu yang sems can thams cad snyeng du gyur la de dag thams cad bsnams te/ de snyed kyi ba spu'i khung
37b3(phal chen): bur tshul de bzhin du bshams te/ thugs bskyed pa de lta bus de bzhin gshegs pa 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du rgyu zhing gshegs sam/ phyogs kyi dra ba thams cad du rgyu zhing gshegs
37b4(phal chen): sam nam mkha'i dbyings thams cad du rgyu zhing gshedags sam/ 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyud 'grangs pa/ da sngon gyi mthar gtogs pa nas bzung ste/ phyi ma'i mtha'i bskal
37b5(phal chen): pa'i mur thug par de bzhin du gshegs pas bskal pa tha mas cad zad par gyur kyang de bzhin gshegs pa bzhud pa la brtson pa ni nyams par mi 'gyur ro// sku nyam chung bar
37b6(phal chen): mi 'gyur ro// thugs rnam par 'khrug par mi 'gyur ro// ting nge 'dzin nyams par mi 'gyur ro// de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku yongs su nyams par mi 'gyur te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom
37b7(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu bo che chen po'i stobs/ sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos gsum pa'o// gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni bsod snyoms gcig bcu
37b8(phal chen): nas bskal pa brjod du med par dkyil mo krung gcig bcas pas nyin mtshan gyi rgyud du sngon gyi mtha' dang / phyi ma'i mtha'i mur gtogs pa'i bskal pa 'das par bzhugs kyang sku mi g.yo zhing
38a1(phal chen): bde ba'i dam pa la spyod pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi rnam par spyod pa bsam gyis mi khyab pas/ rnam par spyod kyang sems can 'ga' tsam la'ang / sangs rgyas kyi phrin
38a2(phal chen): las rgyun 'chad par mi 'gyur ro// de bzhin gshegs pa'i sgra de la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad yongs su bkod de/ 'jig rten gyi khams de dag gi sems can gcig gi lus kyang 'jig rten
38a3(phal chen): gyi khams sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang sdod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed tsam du che bde lta bu gyur la/ sems na gcig gi lus kyi tshad ji tsam pa de tsam gyi lus su sems can thams cad kyang rgyan
38a4(phal chen): la sems can de dag re re'i gzugs kyang 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi lding ji tsam yod pa de tsam du gyur te/ sems can gcig ji ltar lci ba bzhin du sems
38a5(phal chen): can thams cad re re'i ljing kyang de tsam du 'gyur te/ sems can de dag thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa'i phyag so ra gyi rtse mo gcig la phyi ma'i mtha'i bskal pa'i mur thug par
38a6(phal chen): bsnams te/ phyag sor gyi rtse mo gcig gis ji ltar bsnams pa de bzhin du phyag sor thams cad kyi rtse mo la'ang de tsam re re bsnams kyang / de'i phyir de bzhin gshegs pa la sku mnyel
38a7(phal chen): ba'am thugs dub par mi 'gyur te thugs bskyed pa'i cha shas shin tu phra ba gcig tsam du yang sdug bsngal mi bde ba skye bar mi 'gyur ro// de bzhin du 'jig rten gyi khams la 'jug
38a8(phal chen): pa dang / na mkha'i dbyings la 'jug pa dang / phyogs kyi dra ba'i rnam pa la 'jug pa re re dang / de lta bu la 'jug pa/ nam mkha'i khams ma lus pa'i dbyings kyis klas pa/ chos
38b1(phal chen): / kyi dbyings kyi mthas gtugs pa/ sgra'i rtsa ma ma shas kyis gzhal ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams la 'jug pa thams cad re shing yang / sna ma cha shas kyis gzhal te/ nam ma pan
38b2(phal chen): dbyings kyi kun tu khyab pa thams cad ma lus pa'i sgra'i rtse mo'i cha shas kyi tshad kyis nam mkha'i dbyings la 'jug pa thams cad du zhugs te/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyod lam 'di'i tshul dang / 
38b3(phal chen): skyil mo krung gcig tu bzhugs pa'i spyod pas/ sngon gyi mtha' dang / phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa'i bskal pa zang par mdzad de/ bskal pa 'da' bar mdzad cing bskal pa la rab tu 'jug ste// 
38b4(phal chen): 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu bo che chen po'i stobs/ sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos bzhi pa'o// gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
38b5(phal chen): rnams ni sku gcig la dbu sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed byin gyis brlabs te/ dbu re re la ljags sangs rgyas kyi zhing
38b6(phal chen): brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed byin gyis brlabs nas/ de dag re res kyang dbyangs kyi yan lag dang / sgra skad kyi gsung sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang
38b7(phal chen): brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed re re brjod de/ chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa'i sems can gyi khams thams cad go bar mdzad cing dbyangs kyi yan lag dang / sgra skad kyi gsung re res
38b8(phal chen): kyang mdo sde sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed bshang la mdo sde re re la yang chos bstan pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du
39a1(phal chen): med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed rab tu gzhol bar mdzad de/ chos bstan pa gcig las kyang chos kyi tshig dang / yi ge sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du
39a2(phal chen): med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed brjod par gyur la/ chos bstan pa gcig la ji lta ba bzhin du chos bstan pa thams cad las kyang de snyed kyi chos kyi tshig dang / yi ge brjod de/ de ltar brjod pas
39a3(phal chen): bskal pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed du rab tu bstan la bskal pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu
39a4(phal chen): phra ba snyed zad par gyur kyang / da dung gzhan yang bskal/ pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du da med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed du brgyud cing rab tu ston pa'i
39a5(phal chen): tshul gyi rnams grangs 'dis bskal pa 'jig rten gyi kham sa thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed du rab tu bstan la/ rnam grangs 'di 'dra bas bskal pa 'jig rten gyi khams tham
39a6(phal chen): cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyeng zad la sems can thams cad kyi sems kyi spyod pa snyed kyi bskal pa 'das par gyur te/ phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa'i bskal pa zad cing 'das par byas kyang de bzhin
39a7(phal chen): gshegs pa'i sprul pa chos thams cad snang ba'i 'khor lo bskor ba dang / chos thams cad rab tu shes par bstan cing lung bstan pa dang / the tsom thams cad rab tu gcod pa'i chos kyi 'khor
39a8(phal chen): lo bskor ba dang / chos thams cad snang bar byed pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad brjod pa'i rgyun dang ldan pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba dang / 
39b1(phal chen): ye shes kyi nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor chen po'i rgyan dang ldan pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba dang / 'gro ba thams cad ma lus pa'i ye shes kyi sgron ma chen pos brgyan pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba
39b2(phal chen): dang / tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa dang / mi 'jigs pa chen pos brgyan pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba rgyan mi 'chang ngo // sangs rgyas kyi sku gcig gi byin gyis brlabs kyis ji lta ba de bzhin
39b3(phal chen): du chos kyi 'khor lo'i sprin chen po dpe thams cad la dpe med par rab tu 'byung bar 'gyur ro// de bzhin du chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi na mkha'i dbyings kyi mthas gtugs pa sku'i/

39b5(phal chen): sprul pa de snyed de snyed du thugs kyi skad cig re re la phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa'i bskal par sprul pa mdzad cing / de bzhin gshegs pa'i sprul pa'i sku thams cad las de bzhin
39b6(phal chen): gshegs pa'i sku re re la'ang de snyed de snyed kyi dbu mnga' bar gyur la gzung de bzhin du skyu re re la'ang de snyed de snyed kyi ljags mnga' bar gyur te/ ljags re re las kyang de snyed ngo snyed kyi dbyangs kyi yan

39b8(phal chen): snyed kyi mdo sde bshad par gyur la/ mdo sde de dag re re la yang de snyed de snyed kyi chos bstan par rab tu gzhol ba mdzad de/ chos bstan pa de dag re re las kyang de snyed nge snyed kyi chos kyi tshig
40a1(phal chen): yi ge brjod par gyur la chos kyi tshig dang / yi ge de dag re res kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad dbyangs kyi rgyas par bkang ste/ sems can gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad/

40a3(phal chen): bskal pa phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa'i bar du rgyun 'chad par mi 'gyur te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu bo che chen po'i stobs/ sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal
40a4(phal chen): mtshan gyi chos lnga pa'o// gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom/ ldan 'das rnams ni thugs dpal gyi be'us brgyan pa rdo rje chen po ltar shin tu bstan par grub pa mnga' bdag ste/ 
40a5(phal chen): de dag byang chub kyi shing drung du byon na bdud sdig to can gyis se mas can thams cad snyed kyi bdud kyi sde gzugs sna tshogs can shin tu mi sdug pa/ 'jigs 'jigs ltar/ 
40a6(phal chen): 'dug pa rab tu sdang ba'i gzugs can 'jig rten thams cad shin tu 'jigs pa'i gzugs can rab tu skye g.ya' ba skyed pa'i gzugs can/ bdud shin tu mi sdug pa'i gzugs 'chang ba/ rab
40a7(phal chen): mchog por 'jigs pa 'jigs pa chen po skyed pa/ 'gro ba thams cad gsod pa/ 'jig rten thams cad phung par byed pa/ de lta bu sha stag gis byang chub kyi shing drung dang
40a8(phal chen): chos kyi dbyings thams cad dang / na mkha'i dbyings kyi mthar thugs par gang par gzigs kyang byang chub kyi shing drung na bzhugs pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa rnams la bsnyengs pa mi mang/ 
40b1(phal chen): bag cha ba mi mnga'o// ba spu gcig kyang g.yo ba med do// thugs kyi cha shas shin tu phra ba 'ga' tsam gyis kyang de ltar rnam pa tha dad pa'i gzugs la mtshan ma rnam pa tha dad pa 'dzin pa mi ma
40b2(phal chen): ste shin tu brtan no// g.yo ba med do mi sgul to// 'gyur ba med // rnam par rtog pa med do// shin tu zhi ba'o// bsnyengs pa dang / bag tsha ba thams cad dang shin tu bral lo// 
40b3(phal chen): sdug pa dang khong khro ba shin tu spangs so// sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa rgyun mi 'chang ngo // byams pa chen po'i stobs dang ldan pa'o// thugs rje chen po'i gnas kyis dbang po shin tu dben pa

40b6(phal chen): zil gyis mnan te spa gong ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa lo skyabs tshol lo// de dag la'ang bcom ldan 'das de dag cho 'phrul chen po gsum gyis de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'dul ba ma
40b7(phal chen): pa nye bar sgrub ste/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub las phyir mi ldog par 'gyur ro// 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu bo che chen po'i stobs/ sangs
40b8(phal chen): rgyas kyi sbyang ba'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos drug pa'o// gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gsung thogs pa med pa ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa de dang de dag thams cad du sem
41a1(phal chen): can rnams 'dul ba'i don gyis rnam par dmigs par kun sa khyab par 'byung ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung de ni ri rnams la thogs pa med do// ri rab la thogs pa med de/ 
41a2(phal chen): rin po che'i ri la thogs pa med do// khor yug dang khor chen po la thogs pa med do// lha'i khyim la thogs pa med do// klu'i khyim la thogs pa med do// gnod sbyin gyi khyim la
41a3(phal chen): thogs pa med do// dri za'i khyim la thog pa med do// lha ma yin gyi khyim la thogs pa med do// na mkha' lding gi khyim la thogs pa med do// mi'am ci'i khyim la thogs pa med do// 
41a4(phal chen): lto 'phye chen po'i khyim la thogs pa med do// mi dang mi ma yin pa'i khyim la thogs pa med do// gal brgyal 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad na yod pa'i sgra chen
41a5(phal chen): po 'jig rten rnam pa tha dad pa'i sgras 'jig rten gyi khams thA mas cad gang ste/ ca co 'dres par gyur kyang de la de/ bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung ni 'dul ba'i sems can rnam
41a6(phal chen): kyi rna ba'i rnam par dmigs pa la bsgribs pa med pa yin te/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung 'ba' shig de dag gi rna ba'i rnam par dmigs pa la lhang nge lham me lhan ne ste go bar mdzad
41a7(phal chen): pa'i tshig dang / yi ge rnams kyang rlag par mi 'gyur te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu bo che chen po'i stobs/ sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos bdun
41a8(phal chen): pa'o/ gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi thugs ni chags pa mi mnga' ba ste/ bskal pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med par yongs
41b1(phal chen): sbyangs pa'o// 'das pa dang / mabyon pa dang / da lta byung ba'i sangs rgyas thams cad dang / rgyan gcig tu gyur pa'o// dag pa med cing rnam par ngas te shin tu gsal ba'o/ 
41b2(phal chen): bdag gi zhes bya ba mi mnga' ba'o// chos thams cad la mi gnas pa'o// nang na gnas pa ma yin pa'o// phyi rol na gnas pa ma yin pa'o// ma skyes pa'o// dmigs pa thams cad
41b3(phal chen): kyis dben pa'o// zhi zhing gnas pa med pa'o// rtsom pa med pa'o// 'du shes sna tshogs thams cad la mi gnas pa'o// dngos po'i rnam par rtog pa thams cad 'gags pa'o// 
41b4(phal chen): rang bzhin gyis 'od dang zhing gsal ba'o// yongasu dag pa/ 'o// dmigs pa dang / yid la bya ba thams cad nga// nga ma 'dres pa'o// chos thams cad nyon mongs pa med pa'i
41b5(phal chen): yul dang ldan pa'o// yang dag pa'i mtha' 'dod chags dang bral bas dag pa'o// chos kyi dbyings shin tu bsten pa'i mthar thug pa'o// chos kyi dbyings kun nas mi zad pa dang
41b6(phal chen): ldan pa'o// 'du shes kyi rnam pa thams cad kyi tshad dang tshad med pa dang bral ba'o// 'dus byas dang 'dus ma byas kyi brjod pa thams cad 'gags pa'o// tshig gi lam gyis brjod du med pa'i
41b7(phal chen): mthar thug pa'i yul lo// mi zang ba dang chags pa med pa'i dbyings kyi mthar thug pa'o// ye shes sngon du 'gro ba'o// stobs bcu'i rgyan du gyur pa'o// chos thams cad kyis rnam par dag par
41b8(phal chen): thabs mkhas pas byung ba'o// chos sna tshogs dang / chos du ma dang / chos thams cad shin tu bstan pa dang mi 'gal ba'o// dus gsum du tha dad pa med pa'o// chos kyi dbyings thams cad chos/ 
42a1(phal chen): gzhi med pa thams cad kyi mnga'i pha rol tu phyin pa gnyis pa'o// chos thams cad la mnga' ba'i 'byung gnas dang mdzod du gyur pa'o// chos kyi tshul thams cad la
42a2(phal chen): dgongs pa khyad par du rmongs pa med pa'o// zhing gi rgyung du gtogs pa thams cad dang phyogs kyi dra ba dang / rgyud 'byam klas pa ma lus pa thams cad la mi gnas pa brtan zhing mi g.yol
42a3(phal chen): nyams pa med pa'i ye shes kyis rab tu gzigs pa chos ma lus pa thams cad kyi mthar thug pa zag pa thams cad yongs su zad pa thugs rnam par grol zhing zag pa mi mnga' ba dang / shes rab
42a4(phal chen): rnam par grol bas shin tu rnam par grol ba yang dag pa'i mtha' mi zad pas klas pa/ chags pa med par rnam dpar spyod pa rtag tu mnyam par bzhag pa/ dus gsum thas
42a5(phal chen): cang du bsgribs pa med par 'byung ba/ sems can tham sa cad kyi dus gsum gyi sems dang spyod pa thams cang ma lus par thugs skad cig gis rab tu mkhyen pa
42a6(phal chen): ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi mthu bo che chen po'i stobs sangs rgyas kyi spyod ba'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos brgyad pa'o// gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi
42a7(phal chen): chos kyi sku ni sgra mi mnga' ba ste/ rang bzhin gcig tu gyur pas sangs rgyas thams cad kyi yul tshang med pa'i sku'o mtha' dang dpung med par yongs su grub pa'i sku'o// 'jig rten thams cad
42a8(phal chen): kyis zad par mi nus pa'i sku'o// khams gsum pas gos pa med pa'i sku'o// brten pa'i skus rnam par dmigs pa'o// lhag pa'i bsam pa dang rjes su dran pa'i byin gyi brlabs kyis
42b1(phal chen): sku'i rang bzhin yang dgu par ston pa ma// bden pa med pa dang / brdzun pa med pa'i sgra mnyam nyid kyi yongs su ga pa'o// chos kyi su bzung ba dang / byon pa med pa'i mu'o// 'dus ma byas pas
42b2(phal chen): 'jig pa med pa'i sku'o// mtshan nyid med pas mtshan nyid gcig po'i chos kyi sku'i rang bzhin no// yul na mi gnas pa dang / phyogs na mi gnas pa'i sku'o// ma lus pa thams cad
42b3(phal chen): kyi lus kyi sku'o// sangs rgyas kyi khyu mchog gi mthu phyung ba dang / rnam par 'phrul pa mtha' yas pa'i sku'i rang bzhin no// lus thams cad du yongasu gzhol ba'i sku sna tshogs su rnam par
42b4(phal chen): dmigs pa mdzad kyang chos kyi sku'i tshul gyi rjes su 'drang ba'o// ye shes kun tu snang ba'i snying po can no// sku yongs kyi/ mdzod du gyur pa'o// chos kyi dbyings rnam pa tha dad pa med
42b5(phal chen): pa shin tu bstan pa'i sku'o// khams gsum ma lus patha mas cad rgyas par 'gengs pas kun tu khyab pa'i sku'i bzhin no// mi g.yo mi dgongs pa'i sku rnam par dag pa'o// 
42b6(phal chen): yod pa yang ma yin med pa yang ma yin pa'i tshul dang tshul ma yin par rab tu brjod pa'i sku'o// sems can gyi mos pa rnam pa sna tshogs 'dul bar 'gyur ba'i sku'o// 'gags pa yang ma yin// 
42b7(phal chen): ma 'gags pa yang ma yin pas 'dul ba ston pa'i sku'o// yon tan rin po che thams cad yang dag par byung bas shin tu 'phags pa'i sku'o// chos thams cad sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi de bzhin nyid
42b8(phal chen): du yang dag par bsgrubs pa'i sku'o// rang bzhin gyis rab tu zhi zhing bsgribs pa med pa'i mthar thug pa'i sku'o// thogs pa mi mnga' bas chos thams cad thugs su chud pa'i sku'o// thams cad
43a1(phal chen): mams sar+b+ba sa sa rnam pa gas / 'ag tan thamasas du shin zhum par bye ba'i sul/ bya mthag cang brnabs pa ma la/ mas
43a2(phal chen): rnam par thar pas ye shes thams cad kyi rjes su 'brang zhing sa dag par gzhol bas thugs su chung pa'i sku ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu 'a che chen po'i stobs sangs rgyas

43a4(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad kyis byung ba'o// / mngon par 'grub pa'i spyod pa khyad par du 'phags pa'i smon lam dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pas rnam par ngas

43a6(phal chen): cad kyis bzung ba'o// byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa rgya mtsho'i spyod pa'i tshul thams cad thugs su chung ba'o// smon lam dang spyod pa chen pos yongs su mi dog pa'o// spyod pa thams cad mi maH
43a7(phal chen): pa med pas yongs su rdzogs par byas pa'o// spyod pa'i stobs la thug par dka' ba'i spyod pa thams cad kyis mngon par 'byung ba'o// spyod pa thams cad kyi rnam par dag pa'o// byang chub sems dang/ 
43a8(phal chen): spyod pa legs par spyad pas rgyung dma' ba med pa'o// sangs rgyas thams cad kyis tshad med par spyad pa'o// ting nge 'dzin thams cad kyi spyod yul mtha' yas pa'o// lam thams cad kyis
43b1(phal chen): rab tu brjod ba ma yin pa'o// lam gyi yul mang ba'o// lam thams cad la rab tu zhugs par// ye shes ngas pa'i stongs kyi tshul mkhyen pa'o// ngag chab mi mnga' bas chos kyi char 'bebs

43b6(phal chen): pa'i shes pa thams cad kyis bsam gyis mi khyab pa'o// chos thams cad ma lus par mkhyen cing gzigs pas sems can thams cad yongs su skyob pa'o// dus gsum yangs pa
43b7(phal chen): thams cad kyi tshul shin tu phra ba mtha' dang dpung med pa ma lus par mkhyen pa'o// 'jig rten las 'das pa'i don mkhyen pa'i phyir phra ba'i ye shes thugs su chud bas 'jig rten gyi khams ma

44a1(phal chen): 'grangs pa thams cad thugs su chung ba'i ye shes kyis yi ge med pa'i chos thugs su chud pa'o// yi ge sna tshogs rnam par phye ba dang / yi ge thams cad smos
44a2(phal chen): shing brjod pa mkhyen pas brjod du med pa thugs su chud pa'o// kun tu bzang po'i ye shes kyis dge ba'i chos spyad pa thams cad rnam par dag pa'o// dam bcas pa'i tshul bzhin/

44a5(phal chen): lus pa thams cad yul du gyur pa'o// dus gsum thams cad la thugs skad cig gis chags pa med par mkhyen cing thugs su chud pa'i yul dang ldan pa'o// de bzhin
44a6(phal chen): gshegs pa thams cad kyi sangs rgyas 'byung ba ma lus par yul du gyur pa'o// 'jig pa med par 'dul ba thams cad yul du gyur pa'o// thams cad kyi rjes su song zhing rnam par
44a7(phal chen): dag pa'i yul thams cad mngon par sangs rgyas pa'o// sa mtshams med cing thug pa'i mngon par shes pa rnam par sangs rgyas pa'o// sems can thams cad kyi sems dang yid dang /

44b1(phal chen): pa'o// 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rnam pa thams cad la mu med pa'o// dus gsum gyi rnam pa thams cad la mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas kyi khyu mchog gi mthu phyung ba'i rnam pa thams cad
44b2(phal chen): la tshad med pa'o// shes bya'i rnam pa thams cad la lhag ma ma lus pa ste/ de dag thams cad lhag ma med par mngon par sangs rgyas pas/ sangs rgyas kyi ye shes sangs rgyas
44b3(phal chen): kyi rdzu 'phrul dang / rnam par 'phrul pas byung ba thams cad thugs su chud pa dang / mkhyen pa thams cad rgyun 'chang ba med de/ de la sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sangs rgyas

44b5(phal chen): yin/ thugs rje chen po'i sbyor bas dus thams cad/ du rtag tu rgyun mi 'chad par chos bstan pa la spyod pas/ mtha' dang dbus med par spyod pa yin te/ 'di ni sangs

44b7(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis mthu bo che chen po'i stobs sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos rnams te/ 'das pa dang / ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i
44b8(phal chen): sems can thams cad dang / nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyis bsam gyis mi khyab cing dpag tu mi nus pa dag go/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs
45a1(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi thogs pa mi mnga' ba rnams te/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dga' ldan gyi tshe ji srid par bzhugs nas 'pho ba la thogs
45a2(phal chen): pa mi mnga'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni zla ba bcus bltam pa bstan pa la thogs pa mi mnga'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/ mngon
45a3(phal chen): par 'byung bar dgyes pa'i thugs kyi mngon par 'byung ba la thogs pa mi mnga'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni byang chub kyi shing drung du bzhugs nas/ sangs rgyas kyi chos
45a4(phal chen): thams cad mngon par 'tshang rgya bas thogs pa mi mnga'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni thugs skad cig gis sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad mngon par sangs rgyas nas
45a5(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa thams cad yongs su bstan pa la thog/ sa pa mi mnga'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
45a6(phal chen): ni dus bzhin du 'dul ba rnams la chos kyi 'khor lo skor ba la thogs pa mi mnga'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dge ba'i rtsa ba ji ltar bskyed pa'i tshul bzhin du dus la bab par
45a7(phal chen): bshad cing lung bstan pa la thogs pa mi mnga'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dus la bab pa'i tshul bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad pa la thogs pa mi mnga'o// 
45a8(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni byang chub sems dpa' yongs su grub pa lung bstan pa la thogs pa mi mnga'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni skad cig gcig tu sems can tham
45b1(phal chen): cad kyi dri ba yongs su dris pa skad cig gcig gis lung bstan pa la thogs pa mi mnga' ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi thogs pa mi mang
45b2(phal chen): ba'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa mthong ma thag tu myur du 'byung ba'i chos rnams te / bcu gang zhe na/ sangs
45b3(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams myur du ngan song dang bral bar 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams
45b4(phal chen): myur du bsod nams yongs su rdzogs pa 'thob par 'gyur ro// / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams myur du dge ba'i rtsa ba la yongs su smin par
45b5(phal chen): 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni ma thong ma thag tu sems can rnams myur du mtho ris su skye ba yongs su dag pa 'thob par 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas ba
45b6(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams ni mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams myur du yid gnyis dang / nem nur yang dag par bsal ba 'thob par 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mthong ma thag tu sems
45b7(phal chen): can rnams myur du byang chub kyi sems bskyed nas phyir mi ldog pa 'thob par 'gyur te/ sems can mos pa yangs pa dang ldan pa/ sangs rgyas kyis 'dul ba las byang chub tu sems ma bskyed
45b8(phal chen): pa'i rnams kyang bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed do// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mthong ma thag tu skyon med par ma 'das pa dmigs pa'i lta ba can gyi sems
46a1(phal chen): / can rnams myur du skyon med pa 'da' ba'i rgyu rab tu 'dzin to// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams myur du 'jig rten pa dang / 'jig rten las 'das
46a2(phal chen): pa'i dbang po rnam par dag par 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams myur du bsgribs pa thams cad byang ba 'thob par 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas
46a3(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams myur du snang ba 'thob cing mi 'jigs pa zhum pa med pa'i spongs pa rab ti rtsom te/ kye rgyal ba'i rdzas ba po de dag na/ sangs
46a4(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa mthong ma thag tu myur du 'byung ba'i chos rnams so// / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas
46a5(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi rjes su dran pa rnam par dag pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sngon gyi sbyor bas kyang / byang chub sems dpa'
46a6(phal chen): rnams kyis rjes su dran par bya ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni spyod pa rnam par dag pas kyang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis rjes su dran par bya ba yin/ 
46a7(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs pas kyang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis rjes su dran par bya ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
46a8(phal chen): ni smon lam chen po yongs su rdzogs pas kyang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis rjes su dran par bya ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni yang dag par bsgrubs pas kyang
46b1(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis rjes su dran par bya ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sngon gyi mthar sangs rgyas kyi tshangs par snang ba la spyad pas kyang byang chub sems dpa'
46b2(phal chen): rnams kyis rjes su dran par bya ba yin sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mngon par 'chang rgya ba'i sgo nas kyang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis rjes su dran par bya ba yin/ sangs
46b3(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni gzugs kyi sku tshang med mu med pas kyang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis rjes su dran par bya ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs
46b4(phal chen): rgyas kyi yul gyis rnam par 'phrul pa chang med mu med pas kyang byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis rjes su dran parabya ba yin sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni
46b5(phal chen): stobs bcu dang mi 'jigs pas kyang / byang chub sem sa dpa' rnams kyis rjes su dran par bya ba yin te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas
46b6(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi rjes su dran pa rnam par dag pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi rnam par sbyong ba / 
46b7(phal chen): bcu gang zhin/ 'di ltar chos kyi dbyings thams cad dang / dus gsum gyi sems can thams cad kyi sems sna tshogs dang / sems dum dang / spong ba dang / g.yo ba'i rgyung thams cad ma lus par thugs
46b8(phal chen): gcig gis thugs su chud pa dang / dus gsum gyi sems can thams cad kyi las dang / las kun nas blangs pa sna tshogs cho mcho dgu rnam pa tha dad pas mngon par 'gro zhing nye bar sogs pa ma
47a1(phal chen): kyang dang / rnam par smin pa tha dad pa ma lus par thugs gcig gis thugs sa chung bdang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyi sems can gyi rigs sna tshogs dang / sems
47a2(phal chen): gyi rigs du ma'i sems can ma lus pa thams cad 'dul ba'i dus ji bzhin du yongs su bstan pa'i tshe 'phrul dang / rjes su bstan pa'i tshe 'phrul dang / rdzu 'phrul gyi tshe 'phrul gyis byin gyis
47a3(phal chen): brlabs yang dag par bstan pa ma lus par thugs su chung ba dang / chos kyi dngongs thams cad dang / phyogs dra ba'i rgyang thams cad dang / 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyud thams cad kyi sem
47a4(phal chen): tsanathams cang kyi sems kyi mtshan bdud ste/ sa sa rgyas bstan pa dang / bye dang / rnam par / pa ma lus par dgasas chung ba dang / 'ji rten gyi
47a5(phal chen): thams cad kyi sems can rnams kyi bsam pa ji lta bang mos pa ji lta ba dang / 'dul ba ji lta ba bzhin du/ rnam pa tha dad pa tshad med par skang cig tu/ sangs rgyas bstan/ 
47a6(phal chen): pa dang rnam par dmigs par bya ba dang / byin gyis brlabs pa ma lus par thugs su chud pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi sems can pha rol gyi bsam pa la/ sangs rgyas kyi
47a7(phal chen): byin gyis brlabs yang dag par bstan pa ma lus par thugs su chud pa dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyi sems can rnams 'dul ba ji lta ba bzhin du nye bar len pa med pa'i sangs rgyas nyid du
47a8(phal chen): 'gyur bar gdams ngag dang / rjes su bstan pas de bzhin gshegs pa 'byung ba bstan pa ma lus par thugs su chud pa dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyi sems can thams cad kyi thams
47b1(phal chen): cad du 'gro ba dang / de dang der 'gro ba'i lam ma lus par thugs kyi skad cig gcig gis thugs su chung ba dang chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyi sems can rnams kyis/ sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa phyogs
47b2(phal chen): thams cad du btang ba'i tshul ma lus par thugs kyi skad cig gcig gis thugs su chung ba dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyi sems can rnams kyi mos pa dang / sems kyi tshad ji lta ba bzhin
47b3(phal chen): du sangs rgyas kyi sku kha dog mu med pa/ dbyibs mtha' yas pa bstan pa ma lus par thugs kyi skad cig gcig gis thugs su chud pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ de bzhin
47b4(phal chen): gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi rnam par spyod pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ de bzhin
47b5(phal chen): gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi ting nge 'dzin tshad med pas ma gyis mi khyab pa rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar sangs
47b6(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/ chos thams cad la rtag tu mnyam par bzhag kyang / chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi sems can rnams la 'di skad cig gcig tu chos ston pa mdzad do// 
47b7(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/ chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi sems can thams cad la mnyam par bzhag kyang skad cig gcig gis/ sems can gyi khams sna tshogs rnam
47b8(phal chen): pa tha dad pa rnams kyang bdag med pa'i mtha' la gnas par yongs su ston to// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/ chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi dus gsum la mnyam par
48a1(phal chen): bzhag kyang thugs kyi rkang cigagacig gi cha shas la'ang mnyam par bzhag cing rnam par sna nga// sa sa rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams na nas kyi dbyis ma lus pa thams sa/ 
48a2(phal chen): phyogs 'byam klas pa'i dra ba thams cad kyi sangs rgyas kyi ning gi rgyung/ rnam pa thams cad la mnyam par bzhag kyang mi zad pa'i zhing gi mtha' la yang bzhugs shing rnam par spong ngo // sangs rgyas
48a3(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi sangs rgyas kyi sku mu med pa la mnyam par bzhag kyang 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyis kyang sangs rgyas kyi skus
48a4(phal chen): tshogs rnam par dmigs par yang dag par ston pa mdzad do// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbying das ma lus pa thams cad su dang / gsung dang thugs kyis
48a5(phal chen): yongs su rgyas par rtag tu mnyam par bzhag kyang / sa mas can thams cad kyi sems 'byung ba'i mdzod sna tshogs la yang mos pa dang yid la byed pa ji lta ba bzhin du rnam
48a6(phal chen): bar spyong ngo // sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi chos thams cad kyi rang bzhin la rtag tu mnyam par bzhag kyang 'dod chags dang bral ba
48a7(phal chen): mtha'i mur thug pa la bzhugs pa yang yongs su mi gtong ngo // sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi 'jig rten thams cad kyi brten pa la rtag tu
48a8(phal chen): par bzhag kyang thugs skad cig gcig gis rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba brjod pa yang rab tu ston to// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/ chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad
48b1(phal chen): kyi 'jig rten pa dang / 'jig rten las 'das pa 'byam klas pa la rtag tu mnyam par bzhag kyang thugs skad cig gcig gis sems can thams cad la sangs rgyas mu med pa bstan pa rnam par dgod pa'i tshul/ 
48b2(phal chen): mu med pas sangs rgyas bstan pa rgyan mi gcod do// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/ chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad du bsgribs pa med par rtag tu mnyam par
48b3(phal chen): bzhag kyang thugs skad cig gcig gis sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad kyang rtogs par thugs su chud cing / sangs rgyas kyi rnam par thar nga mu med pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i mchog brnyes par bzhugs
48b4(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi ting nge 'dzin tshad med bsam
48b5(phal chen): gyis mi khyab pa rnams so// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di ngag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi rnam par thar pa rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ rdul shin tu phra ba
48b6(phal chen): gcig la sangs rgyas skye ba brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa yongs su bstan pa'i rnam par thar pa dang / rdul shin tu phra ba gcig la chos kyi 'khor lo brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med
48b7(phal chen): med pa bskor ba yongs su bstan pa'i rnam par thar pa dang / rdul shin tu phra ba gcig la sems can yongs su smin par bya ba dang / gdul ba brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa yongs su bstan
48b8(phal chen): pa'i rnam par thar pa dang / rdul shin tu phra ba gcig la zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa yongs su bstan pa'i rnam par thar pa dang / rdul shin tu phra ba gcig la 'das pa dang / ma byon
49a1(phal chen): pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas skye ba thams cad yongs su bstan pa'i rnam par thar pa dang / rdul shin tu phra ba gcig la 'das pa dang / ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar/ 
49a2(phal chen): byung ba'i zhing gi rgyud yongs su bstan pa'i rnam par thar pa dang / rdul shin tu phra ba gcig la 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdzu 'phrul dang / 
49a3(phal chen): rnam par 'phrul pa yongs su bstan pa'i rnam par thar pa dang / rdul shin tu phra ba gcig la 'das pa dang / ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sems can gyi khams thams cad yongs su
49a4(phal chen): bstan pa'i rnam par thar pa dang / rdul shin tu phra ba gcig rang la 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas kyi phrin las thams cad yongs su bstan pa'i rnam
49a5(phal chen): par thar pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi rnam par thar pa'o// shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo// sangs rgyas pa la
49a6(phal chen): po che zhes bya ba las sangs rgyas kyi chos bsam gyis mi khyab pa bstan pa'i le'u ste/ sum cu dgu pa'o// / bam po drug cu rtsa bdun pa// / 
49a7(phal chen): de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos mtshan rgya mtsho brjod pa'i don du/ byang chub sems dpa' de dag la smras pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbu la mi chen po'i/ 
49a8(phal chen): mtshan chos kyi rgyan rin po che sna tshogs sum cu rtsa gnyis mnga' bas/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbu de ni 'khor kun nas 'od zer gyi dra bas shin tu 'phro ba'i sprin rab tu 'byung zhing rgyas par 'geng ba ste/ 
49b1(phal chen): de la mi chen po'i mtshan rin po che dang por ngu'i dbu mtshams na/ rin po che sna tshogs thams cad kyi rgyal po las 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du snang ba bkyengs/ dpal gyis yongasu rgyas/ 
49b2(phal chen): shing yan lag dang / nying lag thams cad nas de bzhin gshegs pa'i sprin rnam par bkye ba yongasu 'khyil pa'i grong gi dbyings kyis phyogs thams cad 'od kyis rnam par snang ba zhes bya ba mnga' ba
49b3(phal chen): dang sangs rgyas kyi dbul 'pho ba'i 'od kyi dkyil 'khor glog gi 'phreng ba lta bur 'byung bas/ phyogs mtshams thams cad du de bzhin gshegs pa snying po byang chub tu bzhugs pa ston
49b4(phal chen): cing thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi nam mkha'i sprin kun tu 'dal bas chos kyi dbyings kyi gzhi de bzhin gshegs dpa'i mtshan rin po che'i rgyal po sna tshogs mdzod spu g.yas
49b5(phal chen): phyogs su 'khyil pa'i dbyibs las gser gyi kha dog bzla nga por 'od zer 'bar bar 'jig rten gyi khams su byung ba'i 'od kyis/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad du de bzhinag
49b6(phal chen): ba'i dbu dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyan gsal ba'i 'od kyi sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbul rin po che'i 'od kyi glong g.yas phyogs su yongasu 'khyil ba chos
49b7(phal chen): kyi dbyings thams cad dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du de bzhin gshegs pa'i bsod nams dang / ye shes kyi sgron ma snang ngas 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad du sangs
49b8(phal chen): rgyas kyi sprin rnam par 'dal ba byang chub sems dpa'i mchog rnams la snang bas/ chos kyi dbyings rgyas par khyab pa'i sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan gas
50a1(phal chen): yid du 'ong ba'i sprin sna tshogs kyis/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i khyu mchog gi mthu phyung ba rab tu 'bar bas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'od zer rnam par snga
50a2(phal chen): bar byas pas/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing bsam gyis mi khyab pa snang bar bstan pa'i 'od kyi sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbu la/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che baM
50a3(phal chen): DUr+ya'i 'od zer dang / me tog gi mdog gis chos kyi dbyings thams cad snang bar rnam par 'phrul pa'i sprin/ nor bu rin po che'i rgyal po'i mtshan nyid lta bu'i dbu skra/ rin po che sna tshogs
50a4(phal chen): snang ba'i mtshan nyid kyi 'od chags pas/ phyogs tham sa cad rnam par snang bar byed pas/ sangs rgyas kyi sngon gyi dka' thub dang / dpal gyi ye shes las rnam pa
50a5(phal chen): de lta bur byang ba'i rin po che'i 'od zer rab tu bkye ba'i sprin ce/ sa bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbu la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan dang / rin po che'i 'od
50a6(phal chen): zer g.yas phyogs su 'khyil zhing 'phro bas byang chub sems dpo'i rnam par 'phrul pa/ rin po che'i cod pan gyi 'od de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs kyi rnam par rgyas pas/ 'jig
50a7(phal chen): rten gyi khams thams cad du rin po che 'od tshad med par de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos kyi rang bzhin gyis/ rnam par 'phrul pa yang dag par ston pa'i sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / sangs
50a8(phal chen): rgyas kyi dbu de la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che rnam par 'phrul pas/ nor bu rin po che rgya mtshos bkye ba'i 'od dang / 'od zer dri ma med pa rab tu 'phros pas/ byang chub sems
50b1(phal chen): dpa'i chos bstan pa rgya mtsho rnam par snang bar 'das pa dang / mabyon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi ye shes rgya mtsho shin tu yangs pas chos kyi dbyings kun tu de bzhin/ 
50b2(phal chen): gshegs pa'i gsungs gi sprin 'byung ba zhes bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbu la/ rin po che'i rgyal po sems kyi rgyal po dang / in+d+ra ni la las 'ong bkye ba g.yas
50b3(phal chen): phyogs su 'khyil pas 'jig rten gyi khams dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad du snang ba'i byang chub sems dpa'i 'od 'phro ba sgron ma'i sprin/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi yon tan
50b4(phal chen): rgya mtsho rab tu sgrog pas/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho tha dmas cad dung ro 'byin cing / sangs rgyas kyi stobs so dngas su dag pa rgya mtsho dang / sangs rgyas rgya mtsho 'byin pa
50b5(phal chen): sprin shin tu yangs pa'i 'od ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che'i me tog sna tshogs dang rin po che'i rgyal po bai DUr+ya'i 'od zer rin po che
50b6(phal chen): thams cad kyi 'od zer kun tu 'byung ba'i dra ba/ mngon par 'phags pa las chos kyi lus dang ldan pa'i byang chub sems dpa' 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad dang / phyogs rgya
50b7(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa'i sa yang dag par ston cing sangs rgyas kyi stobs chos kyi dbyings la mngon tu gyur pa rab tu ston par bzhugs pa/ sems can thams cad la yongs su ston pas de bzhin

56b4(phal chen): mched pas 'od kyi sprin rin po che'i 'od du 'phro ba ri rab kyi snying po can zhes bya ba mnga'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i/ tshems mche ba g.yon pa 'og ma la de bzhin gshegs pa'i
56b5(phal chen): mtshan tha dad pa'i mtshan nyid shin tu ston pas spos dang rin po che yid du 'ong ba'i me tog sna tshogs thams cang de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshul sna tshogs kyi 'khor lo dang / 
56b6(phal chen): rin po che thams cad kyi 'od zer rnam par snang ba kun tu 'phro ba'i sgron ma dri ma med pa'i sprin yang dag par bstan pas 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad du rab tu gsal bas/ 
56b7(phal chen): rnam par snang zhing de bzhin gshegs pa gang na seng ge'i khri pad+mo'i snying po can/ dri ma med pa la bzhugs pa'i sprin/ byang chub sems dpa'i rgya mtsho'i dbyings su
56b8(phal chen): rin po che sna tshogs thams cad kyi ri rab kyi mar me rab tu snang ba'i sprin ces bya ba mnga'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshems mche ba g.yon pa gong ma la/ de bzhin gshegs
57a1(phal chen): pa'i mtshan rin po cha gser gyi 'od sna chags kun nas rnam par dag pa/ 'dzam bu chu klung gi rin po che'i rgyud kyi dra ba'i 'khor lo dang rin po che'i me tog shinaH
57a2(phal chen): snang ba'i 'khor lo sna tshogs yongs su 'khyil ba/ chos kyi dbyings su gsung spogs cing / sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa yongs su ston pas
57a3(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' yongs su smin par mdzad cing / nam mkha'i dbyings su rgyan thams cad kyi gzugs brnyan gyi sprin zad mi shes pa kun tu mched par 'gyed pasachos
57a4(phal chen): rgya mtsha rab tu ga pa'i sangs rgyas kyi gsung dang rin po che thams cad kyi tshan du snang ba'i sangs rgyas nam mkha'i dbyings la gsung gi sgra 'byin/ 
57a5(phal chen): pa chos kyi sgron ma'i 'od/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i sprin du snang ba zhes bya ba mnga'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshems kyi mtshams na
57a6(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan tshems kyi mtshams thams cad mtshan gcig par me tog gi mtshan dang rgya mtsho'i sgo'i mtshan gyi sprin rin po che thams cad kyi kha dog tu 'dal ba las
57a7(phal chen): rin po che'i 'od zer rgya mtsho rab tu 'gyed cing / bzhang mo 'dzum pas/ sangs rgyas kyi 'od nor bu rin po che'i 'od du 'phro ba g.yas phyogs su 'khyil zhing / chos kyi dbyings
57a8(phal chen): rgyas par khyab par rin po che'i 'od zer rgya mtsho khongs su chud pa'i snying po can gyis/ sangs rgyas kyi rnams kyi mtshams thams cad rgyas par gang bas/ skad cig tu 'od kyis rgyas
57b1(phal chen): par kun tu rgyu ba'i 'od zer/ sangs rgyas kyi gsung gi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho kun tu 'gyed pa'i sprin snang ba zhes bya ba mnga'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i spros la/ de bzhin gshegs
57b2(phal chen): ba'i mtshan 'dzam bu chu klung gi gser dang / pad+mo'i mdog dang / 'od ltar snang ba/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad du mdangs rab tu snang bas dpal phun sum tshogs pa rin
57b3(phal chen): po che thams cad kyi 'od zer dang / mdangs kyi kun tu khyab par rnam par snang zhing / gser dang / pad+mo'i mdog yongs su dag pas kun tu sbyangs pas/ rin po che thams cad kyi
57b4(phal chen): mdangs dang / mdog tu snang ba mnga'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i mgur la/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan dung gi mgur/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi
57b5(phal chen): 'od lam me/ lam mer yongs su snang bas mdog shi na tu gsal zhing / gzhi thams cad rin po che'i rgya la pos rnam par snang bar byas pas/ phyogs thams
57b6(phal chen): cad du rnam par gsal ba'i 'od zer rab tu 'gyed cing / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi snang bar mdzad pa'i sprin ces bya ba mnga'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku phrag pa g.yas
57b7(phal chen): pa la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che thams cad kyi 'od dang / gser gyi kha dog rab tu 'phel bas/ pad+ma'i mdog rnam par snang ba dang / rin po che'i 'od kyi dra
57b8(phal chen): ba rab tu snang ste/ kun tu gsal bar chos kyi dbyings snang bar mdzad cing / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad khongs su chud pa'i sprin rab tu snang bas sangs rgyas rab tu
58a1(phal chen): mang po thams cad snying por byas pa/ rin po che thams cad kyi gzhi dang ldan pa'i sbyin ces bya ba mnga'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku phrag pa'i dbus na/ 
58a2(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan shin tu 'phags shing / yongs su rgyal la/ 'dzam bu chu klung gi gser gyi 'od dang / mdog yongs su dag pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor lo
58a3(phal chen): rab tu snang bas chos kyi dbyings snang bar rin po che'i rgyal po mchog tu kun tu snang ba'i sprin ces bya ba mnga'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku phrag pa g.yon pa la/ sangs rgyas kyi dbu'i
58a4(phal chen): mdzod spu'i dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho'i gzhi las rin po che 'od zer gyi dra ba sna tshogs shin tu bsgrubs pa/ 'dzam bu chu klung gi gser dang / pad+mo'i mdog ltar gsal zhing bzang
58a5(phal chen): ba rab tu bkye bas chos kyi dbyings dang 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du rnam par 'phrul pa'i 'od ston cing / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi mdzod
58a6(phal chen): spu rin po che'i sprin gyi 'od rab tu snang ba bkye bas dpal rab tu 'bar zhing / chos kyi dbyings snang bar mdzad pa'i sprin ces bya ba mnga'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku phrag pa
58a7(phal chen): g.yas pa'i lhun la/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan/ mtshan nyid rnam par phye ba rin po che'i go cha/ 'dzam bu chu klung gi gser lta bu/ dpal thams cad kyis rgyas
58a8(phal chen): pas chos kyi dbyings kyi sangs rgyas thams cad kyi 'od kyi dbyings rgya mtsho'i 'od rnam par snang b.rin po che'i me tog spos kyi 'od 'phro bas zhing rgya mtsho thams cad rgyan
58b1(phal chen): rnam par byengs brnyan te/ kun tu snang ba'i sbyin ces bya ba mngag// de bzhin gshegs pa'i su phrag pa g.yon pa'i rdzun la/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan/ sman ma'i 'oda'adra ba'i \u0f7f/ 
58b2(phal chen): po'i sprin chos kyi dbyings kun tu rab tu mched pas byang chub sems dpa'i dge 'dun yongs su khyab cing / chos kyi dbyings kyi gzhi'i rgyan du gyur par kun tu mched cing snang ba'i dbyings kyi sprin
58b3(phal chen): ces bya ba mnga'o// sangs rgyas kyi thugs ka'i dpal gyi be'u la/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan/ mtshan nyid rgya mtshos/ kun tu brgyan pas rab tu 'jam pa'i gzhi rin po che thams cad
58b4(phal chen): kyi mdog lta bur snang ba/ rin po che sna tshogs kyi tshad du 'od zer gyi dkyil 'khor kun tu 'khyil pas yongasu dag cing / chos rgya mtsho ga sung dbyangs dang ldan pa/ rin po
58b5(phal chen): tshe'i me tog shin tu rgyas pas rnam par brgyan te/ rin/ kho che'i 'od zer gyi mtshan gyi dbyings rgya mtsho la gnas/ pa'i dpal rgya mtsho kun gyi gzhung gi sprin ces bya ba mnga'o// 
58b6(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa'i dpal gyi be'u'i g.yas phyogs mngab chags na de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan chos kyi dbyangs rnam par dag pa'i 'khor lo snang ba'i gzhi'i rgyan rin po
58b7(phal chen): che'i mig 'phrul gyi 'khor lo rnam par dag pa las sangs rgyas kyi sprin gyi lhun/ dri ma med pas rab tu snang zhing / phyogs thams cad kyi chos kyi dbyings su 'ong rnam par snang ba/ dpal
58b8(phal chen): gyi be'u dang / mtshams sbyor ba rab tu ston pa'i sprin ces bya ba mnga'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i dpal gyi be'u'i 'dab chags g.yon phyogs na/ byang chub sems dpa'i rin po che'i cong ngan
59a1(phal chen): la snang ba shin du 'angags pa'i sprin gyi ldan/ drim med bas thams cad du/ sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa yang dag par ston cing / chos rgya mchatsha'i stong parab tu sbyan ngas/ 
59a2(phal chen): 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad rab tu ston pa'i sprin ces bya ba mnga'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i dpal gyi be'u'i g.yas
59a3(phal chen): phyogs kyi 'og rol 'dab chags na/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che'i me tog dang / rin po che'i mdzod spus rab tu brgyan pa'i rin po che'i 'khor lo// rin po che'i 'od 'phro ba'i sgron ma/ 
59a4(phal chen): dri ma med pa/ pad+mo'i dbyibs 'jig rten gyi khams su ston pas / me tog rgyas pa'i sprin ces bya ba mnga'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i dpal gyi be'u'i g.yon phyogs kyi 'og rol gyi 'dang / 
59a5(phal chen): chags na/ rin po che thams cad kyi 'od sems kyi rgyal po/ 'i snying po can rin po che'i rgyal po'i 'od zer gyi 'khor lo dang 'od rab tu bkye bas/ kun tu dri ma med pa'i
59a6(phal chen): mtsho shin tu 'phags pa'i khongs su sangs rgyas kyi tshul thams cad rab tu snang ba'i rin po che'i phung po ma lus par chung ba'i snying po can/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad du gser rab tu 'bar ba'i sprin ces bya ba
59a7(phal chen): mnga'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i dpal gyi be'u'i rtse mo la/ nam mkha'i dbyings su rin po che'i sgron ma spos rin po che'i rgyal po lus thams cad la snying po byang chub kyi 'od zer rab tu 'bar zhing
59a8(phal chen): bai DUr+ya'i dkyil 'khor gyi sgron ma spos kyi phreng bas phyogs yangs pa thams cad rgyas par 'gengs shing kun tu g.yas phyogs su 'khyil ba/ sangs rgyas kyi dpal gyi be'u rgya mtsho'i sprin ces bya ba/ 
59b1(phal chen): mnga'o// de'i 'og na rjes su 'gro ba'i dpal gyi be'u gnyis pa yod pa'i dbus na/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan/ mtshan nyid kyi pad+mo'i gzhi la ze ba byang chub sems dpa' g.yas phyogs su
59b2(phal chen): 'khor bar 'khod pa'i rab tu snang bas shin tu 'phags shing yongs su dag la/ chos kyi dbyings rgya mtshor gsung sgrog pa'i sangs rgyas kyi 'od zer gyi phung po'i snying po can rin po che'i rgyal
59b3(phal chen): pos shin tu brgyan pa/ rin po che'i 'od rab tu 'bar bas 'od zer rnam par snang ba'i 'od kyi lhun dang ldan pa'i sprin ces bya ba mnga'o// rjes su 'gro ba'i dpal gyi be'u gsum pa la
59b4(phal chen): bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan mtshan rgya mtshos yongs su gang ba'i ri na po che rgya mtsho'i nang na/ zhing thams cad gzugs pan na du 'khor bar ston cing / byang chub sems dpa' sprin gzhan/ 
59b5(phal chen): dang gzhan mngon par phyung bas chos kyi dbyings rnam par snang / ba'i sprin kun tu ston pa'i 'od kyi sprin ces bya ba mnga'o// // rjes su 'gro ba'i dpal gyi de'u bzhi pa la de bzhin gshegs
59b6(phal chen): pa'i mtshan mtshan nyid kyi rnam pa rgya mtshos chos kyi dbyings thams cad du de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par snang ba dang / 'jig rten gyi khams dang / rgyan thams cad snang bas 'jig rten
59b7(phal chen): gyi khams rgya mtshor 'od rab tu bkye ba'i 'od zer snang ba phun sum tshogs pas rgyas par snang ba'i 'od zer gyi sprin rin po che'i rgyal po'i 'khor lo g.yas phyogs su 'khyil pa'i nyi ma rnam par snang ba
59b8(phal chen): dang dreng ba kun tu byung zhing 'phags pa'i sprin ces bya ba mnga'o// dpal gyi be'u de'i 'og rol na chos thams cad kyi sgron ma'i dbyings dri ma med pa spos kyi me tog gi 'od zer rab tu snang ba/ 
60a1(phal chen): sangs rgyas rgya mtsho thams cad kyi thugs su 'dus pa de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan/ rgya mtsho las chos kyi dbyings thams cad du/ chos kyi 'khor lo'i glong thams cad kyi/ gsung
60a2(phal chen): gi dbyangs kyi sprin 'byin pa zhes bya ba mnga'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i dpal gyi be'u bcu pa la/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa'i phyogs
60a3(phal chen): thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi spyod pas mthu phyung zhing sangs rgyas kyi 'od yongasu dag pa dang / dri ma med pa 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyi ye shes
60a4(phal chen): rgya mtsho'i glong yongs su dag pa thams cad kyis zhing rgya mtsho rab tu brgyan cing klubs te/ rnam par 'god pa'i sprin ces bya ba mnga'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i phyag gi mthil la/ de
