259a5(phal chen): bzhin dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi sku dang gcig tu/ 'dres pas ye shes kyi rang bzhin dang / skye ba'i mched thams cad las 'das pasachos kyi rang bzhin
259a6(phal chen): dang / thams cad sgo yongasu ston pas/ thams cad kyi rang bzhin dang / rdzu 'phrul dang / rnam par 'phrul pa thams cad yongasu ston pas/ rdzu 'phrul gyi rang bzhin dang
259a7(phal chen): nam 'dod pa'i dus su mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bas byang chub kyi rang bzhin no// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rang bzhin te/ 
259a8(phal chen): dag la gnas shing byang chub sems dpa' rnams de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes chen po'i rang bzhin bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ 
259b1(phal chen): chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ngag ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar sems can thams cad bde bar byed pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ngag ni 'jam pa'o// sems can
259b2(phal chen): thams cad kyi sems sim par byed pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ngag ni snyan pa'o// yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du go bar byed pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi/ 
259b3(phal chen): ngag ni mi rdzun pa'o// rmi lam na yang log par mi smra bas/ byang chub sems dpa'i ngag ni bden pa'i rjesu 'brang ba'o// brgya byin dang / tshangs pa dang / 'jig rten gyi
259b4(phal chen): mgon po thams cad zil gyis gnon pas byang chub/ sems dpa' rnams kyi ngag ni rgya che ba'o// cho das kyi rang bzhin ston pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams
259b5(phal chen): kyi ngag ni zab mo'i dbyangasu sgrog pa'o// chos bstan pa/ mas cad mi zad pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dag ni stong pa dang ldan pa'o// sgra ji lta ba bzhin du
259b6(phal chen): khong du chud par byed pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ngag ni shin tu gsal ba'o// dus dang las dang rnam par smin pa ji lta ba bzhin du yongs su ston pas/ byang chub
259b7(phal chen): sems dpa' rnams kyi ngag ni rnam pa tha dad pa'o// bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du rnam par spyod pa la 'jug par byed pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ngag ni 'gro ba thams
259b8(phal chen): cad la bgro ba'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ngag ste/ de dag la gnas shing byang chub sems dpa' rnams de bzhin gshegs pa'i
260a1(phal chen): gsung bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go/ kye rgyal ba'i sras/ byang chub sems dpa'i gi de yang las rnam par dag pa bcus yongasu sbyangs pa yin
260a2(phal chen): bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung la mos pa yongasu dag pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i tshig sngon ma thos pa la mngon par mos pa yong su dag pa dang
260a3(phal chen): 'gro ba thams cad kyi yid du mi 'ong ba'i tshig yongasu spangs pas/ yongasu dag pa dang / sngon gyi mthar ngag nyes pa bzhi dang bral bas yongasu dag pa dang / dga' ba dang mos pa
260a4(phal chen): chen pos de bzhin gshegs pa mngon du bstod pas yo dang su dag pa dang / sgra chen pos de bzhin gsheg/ ngas pa mchod par 'os pa/ yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du
260a5(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi yon tan dang / legs pa brjod pas yongasu dag pa dang / bsam pa thag pas sems can gzhan la chos kyi sbyin pas bsdud pas yongasu dag pa
260a6(phal chen): dang klu'i dbyangs dang / rol mo brdung ba dang / dkrol ba'i dbyangs kyis de bzhin gshegs pa la mngon par bstod pas yong su dag pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
260a7(phal chen): rnams las mngon sum du chos thos nas/ rang gi lus 'bul bas yongasu dag pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i chos smra ba thams cad las chos thos nas/ rim gro bya ba'i phyir/ 
260a8(phal chen): bdag 'bul zhing snying thag pa nas yongasu gtong bas yongasu dag pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras/ byang chub sems dpa'i ngag ni las rnam par dag pa bcu po de dag gis shin tu
260b1(phal chen): sbyangs par 'byung ngo // kye rgyal ba'i sras/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ngag de ltar yongs su sbyangs pa de yang yongasu 'dzin pa bcus yongasu bzung bar 'byung ste/ bcu gang
260b2(phal chen): zhe na/ 'di ltar lha'i dbang po la sogs pa lha thams cad kyis yongasu bzung bar 'byung ba yin/ klu'i dbang po dang / gnod sbyin gyi dbang po dang / dri za'i dbang po dang / lha ma yin/ 
260b3(phal chen): gyi dbang po dang / na mkha' lding gi dbang po dang / mi'am ci'i dbang po dang / lto 'phye chen po'i dbang po dang / tshangs pa'i dbang po la sogs pa tshangs pa'i ris su gtogs
260b4(phal chen): pa'i lha thams cad kyis yongs su bzung bar 'byung ba yin// de bzhin gshegs pa chos kyi dbang po la sogs dpa chos smra ba thams cad kyis yongasu bzung bar 'byung ba yin/ 
260b5(phal chen): te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras/ byang chub sems dpa'i ngag ni yongasu 'dzin pa bcu po de dag gis shin tu bzung ba 'byung // kye rgyal ba'i sras/ byang chub sems dpa'i
260b6(phal chen): ngag de ltar shin tu bzung bar 'byung ba de yang dgos pa bcu yongasu grub par byed de/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar sems can gyi khams mngon par dga' bar byed do// 'jig rten gyi
260b7(phal chen): kham su go bar byed do// dbang po'i khams la 'jug par byed do// mos pa'i khams rnam par dag par byed do// nyon mongs pa'i khams sel bar byed do// bag chags
260b8(phal chen): kyi khams spong bar byed do// bsam pa'i khams spyod par byed do// lhag pa'i bsam pa'i khams rnam par 'phel bar byed do// chos kyi khams rgyas par byed do// mya ngan
261a1(phal chen): las 'das pa'i khams yang dag par rtogs par byed de/ dgos pa bcu po de dag yong su sgrub pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems
261a2(phal chen): dpa' rnams kyi sems te/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'gro ba thams cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba yang dag par 'dzin cing sbyin pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sems ni sa lta bu'o// 
261a3(phal chen): sangs rgyas thams cad kyi ye shes rgya chen po'i rgya mtsho mtha' dang dbus med pa la zhugs pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sems ni rgya mtsho lta bu'o// 'jig rten las 'das/ 
261a4(phal chen): pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba shin tu mtho ba la 'gro ba thams cad rab tu dgod pa'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa'i sa dmas ni ri bo chen po lta bu'o// kun nas nyon mongs pa med
261a5(phal chen): cing bsam pa dag pa dang ldan pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sems ni nor bu rin po che lta bu'o// / chos thams cad la rab tu rno bas/ byang chub sems dpa
261a6(phal chen): rnams kyi sems ni rdo rje lta bu'o// bdud dang mu stegs can gzhan dang phas kyi rgol ba thams cad kyis mi skul bas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sems ni ro'i rgyal po
261a7(phal chen): rdo rje'i khor yug shin tu brtan zhing mi shigs pa lta bu'o// 'jig rten gyi chos thams cad kyis mi gos pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sems ni pad+mo lta bu'o// bskal
261a8(phal chen): pa thams cad du 'byung ba dang / mthong bar dka' bas byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sems ni me tog u dum par lta bu'o// 'gro ba thams cad kyi ma rig pa'i mun pa mun nag
261b1(phal chen): dang / rab rab kyi rgyus pa sel ba'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sems ni nyi ma lta bu'o// 'gro ba thams cad kyis brjod du med pa'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa'
261b2(phal chen): rnams kyi sems ni bar snang lta bu'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sems te/ de dag la gnas shing / byang chub sems dpa' rnams
261b3(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa'i thugs rgya chen po yongasu dag pa bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go// kye rgyal ba'i sras po bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sems
261b4(phal chen): bskyed pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar 'gro ba thams cad rab tu dgrol bar bya'o zhes byang chub sems dpa' sems bskyed do// sems can thams cad kyi nyan
261b5(phal chen): mongs pa bsal bar bya'o zhes byang chub sems dpa' ste/ mas bskyed do// bag chags kyi mtshams 'brel ba thams cad spang bar bya'o zhes byang chub sems dpa' sas/ 
261b6(phal chen): bskyed// chos thams cad la the tsom med pa thob par bya'o zhes byang chub sems dpa' sems bskyed do// sems can thams cad kyi sdug bsngal gyi phung po rab tu zhi bar bya'o zhes byang chub
261b7(phal chen): sems dpa' sems bskyed do// ngan song dang mi khom pa thams cad gcad par bya'o zhes byang chub sems dpa' sems bskyed do// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad mnyes par
261b8(phal chen): bya'o zhes byang chub sems dpa' sems bskyed do// byang chub sems dpa'i bslab pa thams cad la nan tan du bya'o zhes byang chub sems dpa' sems bskyed do// skra'i sbubs
262a1(phal chen): 'jug pa thams cad kyang ma lus par 'gro ba thams cad du sangs rgyas thams cad byang chub tu 'tshang rgya ba bstan par bya'o zhes byang chub sems dpa' sems bskyed
262a2(phal chen): do/ 'gro ba ma lus pa thams cad kyi bsam pa dang / dbang po rab tu rtogs pas 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du grags par bya bar chos kyi rnga bla na med pa brdung bar bya'o zhes byang
262a3(phal chen): chub sems dpa' sems bskyed do// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sems bskyed pa ste// de dag la gnas shing byang chub sems dpa' rnams
262a4(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa'i thugs rgya chen po'i phrin las bla na med brtsom par 'gyur ba dag go// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sems
262a5(phal chen): kyis rgyas par dgang ba ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta/ ra sems shin tu yangs pa dang ldan pas/ nam mkha'i dbyings thams cad rgyas par dgang ba dang / mtha'
262a6(phal chen): dang dbus med pa khong du chud pas chos kyi dbyings thams cad rgyas par dgang ba dang / skad cig gcig tu 'dzud pas dus gsum thams cad rgyas par dgang ba dang / gshegs pa dang / 
262a7(phal chen): skye ba dang / 'byung ba dang / rnam par 'tshang rgya ba dang / chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba dang / mya ngan las 'das pa chen po mngon sum du shes pas/ sangs rgyas skye ba thams cad du rgyas
262a8(phal chen): par dgang ba dang / bag chags dang dbang po na mkha' lta bur khong du chud pas/ sems can gyi khams thams cad du rgyas par dgang ba dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad khong du chud pa'i
262b1(phal chen): ye shes dang ldan pas/ mig yor lta bu'i ye shes kyis rgyas par dgang ba dang / sgyu ma'i dra ba rnam pa tha dad pa lta bur khong du chud pas/ mtha' dang dbus med pa rgyas par dgang ba
262b2(phal chen): dang / rang bzhin mi dmigs pas mi skye bar rgyas par dgang ba dang / rang gi sems dang gzhan gyi sems la thogs pa med pas/ chags pa med par rgyas par dgang ba dang
262b3(phal chen): sems bskyed pa thams cad la mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa yongasu ston pas/ dbang gis rgyas par dgang ba'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems
262b4(phal chen): dpa' rnams kyi sems kyis rgyas par dgang ba ste/ de da ga la gnas shing byang chub sems dpa' rnams sa/ des rgyas kyi chos thams cad kyis rgyas par dgang ba mtha' dang
262b5(phal chen): dbus med pa'i rgyan bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chubabasems dpa' rnams kyi dbang po ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 
262b6(phal chen): 'di ltar sangs rgyas thams cad mthong bar dad pa phyir ldog pa med pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dbang po ni dga' bar byed pa'o// sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad mngon
262b7(phal chen): par 'tshang rgya bar byed pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dbang po ni mngon par mos pa'o// bya ba thams cad la thogs pa med pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dbang
262b8(phal chen): po ni phyir mi ldog pa'o// byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad rgyun mi gcod pa'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dbang po ni gnas pa'o// shes rab kyi pha rol tu
263a1(phal chen): phyin pa'i tshul khong du chud pa'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dbang po ni shin tu phra ba'o// sems can thams cad kyi dgos pa yongasu grub par byed
263a2(phal chen): pa'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dbang po ni rgyun mi 'chad do// chos thams cad la rab tu rno ba'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dbang po ni rdo rje lta bu'o// 
263a3(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi yul la snang ba 'thob pa'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dbang po ni rdo rje'i 'od 'phro ba ltar snang bar byed pa'o// de bzhin gshegs
263a4(phal chen): pa thams cad kyi sku dang / lus gcig tu gyur pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dbang po ni tha mi dang dpa'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs kyi rjesu zhugs
263a5(phal chen): pa'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dbang po/ ni chags pa med pa'i mthar phyin pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams
263a6(phal chen): kyi dbang po ste/ de dag la gnas shing / byang chub sems dpa' rnams de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbang po rgya chen po yongasu rdzogs pa bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go/ kye
263a7(phal chen): rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi bsam pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi bsam pa 'jig rten gyi chos
263a8(phal chen): thams cad kyis ma gos pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi bsamam pa nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi yid la bya ba dang ma 'dres pa dang / byang chub sems
263b1(phal chen): dpa' rnams kyi bsam pa sangs rgyas kyi byang chub kyi rjesu song ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi bsam pa thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes 'byung ba'i lam dang 'thun pa dang / 
263b2(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi bsam pa bdud dang / mu stegs can gzhan dang / mu stegs spyod pa'i rgol ba thams cad kyis mi 'phrogs pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams/ 
263b3(phal chen): kyi bsam pa de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor gyis rnam par drag pas/ kun nas nyon mongs pa med pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi bsam
263b4(phal chen): pa chos ji skad du thos pa yongasu mi gtong bas shin tu zi dran par yang dag par 'dzin pa dang / byang chub sem ngas dpa' rnams kyi bsam pa skye ba'i skye mched thams cad
263b5(phal chen): kyis ma gos pas yongasu nyams pa med pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi bsam pa ye shes phra ba la zhugs pa'i phyir zab pa dang / byang chub sems
263b6(phal chen): dpa' rnams kyi bsam pa sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la shin tu brtson pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag no/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi bsam pa ste/ 
263b7(phal chen): dag la gnas shing byang chub sems dpa' rnams thams cad mkhyen pa'i dgongs pa bla na med pa yongasu rdzogs par 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni// 
263b8(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lhag pa'i bsam pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lhag pa'i bsam pa dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad bsags pa
264a1(phal chen): la phyir mi ldog par dbang bsgyur ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lhag pa'i bsam pa de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dgongs pa'i tshul bstan pa
264a2(phal chen): la nem nur med pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lhag pa'i bsam pa smon lam dang spyod pa chen po'i rgyun yongasu 'dzin pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lhag pa'i
264a3(phal chen): bsam pa sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la 'jug par bya ba la phul du phyin pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lhag pa'i bas pa sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la dbang bsgyur bas
264a4(phal chen): mngon sum du gyur pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams/ dkyi lhag pa'i bsam pa chos sna tshogs kyi tshul la rab tu zhugs pas rgya che ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams
264a5(phal chen): kyi lhag pa'i bsam pa brtsams pa thams cad mthar phyin par byed pas gtso bor gyur pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lhag pa'i bsam pa ting nge 'dzin dang snyoms
264a6(phal chen): par 'jug pa dang / rnam par 'phrul pa'i rgyan thams cad la dbang bsgyur ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lhag pa'i bsam pa sngon gyi smon lam gyis yongasu gzung bas shin
264a7(phal chen): tu brtan pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lhag pa'i bsam pa sems can thams cad yongasu smin par bya ba dang / gdul ba la rgyun mi 'chad pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de/ 
264a8(phal chen): dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lhag pa'i bsam pa ste/ de dag la gnas shing / byang chub sems dpa' rnams sangs rgyas thams cad kyi lhag pa'i dgongs pa bla na med pa yos
264b1(phal chen): su dag pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go// / dam po brgyad cu rtsa gcig pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'ang dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sbyor
264b2(phal chen): ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar rnam par smin pa la re ba med par bdog pa thams cad yongs su gtong bas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sbyin pa'i sbyor ba dang / gzhan
264b3(phal chen): la brnyas pa med pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi tshul khrims dang bslab pa dang / sbyangs pa'i yon tan dang / sdom pa dang / brtul zhugs dang / dka' thub thams
264b4(phal chen): cad du yi dam bcas pa la nan tan byed pa'i sbyor ba dang / bdag dang pha rol gyi 'du shes med pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi gnod sems kyi thab dang ga
264b5(phal chen): pa thams cad rna la gzin cing / sems can gyis ngan du byas pa thams cad bzod pa'i sbyor ba dang / lus dang ngag dang sems yang dag par skul pas brtsams
264b6(phal chen): pa thams cad mthar phyin par byed pa'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi brtson 'grus brtsams pa thams cad las phyir mi ldog pa'i sbyor ba dang / 'dod pa 'khrug
264b7(phal chen): ba dang / nyon mongs pa'i g.yog 'khor yongasu spong bas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi bsam gtan dang / rnam par thar pa dang / ting 'dzin dang / snyoms par 'jug
264b8(phal chen): pa dang / mngon par shes pa thams cad mngon par sgrub pa'i sbyor ba dang / bsod nams bsags pa thams cad la skyo ba med pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi shes
265a1(phal chen): rab kyi nan tan gyi sbyor ba dang / sems can med pa la zhugs pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi byams pa chen po'i sbyor ba dang / chos thams cad rang
265a2(phal chen): bzhin gyis dben pa'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi 'gro ba thams cad kyi sdug bsngal rang gi lus kyis len pa'i snying rje chen po las phyir mi ldog pa'i sbyor ba dang
265a3(phal chen): chags pa med par khong du chud pas 'gro ba thams cad yang dag par ston pa'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu rnam par 'tshang rgya ba'i
265a4(phal chen): sbyor ba dang / sems can gzhan gyi rgyud du phyin par bye/ dad pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi chos dkyi 'khor lo bskor ba las phyir mi ldog pa'i sbyor ba'o// 
265a5(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sbyor ba ste/ de dag la gnas shing byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs
265a6(phal chen): pa'i ye shes chen po'i sbyor ba bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi mos pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 
265a7(phal chen): 'di ltar bsgrub par dga' ba'i dge ba'i rtsa ba sbyor bas/ rlabs po che'i mos pa dang / rgyan sna tshogs mngon par sgrub pas sna tshogs kyi mos pa dang / yid zhum pa med pas rgya chen
265a8(phal chen): po'i mos pa dang / chos zab mo'i tshul la zhugs pas zhi bar byed pa'i mos pa dang / sems rgya chen po skyed pas yangs pa'i mos pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyi mthu
265b1(phal chen): dang / shugs su ldan pas rang gis skabs phye ba'i mos pa dang / bdud kyi las thams cad rab tu 'joms pas mi 'phrogs pa'i mos pa dang / las kyi rnam par smin pa la
265b2(phal chen): gcig tu nges pas shin tu gdon mi zab pa'i mos pa dang / ci 'dod pa'i cho 'phrul yongasu ston pas/ mngon du gyur pa'i mos pa dang / stobs dang mi ldan pa med pa'i phyir/ 
265b3(phal chen): dus gang du 'dod par byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bas/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyis lung bstan pa yang dag par nod pa'i mos pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po
265b4(phal chen): de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi mos pa ste/ de dag la gnas shing / byang chub sems dpa'// rnams de bzhin gshegs pa'i mos pa bla na med pa 'thob
265b5(phal chen): par 'gyur ba dag go/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di ga/ ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi 'jig rten gyi khamasu mos pa la 'jug pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 
265b6(phal chen): 'di ltar 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad 'jig rten gyi khams gcig tu mos pa la 'jug pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams gcig 'jig rten gyi khams thams
265b7(phal chen): cad du mos pa la 'jug pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad pad+mo'i gdan gcig la bzhugs pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i skus yongasu khyab par mos pa la 'jug pa dang / 'jig
265b8(phal chen): rten gyi khams thams cad na mkha'i rang bzhin du yang dag par bstan par mos pa la 'jug pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad sangs rgyas kyi rgyan gyis brgyan par mos pa la 'du/ 
266a1(phal chen): pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad byang chub sems dpa'i lus kyis rgyas par gang bar mos pa la 'jug pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad
266a2(phal chen): skra'i sbubs gcig tu dgod par mos pa la 'jug pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad sems can gcig gi lus kyi rgyud kyi rjesu 'brang bar mos pa la 'jug pa dang / 'jig
266a3(phal chen): rten gyi khams thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa gcig gi byang chub kyi shing dang / de bzhin gshegs pa gcig gi snying po byang chub kyis yongasu rgyas par gang bar mos pa la 'jug pa
266a4(phal chen): dang 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du sgra'i dbyangs gcig gis go bar bya ba dang / sems can gyi kham/ sa thams cad kyi sgra skad rnam pa tha dad pa la 'jug pas
266a5(phal chen): tshom par bya bar mos pa la 'jug pa'o// kye rgyal ba sras bcu po de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi 'jig rten gyi khamasu mos pa la 'jug pa ste/ de dag
266a6(phal chen): la gnas shing / byang chub sems dpa' rnams de bzhin gshegs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing la mos pa bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni
266a7(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sems can gyi khamasu mos pa la 'jug pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar sems can gyi khams thams cad rang bzhin gyis lus med par mos pa la
266a8(phal chen): 'jug pa dang / sems can gyi khams thams cad sems can gcig gi lus kyi rgyud du 'dus par mos pa la 'jug pa dang / sems can gyi khams thams cad byang chub sems dpa'
266b1(phal chen): khong du 'dus par mos pa la 'jug pa dang / sems can gyi khams thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa'i skur 'dus par mos pa la 'jug pa dang / sems can gyi khams thams cad du ses
266b2(phal chen): can gcig gi lus yong su zhugs par gyur par mos pa la 'jug pa dang / sems can gyi khams thad sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi snod du mos pa la 'jug pa dang / sems can gyi khams thams
266b3(phal chen): cad brgya byin dang / tshangs pa dang / 'jig rten gyi mgon po dang / ci 'dod pa dang / gar mos pa'i gzugs dang / kha dog dang / cha byad du mngon par blta bar mos pa la
266b4(phal chen): 'jug pa dang / sems can gyi khams thams cad nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi gzugs dang / kha dog dang / cha byad du yongasu bstan par mos pa la 'jug
266b5(phal chen): pa dang sems can gyi khams thams cad byang chub se mas dpa'i yon tan gyis yongasu brgyan par byin gyis brlab cing / yongasu bstan par mos pa la 'jug pa
266b6(phal chen): dang / sems can gyi khams thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku gzugs dang / mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po dang / gzugs kyi sku sna tshogs kyi spyod lam dang tshul dang / spyod
266b7(phal chen): pa yongasu bstan cing / gzhan gyis rig par bya bar mos pa la 'jug pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sems can gyi khams mos pa
266b8(phal chen): la 'jug pa ste/ de dag la gnas shing / byang chub sems dpa' rnams de bzhin gshegs pa'i dgyes pa dang / khyu mchog gi mthu phyung ba bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba
267a1(phal chen): dgag/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi bag chags te/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar byang chub kyi sems kyi bag chags dang / 
267a2(phal chen): dge ba'i rtsa ba'i bag chags dang / sems can yong su smin par bya ba'i bag chags dang / sangs rgyas lta ba'i bag chags dang / 'jig rten gyi khams yong su dag par skye ba'i bag chags
267a3(phal chen): dang spong ba'i bag chags dang / smon lam gyi bag chags dang / pha rol tu phyin pa'i bag chags dang / chos mnyam pa nyid nges par rtogs pa'i bag chags dang / spyod pa rnam patha
267a4(phal chen): dang pa'i bag chag so// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po deng dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi bag chag ngas te/ de dag la gnas shing / byang chub sems dpa'
267a5(phal chen): rnams nyon mongs pa'i bag chags ma lus par spangs nas de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes chen pos bag chag sa thugasu chud pa bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go/ 
267a6(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi nye bar len pa ste/ nye bar len pa de dag gis/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa rgyun mi gcod pa'o// ba
267a7(phal chen): gang zhe na/ 'di ltar yongasu smin pa'i mthar phyin par bya ba'i phyir/ sems can gyi khams nye bar len pa dang / lhag ma med par yong su dag par bya ba'i phyir/ 'jig rten gyi
267a8(phal chen): khams nye bar len pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pas mnyes par bya ba'i phyir/ de bzhin gshegs pa nye bar len pa dang / mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po dang / sangs rgyas kyi
267b1(phal chen): yon tan yang dag par bsdu ba'i phyir/ dge ba'i rtsa ba nye bar len pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi sdug bsngal gyi phung ba nye bar blangs te rab tu zhi bar bya ba'i phyir/ snying rje chen po
267b2(phal chen): bar len pa dang / sems can thams cad thams cad mkhyen pa'i bde ba la rab tu dgod pa'i phyir/ byams pa chen po nye bar len pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i rgyan yang dag par
267b3(phal chen): bsdu ba'i phyir/ pha rol tu phyin pa nye bar len pa dang / sgo thams cad yongs su bstan pa'i phyir/ thabs mkhas pa nye bar len pa dang / chags pa med pa'i ye shes kyi phyir/ 
267b4(phal chen): byang chub nye bar len pa dang / mdor na thams cad mngon/ sum du shes pas/ mngon par shes par bya ba'i phyi ra/ byang chub sems dpa' chos thams cad nye bar len
267b5(phal chen): pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ bya chub sems dpa' rnams kyi nye bar len pa ste/ nye len pa de dag gos byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa rgyun mi
267b6(phal chen): gcod cing / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi nye bar len pa med pa bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa'
267b7(phal chen): rnams kyi nan tan te/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar pha rol tu phyin pa'i nan tan dang / bslab pa'i nan tan dang / ye shes kyi nan tan dang / don gyi nan tan dang / chos kyi nan
267b8(phal chen): tan dang / mngon par bsgrub pa'i nan tan dang / yang dag par bstan pa'i nan tan dang / spyod pas mi skyo ba'i nan tan dang / mngon par rdzogs par byang chub par bya ba'i nan tan/ 
268a1(phal chen): dang / chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba'i nan tan no// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu pa de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi nan tan te/ de dgu la gnas
268a2(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' rnams chos thams cad kyi nan tan bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi 'grub pa ste/ 
268a3(phal chen): bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar dge ba'i bshes gnyen la sems pa ni sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams 'grub pa'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i bka' la mngon par yid ches pa ni sangs rgyas
268a4(phal chen): kyi chos rnams 'grub pa'o// dam pa'i chos la mi spong ba ni/ sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams 'grub pa'o// tshad med pa'i sems kyis sangs rgyasu dge ba'i rtsa ba yongs
268a5(phal chen): bsngo ba mi zad pa ni/ sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams 'grub pa 'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i yul sa mtshams med par yid ches pa ni sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams 'grub pa'o/ 
268a6(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams kyi yul la 'jug pa ni sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams 'grub pa'o// chos kyi dbyings kyi yul las mi g.yo ba ni sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams 'grub pa'o// bdud
268a7(phal chen): kyi yul las gyen du spag pa ni sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams 'grub pa'o// sangs rgyas thams cad kyi yul rjesu dran pa ni sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams 'grub pa'o// de bzhin gshegs pa
268a8(phal chen): stobs bcu'i yul la mngon par mos pa ni sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams 'grub pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi 'grub pa ste/ de dag
268b1(phal chen): gnas shing / byang chub sems dpa' rnams de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes chen po 'grub pa bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang
268b2(phal chen): chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi chos las 'gol bar lam ste/ de dag ni byang chub sems dpas yongasu spang bar bya ba dag go// bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar dge ba'i bshes
268b3(phal chen): gnyen la brnyes pa ni sangs rgyas kyi chos las 'gol ba'i lam mo// 'khor gyi sdug bsngal gyis 'jigs pa ni sangs rgyas kyi chos las 'gol ba'i lam mo// byang chub sems
268b4(phal chen): dpa'i spyod pas skyo ba ni/ sangs rgyas kyi chos las la/ gol ba'i lam mo// 'jig rten gyi khams nagan/ sa pas yongasu skyo ba ni/ sangs rgyas kyi chos las 'gol
268b5(phal chen): ba'i lam mo// mnyam par gzhag pa la gnas byed pa ni/ sangs rgyas kyi chos las 'gol ba'i lam mo// dge ba'i rtsa ba la chags shing zhen pa ni/ sangs rgyas kyi chos
268b6(phal chen): las 'gol ba'i lam mo// dam pa'i chos spong ba ni sangs rgyas kyi chos las 'gol ba'i lam mo// byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa las dpa' bas 'byed pa ni/ sangs rgyas kyi chos
268b7(phal chen): las 'gol ba'i lam mo// nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas su 'dod pa ni sangs rgyas kyi chos las 'gol ba'i lam mo// byang chub sems dpa' la zhe sdang shing khong khro ba ni/ sangs rgyas
268b8(phal chen): chos las 'gol ba'i lam mo// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi chos las 'gol ba'i lam rnams te/ de dag ni byang chub sems
269a1(phal chen): dpas yong su spang bar bya'o// de dag yongasu spangs nas de'i 'og tu byang chub sems dpa' rnams byang chub sems dpa'i skyon med pa nyid du 'da' bar 'gyur ba dag go/ 
269a2(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi skyon med pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yang mngon par sgrub la/ sems can
269a3(phal chen): thams cad la yang rnam par lta ba dang / lta ba'i rnam pa thams cad dang yang bral la lta ba'i bcing bas glags pa thams cad kyang rab tu 'grel pa dang / mtshan ma thams cad kyang yid / 
269a4(phal chen): byed la/ mtshan ma la mngon par dga' ba'i sems can/ thams cad kyang mi 'dor ba dang / khams gsum/ pa thams cad las yang dag par 'das te/ 'jig rten gyi
269a5(phal chen): khams kyi gnas thams cad na gnas pa dang / nyon mo/ sa pa rnams kyang rnam par bzlog la/ sems can rnams dang phrad cing 'grogs pa dang / chos rnams las
269a6(phal chen): kyang 'dod chags dang bral la/ sems can thams cad la yang snying rje chen pos byams pa dang / dngos po thams cad kyis kyang dben la 'khor thams cad kyang yongasu ston pa dang / 
269a7(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams las kyang gyen du 'phags la skye zhing shi 'pho ba'i spyod pa yang mngon par sgrub pa dang / 'jig rten gyi chos thams cad kyis kyang mgos la/ 'jig rten gyi bya ba
269a8(phal chen): thams cad la yang thogs pa med pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi byang chub kyang mngon du gyur la/ spyod pa dang / smon lam chen po'i nyim yang rgyun mi gcod pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i
269b1(phal chen): sras bcu po de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi skyon med pa 'phags pa 'jig rten las 'das pa/ 'gro ba thams cad dang thun mong ma yin pa/ nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas
269b2(phal chen): thams cad dang ma 'dres pa ste/ skyon med pa de dag la gnas shing / byang chub sems dpa' rnams byang chub sems dpa'i chos nges pa rnams 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go// kye rgyal
269b3(phal chen): ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi byang chub sems dpa'i chos nges pa 'thob ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar de bzhin gshegs pa'i rig su skyes pa
269b4(phal chen): yin/ sangs rgyas kyi yul la gnas pa yin/ byang chub sems dpa'i las la zhugs pa yin/ pha rol tu phyin pa la nan tan byed pa yin/ sangs rgyas kyi rgyud
269b5(phal chen): nas byung ba yin/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i gdungs la sa skyes pa yin/ sangs rgyas kyi stobs la gnas ba yin/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i byang chub tu rjesu song ba
269b6(phal chen): yin/ sangs rgyas thams cad dang sku dang rang bzhin gcig pa yin/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rnam par spyod pa dang / mi gnyis pa yin te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po
269b7(phal chen): de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi byang chub sems dpa'i chos nges pa 'thob pa ste/ de dag ni skyon med pa la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis 'thob dag go/ 
269b8(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi chos la 'byung ba'i lam ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar dge ba'i bshes gnyen rnams
270a1(phal chen): dang / rgyud kyi tshul gcig tu 'gyur ba dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba thun mong du mos pa ni sangs rgyas kyi chos la 'byung ba'i la mo// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi
270a2(phal chen): rnam par 'phrul pa dang tshul 'thun zhing / smon lam chen po la dbugs phyin pa thob pa ni/ sangs rgyas kyi chos la 'byung ba'i lamo// sems rgya chen pos rang gi dge ba'i rtsa ba'i ga/ 
270a3(phal chen): bya pa ni/ sangs rgyas kyi chos la 'byung ba'i la mo// las ji ltar byas pa chud mi za bas/ bskal pa 'grangs pa thams cad du mi skyo ba ni sangs rgyas kyi chos la 'byung ba'i la mo// 
270a4(phal chen): phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa thams cad du yongasu 'dzin pa sa 'jig rten gyi khams grangs med par gnas par bya ba ni sangs rgyas kyi chos la 'byung ba'i la mo// 
270a5(phal chen): sems can gyi khams thams cad yongasu smin par bya ba la mkhas pas/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa rgyu na mo gcod pa ni sangs rgyas kyi chos la 'byung ba'i lamo// 
270a6(phal chen): snying rje chen po bskyed de sems tshad med par byed pa ni sangs rgyas kyi chos la 'byung ba'i la mo// na mkha'i dbyings thams cad sems bskyed pa gcig gis rgyas par dgang bas/ spyad
270a7(phal chen): pa dang smon lam chen po'i khyad par 'jug pa ni sangs rgyas kyi chos la 'byung ba'i lamo// sngon mngon par bsgrub pa chud mi za bas// de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs yang dag par
270a8(phal chen): 'dzin pa ni sangs rgyas kyi chos la 'byung ba'i la mo// 'gro ba thams cad la byang chub kyi sems yongasu ston cing / byang chub kyi sems skyes pa rnams kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad
270b1(phal chen): nye bar ston pa ni sangs rgyas kyi chos la 'byung ba'i la mo// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi chos la 'byung ba'i lam ste/ 
270b2(phal chen): de dag gis byung ba'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams skyes bu dam pa'i ming bcu 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams
270b3(phal chen): kyi skyes bu dam pa'i ming 'thob pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar byang chub kyi ye shes kyi lus dang ldan pas/ byang chub sems dpa' zhes bya ba yin/ theg pa chen po la
270b4(phal chen): rab tu gnas pa'i phyir sems dpa' chen po zhes bya bayin/ chos kyi dam pa mngon par rtogs pas dam/ pa'i sems dpa' zhes bya ba yin/ mchog gi chos
270b5(phal chen): mngon par 'tshang rgya bas mchog gi sems dpa' zhes bya ba yin/ ye shes kyi khyad par rab dang ldan pa sa rab kyi sems dpa' zhes bya ba yin/ phul du brtson
270b6(phal chen): 'grus rtsoms pas phul gyi sems dpa' zhes bya ba yin/ gong na med pa'i chos yang dag par ston pas/ bla na med pa'i sems dpa' zhes bya ba yin/ stobs bcu'i ye
270b7(phal chen): shes yangs pa dang ldan pas stobs kyi sems dpa' zhes bya ba yin/ 'gro ba thams cad na dpe med pas mi mnyam mi 'dra ba'i sems dpa' zhes bya ba yin/ nam 'dod pa'i
270b8(phal chen): sems kyi skad cig la byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bas bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i sems dpa' zhes bya ba yin/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ byang chub sems
271a1(phal chen): dpa' rnams kyi skyes bu dam pa'i ming thob pa rnams so// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lam ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 
271a2(phal chen): 'di ltar gcig pu grogs med par byang chub kyi sems mi gtong bas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lam gcig la rten pa dang / thabs dang shes rab kyis mngon par sgrubangs
271a3(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lam yan lag gnyis pa dang / stong pa nyid kyi sbyor ba dang / mtshan ma med pa'i mtha'i rtse mor phyin pa dang / smon pa med pa'i phyir khams gsum
271a4(phal chen): dang / mi 'dre bas byang chub sems dpa'i lam rnams pa gsum pa dang / nyes pa bshags pa'i tshul dang // bsod nams thams cad la rjes su yi rang ba dang / 
271a5(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa la gsol ba gdab pa'i rim gro rgyun mi gcod pa dang / yongasu bsngo ba las mkhas pas/ shin tu bsngo ba'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa'i lam
271a6(phal chen): spyod pa bzhis smos pa dang / dad pa'i rtsa ba tshugs te shin tu brtan pa dang / brtson 'grus chen po las phyir mi ldog pa dang / dran pa rtse gcig pa dang / ting nge 'dzin gyi tshul ma
271a7(phal chen): 'khrugs pa dang / rab tu rtogs pa'i shes rab kyi spyod yul la mkhas pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lam dbang po lngas rnam par spel pa dang / 'di ltar ste/ lnga'i
271a8(phal chen): mig gis 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi gzugs kyi rnam pa thams cad sems can gyi shi 'pho ba dang / skye ba thams cad yong su mthong ba'i rang bzhin dang ldan pa dang / lha'i rnabs de/ 
271b1(phal chen): bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos bstan pa mnyan cing dran par bya ba dang / yongasu gzung bar bya bas/ sems can pha rol gyi dbang po la yang dag par phyin par byed pa dang / bdag
271b2(phal chen): gi sems chags pa med pas pha rol gyi sems shes pas mthong ba la dbang sgyur ba mngon par bsgrubs pa dang / sngon gyi gnas rjes su dran pas bskal pa 'grangs pa thams cad rjes
271b3(phal chen): dran zhing / dge ba'i rtsa ba rnam par 'phel bar byed pa dang / rdzu 'phrul dang rnam par 'phrul pa chen po bsgrubs pas/ sems can ji ltar 'dul ba bzhin du cho 'phrul sna tshogs
271b4(phal chen): yongasu ston cing / sems can thams cad la chos rjod pa da dang / zag pa zad pa'i ye shes dang ldan pas yang dag pa'i mtha' mngon sum du mthong zhing byang chub sems
271b5(phal chen): dpa'i spyod pa bsgrub pa rgyun mi gcod pas byang chub sems dang kha' rnams kyi lam mngon par shes pa drug gis rnam par 'phrul pa dang / 'di lta ste sems can gyi gtso bo
271b6(phal chen): mtha' yas pa thams cad skra'i rtse mo gcig la bzhugs par mthong ste/ yang dag par gzung zhing / sems can gzhan gyis bsam pas/ rnam par rig par bya ba la 'jug pas sangs
271b7(phal chen): rgyas rjes su dran pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa gcig gi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor nas ma g.yos par de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor du mngon du zhal nas chos
271b8(phal chen): bstan pa bsgrags pa mi bad pas/ 'gro ba thams cad kyi bsam pa dang dbang po ji lta ba bzhin du rnam par rig par bya ba la 'jug pas chos rjes su dran pa dang / byor mi ldog pa'i byang/ 
272a1(phal chen): chub sems dpa'i tshogs mthong ba dang / mi 'bral zhing 'gro ba thams cad la byang chub sems dpa'i lus yongasu ston pas/ dge bdun rje su dran pa dang / byang chub
272a2(phal chen): sems dpa' thams cad kyi sbyin pa yongasu gtong ba la yang dag par gzhol zhing / gtong ba chen pos rnam par spel ba'i yid la byed pas/ gtong ba rjesu dran pa dang / byang chub kyi sems
272a3(phal chen): dang mi 'bral bas dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad 'gro ba thams cad la stobs pas/ tshul khrims rjesu dran pa dang / dga' ldan gyi pho brang gi mchog na/ byang chub sems dpa' tshe
272a4(phal chen): gcig gi thogs pa bzhugs pa rjes su dran pas/ lha rjes su dran pa dang / thabs kyi ye shes chen pos 'a dgro ba thams cad yongasu smin par bya ba dang / gdul ba rgyun
272a5(phal chen): mi 'chad pa la zhugs te/ sems can rjes su dran pa'i phyir dge 'dun rjes su dran pas/ byang chub sems dpa'i lam rjes su dran pa bdun gyis mngon par bsgrubs
272a6(phal chen): pa dang / 'di lta ste/ log par lta ba thams cad yongasu spangs pas/ yang dag pa'i lta ba'i lam du byung ba dang / rnam par rtog pa dang / yongasu rtog pa dang bral bas thams cad
272a7(phal chen): mkhyen pa nyid dang 'thun zhing / don yod la yid la bya ba med pas/ byung ba dang / ngag gi nyes pa bzhi dang bral bas/ 'phags pa dang 'thun zhing yang dag pa'i ngag rab tu brjod pa/ 
272a8(phal chen): dang / lus kyi las thams cad sems can nye bar 'tsho bas/ 'gro ba thams cad thogs pa med par yongasu smin par byed cing / 'dul bas mngon par bsgrubs pa dang
272b1(phal chen): 'phags pa'i rigs la rab tu gnas shing / sbyangs pa'i yon tan gyi sdom pa/ byang chub kyi lam dang ldan pa'i spyod lam dang spyod pa dang / tshul la rab tu gnas shing / thams/ 
272b2(phal chen): cad du kha na ma tho ba med pas/ yang dag pa'i 'tsho ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi brtul zhugs dang / dka' thub kyis kun nas gdungs pa dang / yongasu gdungs
272b3(phal chen): pa yang dag par ston cing / de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu'i rang bzhin thogs pa med pa dang ldan pa'i phyir yang dag pa'i rtsol ba dang / sgra thams cad 'dzin cing dran pa 'jig
272b4(phal chen): rten gyi rnam par 'khrug pa thams cad kyis bar du mi chod/ pa'i phyir yang dag pa'i dran pa dang / byang chub sem/ ud pa'i rnam par thar pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i ting / 
272b5(phal chen): 'dzin gcig gis ting nge 'dzin thams cad mngon par bsdu ba pa la mkhas pa'i phyir/ yang dag pa'i ting nge dzin dang ldan pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi
272b6(phal chen): lam ni/ 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa dang ldan zhing / byang chub dang 'thun par gyur pa dang / 'di lta ste 'dod pa dang / gnod sems dang / 'tshe ba med pa dang / 
272b7(phal chen): ngag gi las thams cad kyis ma bsgrubs par chos ston pa'i tshul dang ldan pas/ rnam par rtog pa dang / rnam par dpyod pa bsal ba dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes la sems/ 
272b8(phal chen): can yongasu smin par bya ba'i bsam pa yongasu mi gtong zhing dga' bzeng zeng po dang bral ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad mthong bas dga' ba'i yid bde ba yang rgyun mi 'chad cing
273a1(phal chen): 'jig rten pa'i bde ba dang / sdug bsngal dang bral bas/ 'phags pa 'jig rten las 'das pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i lam dang 'thun pa dang / mi g.yo ba'i gdugs
273a2(phal chen): med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pas mngon par bsgrubs pa dang / 'dod pa'i khams dang gzugs kyi khams su skyes pa las ma g.yos par 'du shes dang / tshor ba thams cad 'gog pa'i
273a3(phal chen): snyoms par 'jug pas mngon par bsgrubs shing / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa bsgrub pa rgyun mi gcod pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lam mthar gyis spyod cing snyoms
273a4(phal chen): par 'jug pa dgus mngon par bsgrubs pa dang / 'di lta ste gnas dang / gnas ma yin pa la mkhas pa de'i ye shes dang ldan pa dang 'gro ba thams cad kyi 'das pa
273a5(phal chen): dang ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i las dang rgyud nga rnam par smin pa yongasu len pa shin tu rtog pa dang / dbang po ji lta ba bzhin du chos ston cing / go bar byed pas
273a6(phal chen): sems can gyi khams thams cad kyi dbang po rab dang tha ma shes pa'i ye shes kyis shin tu brtags pa dang / khams tha dad pa dang khams dum la mkhas pa dang ldan pa dang / rab dang
273a7(phal chen): tham dang 'bring la mos pa rab tu rtogs pa'i chos kyi tshul la zhugs pa dang / 'gro ba thams cad dang / zhing dang dus dang / bskal pa thams cad byang chub sems dpa'i lus dang // gzugs
273a8(phal chen): kyis rgyas par dgang shing / de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshul yongasu bstan pas/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa bsgrub pa yongasu mi gtong ba dang / bsam gtan dang / rnam par thar pa
273b1(phal chen): dang / ting nge 'dzin dang snyoms par 'jug pa dang / kun nas nyon mongs pa dang / rnam par byang ba thams cad las rnam par ldang ba dus la bab pa dang / dus la ma bab pa rtogs pa'i ye
273b2(phal chen): shes kyi tshul gyis mngon par bsgrubs pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa la rab tu gnas pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi lte ba dang / shi 'pho ba dang / lam gyi rgyud dang / 
273b3(phal chen): 'pho ba tha dad pa'i gnas la mkhas pa dang ldan pa dang / dus gsum gyi bskal pa 'grangs pa thams cad skad cig gcig tu gzud pa rtogs pa'i ye shes snang bas mngon par sgrubs pa
273b4(phal chen): dang / 'gro ba thams cad kyi nyon mongs pa dang / bag ma gas dang / bsam pa dang bag la nyal ba byang ba thob dpa'i ye shes kyi tshul gyis mngon par bsgrubs pa'i byang
273b5(phal chen): chub sems dpa'i spyod pa bsgrub pa mi gtong bas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lam ni de bzhin gshe gas pa'i stobs bcu rab tu rtogs pa la yang dag par
273b6(phal chen): btang ba'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lam ste/ de dag la gnas shing / byang chub sems dpa' rnams de bzhin gshegs pa thams
273b7(phal chen): cad kyi lam la mkhas pas bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go// kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lam ni tshad med pa'o// lam gyi tshogs ni
273b8(phal chen): tshad med pa'o// lam bsgom pa ni tshad med pa'o// lam gyi rgyan ni tshad med pa'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras de la bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi
274a1(phal chen): lam tshad med pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar na mkha'i dbyings tshad med pa dang / mtha' dang dbus med pa'i chos kyi dbyings tshad med pa dang / mi zad pa'i sems
274a2(phal chen): can gyi khams tshad med pa dang / mu med pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams tshad med pa dang / mi zad pa'i bskal pa 'grangs pa tshad med pa dang / 'gro ba thams cad kyi tha snyad mtha' yas shing
274a3(phal chen): tshad med pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku tshad med pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsungs gi dbyangs tshad med pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs tshad med pa dang
274a4(phal chen): thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes tshad med pa ste/ kye rgya/ la ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa/ 'a rnams kyi lam tshad med pa rnamaso// kye rgyal ba'i sras
274a5(phal chen): de ci'i phyir zhe na/ na mkha'i dbyings ji tsam du tshad med pa de tsam du tshad med par byang chub sems dpa' la ma gyi tshogs yongasu bsdu bar bya'o// ji ltar chos kyi
274a6(phal chen): dbyings mtha' dang dbus med pa/ de ltar mtha' dang dbus med par byang chub sems dpas lam gyi tshogs yongasu bsdu bar bya'o// ji ltar sems can gyi khams mi zad pa de
274a7(phal chen): ltar mi zad par byang chub sems dpas lam gyi tshogs yongasu bsdu bar bya'o// ji ltar 'jig rten gyi khams mu med pa de ltar mu med par byang chub sems dpas lam gyi tshogs
274a8(phal chen): yongasu bsdu bar bya'o// ji ltar bskal pa grangasu 'grang zhing bstan pa mi zad pa de ltar 'gro ba thams cad du mi zad par byang chub sems dpas lam gyi tshogs yongasu bsdu bar
274b1(phal chen): bya'o// ji ltar 'gro ba thams cad kyi tha snyad mtha' yas pa de ltar 'gro ba thams cad kyi sgra dang tha snyad la 'jug pa'i ye shes kyis mngon par bsgrubs pa mtha' yas par byang
274b2(phal chen): chub sems dpas lam gyi tshogs yongasu bsdu bar bya'o// ji ltar de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku tshad med pa de ltar 'gro ba dang / zhing dang dus dang sems can dang / bskal pa
274b3(phal chen): thams cad du rgyas par 'gengs shing / tshad med par byang chub sems dpas lam gyi tshogs yongasu bsdu bar bya'o// ji ltar sangs rgyas kyi gsung gi dbyangs tshad med pa de ltar bya
274b4(phal chen): chub sems dpas tshig gi lam gcig brjod pas chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad du rgyas par khyab cing / sems can gyi khams thams cad go bar byed pa'i/ 
274b5(phal chen): lam gyi tshogs yongasu bsdu bar bya'o// ji ltar de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs tshad med pa de ltar de bzhin ga shegs pa'i stobs kyis brtan pa'i byang chub sems dpas
274b6(phal chen): lam gyi tshogs yongasu bsdu bar bya'o// ji ltar thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes tshad med pa de ltar tshad med par byas te/ byang chub sems dpas lam gyi tshogs yongasu bsdu bar
274b7(phal chen): bya'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lam gyi tshogs ste de dag la gnas shing / byang chub sems dpa' rnams de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye
274b8(phal chen): shes mtha' dang dbus med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis lam bsgom pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar
275a1(phal chen): lus dang ngag dang sems kyi mi longs pa med pas/ blang ba med pa dang / dor ba med pa bsgom pa dang / yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du 'jug pa'i ye shes dang ldan pas/ 
275a2(phal chen): bstan pa med pa dang / dbri ba med pa bsgom pa dang / rang bzhin gyis 'jug pa med pas/ bsgom pa med pa dang / rnam par bsgom pa med pa bsgom pa dang / mngon par zhen pa thams
275a3(phal chen): cad dang bral bas/ sgyu ma dang / rmi lam dang / mig yor dang / sgra brnyan dang / gzugs brnyan dang / mig rgyu dang / tshul zla ba lta bur bsgom pa dang / khams gsum pa'i bsod
275a4(phal chen): nams blta bas bsags pa bsal ba'i phyir/ stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa dang / mngon par 'du bya ba med pa bsgom pa dang / chos
275a5(phal chen): gdags pa rnam par dgod pa dang bral bas brjod du med pa dang / bstan du med pa dang / smos su med pa dang // bshad du med pa bsgom pa dang / chos thams cad la zhug
275a6(phal chen): pa'i ye shes mngon sum dang ldan pas/ chos kyi dbyings tha mi dad pa bsgom pa dang / de kho na nyid dang / de bzhin nyid na mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam pa khong du chud bas/ de bzhin
275a7(phal chen): nyid dang / yang dag pa'i mtha' ma nyams par bsgom pa dang / mngon par 'du byed pa'i stobs rgyun mi 'chad pa'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa'i ye shes yangs pa bsgom pa
275a8(phal chen): dang / chos thams cad mngon sum du gyur te/ the tsom med pas/ de bzhin go shegs pa'i stobs bcu dang / mi bsnyengs pa bzhi dang / tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen padang / 
275b1(phal chen): thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes mtshungs pa med pa bsgom pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lam bsgom pa ste/ de dag la gnas shing /

275b3(phal chen): kyi lam gyi rgyan te/ bcu gang zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras 'di la byang chub sems dpa' 'dod pa'i khams nas kyang mi g.yo la/ gzugs dang / gzugs med pa la spyod pa'i bsam
275b4(phal chen): gtan dang / rnam par thar pa dang / ting nge 'dzin dang /  snyoms par 'jug pa la snyoms par 'jug kyang / de dag gi dbang gi mi skye ba 'di ni lam gyi rgyan dang po'o// 
275b5(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang / byang chub sems dpa' nyan thos kyi lam mngon sum du gyur pa'i ye shes la zhu gas kyang / lam des 'byung ba yang ma yin pa 'di ni

275b7(phal chen): stobs rgyun mi gcod pa 'di ni lam gyi rgyan gsum pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang / byang chub sems dpa' g.yog 'khor mang po dang ldan zhing / g.yog 'khor lha dang mi rnam par
275b8(phal chen): dag pa dang ldan zhing lha'i bu mo brgya stong gis rol mo brdung ba dang / dkrol ba'i sgra phyung ste brjod pa la spyod kyang / byang chub sems dpa'i lam dang ldan pa'i bsam gtan dang / rnam
276a1(phal chen): par thar pa dang / ting nge 'dzin dang / snyoms par 'jug pa mi 'dor ba 'di ni lam gyi rgyan bzhi pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' 'gro ba
276a2(phal chen): thams cad kyi rtse rgal dga' dgod pa dang / sems can dang 'dres shing 'bur ldog pa byed kyang / sems kyi skad cig gcig la yang byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin mnyam pa nyid mi
276a3(phal chen): 'dor ba 'di ni lam gyi rgyan lnga pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang / byang chub sems dpa' 'jig rten gyi chos thams cad dang ma 'dres shing 'jig rten gyi pha rol tu phyin pa yin yang /

276a5(phal chen): dag pa ji lta ba bzhin gyi ye shes snang ba la zhugs pa'i lam la gnas kyang lam ngan par zhugs pa'i sems can phyir zlog pa'i phyir lam ma yin pa dang / lam ngan pa yang
276a6(phal chen): gnon la/ lam nges 'khor ba 'dzin pa yang ma yin te/ des dag par yang mi sems pa 'di ni lam gyi rgyan bdun pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang / byang chub sems dpa'
276a7(phal chen): rtag tu tshul khrims legs par bsrungs pa dang ldan zhing / de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshul khrims rnam par dag pa la rten pas/ lus dang ngag dang yid kyi las kyi mtha' kha na ma thob
276a8(phal chen): med pa dang ldan yang / tshul khrims ngan pa dang ldan pa'i sems can yongasu smin par bya'i phyir/ so so'i skye bo tha mal pa'i spyod pa thams cad ston cing / byang chub sems dpa'
276b1(phal chen): lam la brten pas bsod nams kyi tshogs rnam par dag pa thams cad yong su rdzogs pa yin yang / sems can dmyal ba dang / byol song gi skye gnas dang / gshin rje'i 'jig rten
276b2(phal chen): dang / mi khom pa dang / dbul bar skyes pa'i lam du zhugs pa'i sems can thams cad rnam par bzlog pa'i phyir/ de dag gi lam du skyes pa yang ston la/ lam de dag la yang dag

276b5(phal chen): sangs rgyas thams cad kyi chos kyi sku dang / lus gcig tu gyur pa sems can tha~Md kyi chos kyi snying po'i tshul can gongs pa'i snang ba khong du chud pa theg pa thams cad kyi mnyam
276b6(phal chen): pa nyid la rab tu gnas pa/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi spyod yul la mngon par mos pa/ 'gro ba thams cad kyi yid du 'ong ba/ sems can gyi khams thams cad kyis ngor blta ba/ 'gro/ 
276b7(phal chen): ba thams cad kyi slob dpon du bya ba yin yang / chos yongasu btsal bar bya ba rgyun mi gcod cing / ngo mtshar gyis yongasu zin par snang bas/ sri zhu'i las thams cad la gnas te/ 
276b8(phal chen): mkhan po dang slob dpon du ston kyang / de nyid 'gro ba thams cad kyi slob dpon du gyur pa yin te/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni thabs mkhas pa dang ldan par
277a1(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa'i lam la shin tu gnas pa yin pas/ de dag ni thabs gang dang gang gis sems can rnams 'dul bar 'gyur ba de dang de'i thabs sems can rnams la

277a4(phal chen): pa'i mchog thob pa/ chags pa med cing dri ma med pa'i tha/ dpas dang ldan pa 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du thogs pa med par de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku yang dag par
277a5(phal chen): ston pa/ chos kyi 'khor lo thogs pa med par bskor ba'i bya na gyi brlabs dang ldan pa/ 'jig rten gyi khamasathams cad du khyab pa'i lus dang gzugs bdog pa/ chos

277a7(phal chen): 'das pa dang / ma 'ongs pa dang da ltar byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang yul gcig tu gyur pa yang yin la/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa yang rgyun mi gcod cing / bya
277a8(phal chen): chub sems dpa'i chos nyid kyang rnam par mi spong / byang chub sems dpa'i las kyang rnam par mi ldog/ byang chub sems dpa'i lam las kyang phyir mi ldog/ byang chub sems dpa'i
277b1(phal chen): spyod pa yang rgyun mi gcod/ byang chub sems dpa'i nye bar len pa yang 'chad par mi byed/ byang chub sems dpa'i thabs mkhas pa las kyang phyir mi ldog/ byang chub sems dpa'i bya ba
277b2(phal chen): yang thogs par mi byed/ byang chub sems dpa'i mngon par 'du byed pa'i stobs kyis kyang yongasu skyo ba med cing / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa'i byin gyi brlabs las kyang ring du
277b3(phal chen): 'phang ba ma yin te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ltar byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa rgyun mi gcad pa dang / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi sgo la rnam par lta ba de lta bus ni/ bya
277b4(phal chen): chub sems dpa' bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i bya/ dang chub tu myur du 'byung ba'i phyir te/ 'di ni lam gyi rgyan bcu pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni
277b5(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lam gyi rgyan te/ de dgal gnas shing / byang chub sems dpa' rnams de bzhin gshegs pa'i lam rin po che'i rgyan bla na med pa thob
277b6(phal chen): par gyur kyang / byang chub sems dpa'i lam gyi rgyun mi gcod pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rkang pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di
277b7(phal chen): ltar smon lam chen po'i khyad par yongasu bsdu ba shin tu rdzogs par bya ba'i phyir/ tshul khrims kyi rkang pa dang / byang chub kyi yan lag thams cad yang dag par bsdu ba las phyir mi
277b8(phal chen): ldog pa'i phyir/ brtson 'grus kyi rkang pa dang / sems can rnams bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du yongs su tshim par bya ba'i phyir/ mngon par shes pa'i rkang pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi
278a1(phal chen): zhing thams cad du 'gro yang zhing gcig nas mi g.yo ba'i phyir/ rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa dang / khyad par du 'gro ba'i phyir lhag pa'i bsam pa'i rkang pa dang / brtsams pa
278a2(phal chen): thams cad mthar phyin par bya ba'i phyir/ dam bcas pa brtan pa'i rkang pa dang / bla ma thams cad kyis bsgo ba las 'gal bar mi byed pa'i phyir 'thun par 'dzin pa'i rkang pa dang / de bzhin
278a3(phal chen): gshegs pa thams cad kyis gsungs pa yang dag par gzung bas mi skyo ba'i phyir/ chos mnyan pa mi ngoms par tshol ba'i rkang pa dang / tshangs pa'i gnas nas 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor
278a4(phal chen): thams cad du 'gro bas/ sgyid lug pa med pa'i phyir chos kyi char 'bebs pa'i rkang pa dang / thams cad du don ma tho ba med pa'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa'i spong
278a5(phal chen): pa chen po la nan tan du byed pa'i rkang pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' na mas kyi rkang pa ste/ de dag la gnas shing / byang chub
278a6(phal chen): sems dpa' rnams de bzhin gshegs pa'i zhabs kyi mchog gi 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du 'gro ba bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag
278a7(phal chen): nibyang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lag pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis gsungs pa la gcig tu mos shing yid ches pas mthar phyin par
278a8(phal chen): bya ba'i phyir/ dang pa'i lag pa dang / slong ba thams cad yid bzhin du tshim par bya ba'i phyir gtang ba rab tu gtong ba'i lag pa dang / lag pa g.yas pa brkyang ba'i phyir/ tshur shag
278b1(phal chen): bde bar 'ongs sam zhes 'dor te/ gsong por sla ba'i lag pa dang / bsod nams bsags pa rnam par spel ba las mi g.yo ba'i phyir/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad mchod cing
278b2(phal chen): rim gro byed pa'i lag pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi the tsom gcad ba'i phyir thos pa thams cad la mkhas pa'i lag pa dang / 'dod pa'i 'dam du thogs pa'i sems can gyi khams
278b3(phal chen): la lag pa ring du brkyang ste/ 'ju bar rnyebs pa'i phyir khams gsum dang bral zhing shin tu 'byung bar byed pa'i lag pa dang / chu bo chen po bzhis khyer ba la lag pa ring du brkyang zhing
278b4(phal chen): gdon pa'i phyir/ bde ba'i thang la gzhog pa'i lag pa/  dang / 'gro ba thams cad la gnod pa med par bstan dpa'i chos rab tu bstan pa'i phyir/ yang dag par sbyor/ 
278b5(phal chen): ba'i chos la slob dpon gyis mi bcab pa'i lag pa dang / lus dang sems kyi nang rab tu bsal ba'i phyir/ 'jig rten pa dang / 'jig rten las 'das pa'i gtsug
278b6(phal chen): lag thams cad shes pa'i lag pa dang / nyon mongs pa'i mun pa thams cad dang bral ba'i chos kyi snang ba mtshungs pa med pa yongasu bstan pa'i phyir shes rab dang / ye shes
278b7(phal chen): rin po che'i lag pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lag pa ste/ de dag la gnas shing / byang chub sems dpa' rnams de
278b8(phal chen): bzhin gshegs pa'i phyag 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kun nas yog par skyob pa bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go// 
279a1(phal chen): bam po brgyad cu rtsa gnyis pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lto ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar
279a2(phal chen): bsam pa dag pas g.yo med pa'i lto dang / drang bas sgyu med pa'i lto dang / thibs po med pas 'chos pa med pa'i lto dang / dngos po thams cad la mngon par chags pa med pas
279a3(phal chen): yul la mi 'dzin pa'i lto dang / shes pa'i phyir nyon mongs pa thams cad sel ba'i lto dang / skyon med pa'i phyir sems dag pa'i lto dang / chos ji lta ba bzhin du yid la bya ba'i phyir
279a4(phal chen): kha zas thams cad yongasu shes par bya ba so sor rtog/ das pa'i lto dang / rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba rjes su rtog zas par bya ba'i phyir/ mngon par 'du mi byed pa so sor
279a5(phal chen): rtogs pa'i lto dang / bsam pa shin tu smin pas 'byu nga ba thams cad shes pa'i lto dang / sems can thams cad sangs rgyas kyi sku'i nang du chud pa khong du chud pa'i phyir/ 
279a6(phal chen): dri ma mtha' yas pa'i lta ba thams cad dang bral ba'i lte'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lto ste/ de dag la gnas shing / byang chub sem
279a7(phal chen): dpa' rnams de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku 'gro ba thams cad yongasu 'dzin pa bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa'
279a8(phal chen): rnams kyi snying po ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi tshul gyi mthu tshang med pa yongasasu bskyed pa'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi snying po
279b1(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi rigs rgyun mi gcod par kun nas gnas pa dang / ye shes kyi snang ba chen po yongasu bstan pa'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa'i snying po chos kyi rigs rab tu gsal bar byed par
279b2(phal chen): kun nas gnas pa dang / phyir mi ldog pa'i 'khor lo la yang dag par gzhol bar bya ba'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi snying po dge 'dun gyi rigs yongasu sdud par kun nas
279b3(phal chen): gnas pa dang / dus ji lta ba bzhin las mi 'da' bar bya ba'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi snying po chos thams cad nges par gleng pa byed pa dang / rgyu gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa'i
279b4(phal chen): rgyun mi 'chad par bya ba'i phyir/ byang chub sems/ dpa' rnams kyi snying po nges pa med pa yongasasu smin par byed pa// ra gnas pa dang / ma 'ongs pa'i rgyu skyon med par bya ba'i
279b5(phal chen): phyi ra/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi snying po se mas can log par nges pa rnams la snying rje chen po skye bar kun nas gnas pa dang / bdud kyi sde thams cad btul
279b6(phal chen): te/ dge ba'i rtsa ba mi 'phrogs par bya ba'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi snying po de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu thub pa med pa'i rgyu yongasu rdzogs par byed par kun nas
279b7(phal chen): gnas pa dang / 'gro ba ma lus pa thams cad yongasu tshim par bya ba'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi snying po mi 'jigs pa chen po'i seng ge dang / khyu mchog gi nga ro 'byin par
279b8(phal chen): kun nas gnas pa dang / thams cad du ye shes yang dag par gzhol bar bya ba'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi snying po sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad 'thob pa'i
280a1(phal chen): phyi kun nas gnas pa dang / gang cig gcig tu mi mnyam pa med par zhugs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi stong ba nang thams ca dang / chos thams cad dang / sarba/ 
280a2(phal chen): rgyas thams cad mnyam pa nyid du khong du chud par gnas pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi stong po ste/ de dag la gnas shing / byang chub
280a3(phal chen): sems dpa' rnams dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad ma log pas de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes chen po'i snying po bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag
280a4(phal chen): nibyang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi snying po ste/ bcu ga she na/ brtsams pa thams cad mthar phyin pa dar bya ba'i phyir zhe non pa'i snying dang / mtshan dang dpe byang
280a5(phal chen): bzang po'i bsod nams kyi tshogs yongasu bsdu ba'i phyirasems zhum pa med pa'i snying dang / bdud kyi sde tha mas cad rab tu gzhom pa'i phyir/ rnam par gnon pa tshon
280a6(phal chen): po'i snying dang / nyon mongs pa thams cad kyi mo tshugs pa'i phyir/ tshul bzhin du sbyor ba'i snying dang / snying po byang chub kyi bar du phyin par bya ba'i phyir/ phyir mi 'gyur zhing phyir mi ldog
280a7(phal chen): pa'i snying dang / sems 'pho ba med par khong du chud pas mngon par chags pa med pa'i phyir/ rang bzhin gyis 'od gsal ba'i snying dang / ji ltar mos pa'i tshul bzhin du/ rnam par
280a8(phal chen): thar pa 'thob par bya ba'i phyir/ sems can gyi tshul shes pa'i snying dang / theg pa gzhan la mos pa med par sems can gyi khams yongasu bskyab pa'i phyir/ tshangs pa'i rnam
280b1(phal chen): par spyod pa rgya chen pos sangs rgyas kyi chos la 'jug pa'i snying dang / lta ba'i mtshan mas khams gsum la mngon par chags pa med par bya ba'i phyir/ stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med
280b2(phal chen): pa dang / smon pa med pa dang / mngon par 'du bya ba med pa'i snying dang / sems can thams cad bdud du gyur pa'i sgos bdud thams cad 'ongs par gyur kyang / spu gcig kyang mi g.yo/ 
280b3(phal chen): pas dpal gyi be'us brgyan cing / rdo rje'i khams ltar sra zhing brtan pa'i snying po dam pa dang ldan pa'i snying ngo // kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnas
280b4(phal chen): kyi snying ste/ de dag la gnas shing / byang chub sems dpa' rnams de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes snang ba chen po'i snying po dang ldan pa'i snying bla na med pa 'thob par
280b5(phal chen): 'gyur ba dag go/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi go cha ste bcu gang / zhe na/ 'di ltar 'gro ba thams cad yongasu bskyab pa'i
280b6(phal chen): phyirabyams pa chen po'i go cha dang / mi dga' ba thams cad bzod par bya ba'i phyir snying rje chen po'i go cha dang / brtsam pa thams cad mthar phyin par bya ba'i phyir smon lam gyi ga
280b7(phal chen): cha dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rgyun 'byung bar bya ba'i phyir yongs su bsngo ba'i go cha dang / 'gro ba thams cad nye bar 'tsho bar bya ba'i phyir bsod nams kyi go cha dang / 'gro ba thams
280b8(phal chen): cad bsgral ba'i phyir pha rol tu phyin pa'i go cha dang / 'gro ba thams cad kyi nyon mongs pa'i mun pa rab tu zhi bar bya ba'i phyir/ ye shes kyi go cha dang / sgo kun dang ldan pa'i dge ba
281a1(phal chen): rtsa ba mngon par bsgrub pa'i phyir/ thabs mkhas pa'i go cha dang / theg pa gzhan la mos pa med pa'i phyir thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi sems brtan zhing 'khrug pa med
281a2(phal chen): pa'i go cha dang / chos kyi rlom sems med pas gcig tu nges pa'i go cha'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi go cha ste/ de dag la gnas shing / 
281a3(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi bdud kyi sde thams cad spa dkong ba bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi mtshon
281a4(phal chen): ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar ser sna'i spyan rab tu gzhom dpa'i phyir/ gtong ba'i mtshan cha dang / tshul khrim ngas ngan pa thams cad bsal ba'i phyir/ tshul khrims kyi
281a5(phal chen): mtshon cha dang / rnam par rtog pa thams cad bsal ba'i 8/ chos mnyam pa nyid kyi mtshan cha dang / pa thams cad kyi nyon mongs pa yongasu gtsang ba'i phyir/ shes
281a6(phal chen): rab dang ye shes kyi mtshon cha dang / 'tsho ba thams cad la kha na ma tho ba med par bya ba'i phyir/ yang dag pa'i 'tsho ba'i mtshon cha dang / sgo thams cad yongasu bstan pa'i phyir/ thabs
281a7(phal chen): mkhas pa'i mtshon cha dang / nyon mongs pa'i sgo nas sems can bzlog pa'i phyir/ 'dod chags dang / zhe sdang dang / gti mug dang mdor bsdu na/ nyon mongs pa thams
281a8(phal chen): cad kyi mtshon cha dang / spyod pa rgyun mi 'chad pas sems can gyi khams yongasu smin par bya ba'i phyir/ 'khor ba'i mtshon cha dang / mngon par zhen pa thams cad rab tu bsal ba'i byor
281b1(phal chen): chos tshul gcig pa bstan pa'i mtshon cha dang / spyod pa'i sgo las phyir phyogs su mi lta ba'i phyir/ thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi mtshon cha'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ bya
281b2(phal chen): chub sems dpa' rnams kyi mtshon cha ste/ mtshon cha de dag gis byang chub sems dpa' rnams sems can thams cad kyi sems dang / bsam pa la yun ring po'i nye bar nyon mongs pa
281b3(phal chen): dang / bag la nyal ba yod pa thams cad rab tu 'joms pa dag go// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi mgo ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar skye
281b4(phal chen): gtsug da ltar mi snang ba'i phyir mya ngan las 'das pa'i mgo dang / lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten thams cad badra dad par bya ba'i phyir/ bla ma la bdud pa'i mgo dang / snying
281b5(phal chen): gsum thams cad kyi bdag por 'gyur bar bya ba'i phyir/ mos pa yangs pa'i mgo dang / khams gsum gyis mchod par bya ba'i phyir/ dge ba'i rtsa ba thams
281b6(phal chen): cad sngon du 'gro ba'i mgo dang / gtsug tor dang ldan pa'i spyi bo 'thob par bya ba'i phyir/ sems can thams cad kyi khur khyer ba'i mgo dang / thams cad du khyad par du 'gro bar bya
281b7(phal chen): ba'i phyir/ gzhan gyi ltung ba la brnyas pa med pa'i mgo dang / spyi bo la gnas pa'i chos thob par bya ba'i phyir/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i mgo dang / sems
281b8(phal chen): can thams cad kyi mgo mnyam par yongasu bstan pa'i phyir ye shes dang thabs su ldan pa'i mgo dang / 'gro ba thams cad slob par bya ba'i phyir/ sems can thas

282a3(phal chen): pa'i ye shes chen po'i spyi bor gyur pa bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi mig ste/ bcu gang zhe na/

282a5(phal chen): shes rab kyi mig dang / chos thams cad yang dag pa lta ba bzhin du lta ba'i phyir/ chos kyi mog dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu blta ba'i phyir sangs
282a6(phal chen): rgyas kyi mig dang / chos yongasu shes pa lta ba'i phyir ye shes kyi mig dang / sangs rgyas kyi mthu'i 'od snang ba lta ba'i phyir snang ba'i mig dang / mya ngan las 'da' bar bya ba'i phyir
282a7(phal chen): mngon par bsgrub pa'i mig dang / bsgribs pa med par bya ba'i phyir chags pa med pa'i mig dang / chos kyi dbyings sgo thams cad nas lta ba'i phyir thams cad mkhyen pa'i mig
282a8(phal chen): go dkye rgyal po'i sras bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi mig ste/ mig de dag dang ldan pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams de bzhin gshegs
282b1(phal chen): pa'i ye shes chen po'i spyan bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rna ba ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar
282b2(phal chen): bsngags pa thos na dga' ba spong ba dang / mi snyan thos na khong khro ba spong ba dang / nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi gtam thos na 'dod pa med cing mi smon pa dang / byang chub
282b3(phal chen): sems dpa'i 'byung ba'i gtam thos na dga' ba dang / mos pa dang / spro ba chen po skye ba dang / sems can dmyal ba dang byol song gi skye gnas dang / gshin rje'i 'jig rten/ 
282b4(phal chen): dang yi dgas dang / lha ma yin dang / mi khom pa dang dbul por skyes pa thos na snying rje chen po'i go rgyan pa dang / lha dang mi'i rgyud kyi bye brag thos na rtag tu chos
282b5(phal chen): la gzung ba'i blor 'gyur ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi yon tan dang bsngags pa thos na de'i yon tan dang bsngag sa pa yongasu rdzogs par bya ba'i brtson 'grus dang pha rol
282b6(phal chen): tu phyin pa dang / bsdu ba'i dngos po dang / byang chub sems dpa'i sde snod kyi gtam thos na thams cad kyi pha rol tu 'gro ba dang / kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa'i rna ba'i
282b7(phal chen): dbang po la ni phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams nas/ bsgrags pa'i sgra thams cad kyang grag cing thos par 'gyur te/ sgra thams cad sgra brnyan lta bur brjod du med pa'i don du/ 
282b8(phal chen): khong du chud cing shes pa dang / kye rgyal ba'i sras/ byang chub sems dpa'i chos kyi rna ba mnyam par gzhag pa dang ldan te/ thog ma sems bskyed nas snying po byang chub kyi bar du/

283a3(phal chen): sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sna te/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar 'thun pa'i dri la mi mthun par gnas pa dang / mi mthun pa'i dri la mthun par gan+da
283a4(phal chen): padang dri mthun pa dang / mi mthun pa la mnyam pa nyid du gnas pa da dang / dri mthun pa dang / mi mthun pa ma yin pa la btang snyom su gnas pa dang / gos dang / mal cha dang / 
283a5(phal chen): yan lag dang / nying lag gi dril 'dod chags dang / zhe sdang dang / gti mug dang cha mnyam pa la spyod pa'i sems can gyi rgyu shes par gnas pa dang / gter chen
283a6(phal chen): po de dag dang / rtsa dang / gel ba dang / sman dang / nags tshal ji snyed pa de dag gi dris/ gter thams cad mngon sum du shes par gnas pa dang / 'og gi sems can dmyal ba chen
283a7(phal chen): bo mnar med pa yan chad srid pa'i rtse mo man chad la gnas pa'i sems can rnams kyi dri tshor ba tsam gyis/ sngon gyi spyod pa ston par gnas pa dang / nyan thos kyi tshul khrims dang / thos
283a8(phal chen): pa dang / gtong dang shes rab kyi dri tsher bas thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi sems mi 'khrugs par gnas pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi spyod pa'i dri tsher shing / de bzhin
283b1(phal chen): gshegs pa'i sa la yang dag par gzhol ba'i ye shes la gnas pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi yul dang / ye shes kyi dri tsho shing / byang chub sems dpa'i spod pa rgyun
283b2(phal chen): mi gcod par gnas pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sna yongasu dag pa ste/ de dag la gnas shing / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi

283b4(phal chen): gang zhe na/ 'di ltar sems can gyi spyod pa mi zad pa rab tu ston pa'i lce dang / chos kyi tshul mi zad pa rab tu ston pa'i lce dang / sangs rgyas kyi yon tan dang bsdus
283b5(phal chen): pa mi zad pa rab tu ston pa'i lce dang / nges pa'i tshig dang / spobs pa mi zad ba ston pa'i lce dang / theg pa chen po'i tshogs mi zad pa ston pa'i lce dang / de'i lce de phyogs
283b6(phal chen): bcu'i nam mkha' rgyas par 'gengs pa dang / de'i lce de sems can thams cad la yang dag par gzhol ba dang / de'i lce de sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad du 'od kyis snang bar byed pa dang / 
283b7(phal chen): de'i lce de sangs rgyas thams cad mnyes par byed cing / phyag 'tshal ba dang / de'i lce de bdud dang / rgol ba dang / nyon mongs pa dang / 'khor ba thams cad 'jig cing mya ngan las
283b8(phal chen): 'das pa'i lam ston pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lce ste/ de dag la gnas shing / byang chub sems dpa' rnams de bzhin
284a1(phal chen): gshegs pa'i ljags sangs rgyas kyi shing thams cad rgyas par khyab pa tha na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dgag/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu pa 'di dag ni/ byang chub
284a2(phal chen): sems dpa' rnams kyi lus te/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar mi yongasu smon par bya ba'i phyir/ mi'i lus dang / sems can dmyal ba dang / byol song gi skye gnas dang / gshin
284a3(phal chen): rje'i 'jig rten gyi sems can gdul ba'i phyir/ mi ma yin pa'i lus dang / 'dod pa'i khams dang / gzugs kyi khams dang / gzugs med pa na spyod pa'i sems can gdul ba'i phyi
284a4(phal chen): lha'i lus dang / slob pa'i sa bstan pa'i slob pa'i lus dang / mi slob pa'i bstan pa'i phyir/ mi slob pa'i da lus dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi sar gdul ba'i phyir ra
284a5(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi lus dang / theg pa chen po la yang dag par 'byung bar bya ba'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa'i lus dang / dbang bskur ba'i ye shes 'thob par bya ba'i
284a6(phal chen): phyir/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku dang / mngon par bsgrub pa la mkhas par bya ba'i phyir/ yid kyi rang bzhin gyi lus dang / zag pa med cing lhun gyis grub pa'i bya bas/ lus
284a7(phal chen): thams cad yongasu bstan pa'i phyir chos kyi lus so// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lus te/ de dag la gnas shing / byang chub
284a8(phal chen): sems dpa' rnams de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ying rnam par rgyu ba
284b1(phal chen): ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad brtsam pa la yid ni sngon tu 'gro ba'o// nan tan lhur blang ba la yid ni gnas so// sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams la yid ni rjesu zhugs
284b2(phal chen): pa'o// sems can rnams kyi bsam par yid ni khongasu chud pa'o// nyon mongs pa thams cad dang ma 'dres pas yid ni rgyu ba med pa'o// glo bur gyi dri mas kun nas nyon mongs pa med pa'i
284b3(phal chen): phyirayod ni 'od gsal ba'o// dus ji lta ba'i skad cig las kyang mi 'da' ba'i phyir/ yid ni dpyad pa shin tu brtags pa'o// thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med pa'i phyir/ yod ni las
284b4(phal chen): kyi mtha' shin tu dpyad pa'o// dbang po shin tu dul bas yu rang la la mi rgyug pa'i phyir/ yid ni dbang po rab ba'o// / sangs rgyas kyi ting nge 'dzin la bdag gor mi byed pa'i phyir
284b5(phal chen): yid ni shin tu mnyam par gzhog pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras/ bcu po de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi yid rnam par rgyu ba ste/ de dag la gnas shing / byang
284b6(phal chen): chub sems dpa' rnams de bzhin gshegs pa'i thugs rnam par rgyu ba bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams
284b7(phal chen): kyi 'gro ba ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar chos 'dod pas chos nyan du 'gro ba dang / sems can gyi don du chos ston du 'gro ba dang / rang gi sems nges par rtogs pas 'dod pa med
284b8(phal chen): pa dang / sdang ba med pa dang / gti mug med pa dang / 'jigs pa med par 'gro ba dang / sems can yongasu smin par bya ba'i phyir/ 'dod pa'i khamasu 'gro ba dang / myur du
285a1(phal chen): phyir ldog par byabs/ gzugs dang gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug par 'gro ba dang / shes rab myur ba 'thob par bya ba'i phyir/ don dang chos kyi rgyung du 'grob
285a2(phal chen): dang / 'dul ba'i dbang gis skye ba thams cad du 'gro ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa blta ba dang / phyag bya ba dang / bsnyen bkur ba'i phyir sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad du mngon par shes
285a3(phal chen): pas 'gro ba dang / 'khor ba'i rgyud kyi rgyun mi gtsang ba'i phyir/ mya ngan las 'das pa'i rgyud du 'gro ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa rgyun mi gcad pa'i phyir/ sangs rgyas kyi chos
285a4(phal chen): thams cad yong su rdzogs par bya bar 'gro ba'o// kye rma/ la ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa / 'a rnams kyi 'gro ba ste/ de dag la gnas shing / byang chub
285a5(phal chen): sems dpa' rnams de bzhin gshegs pa'i bzhud pa gshe gas pa dang / byon pa med pa bla na med pa 'thob par 'a gyur pa dag go// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang
285a6(phal chen): chub sems dpa' rnams kyi gnas te/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar nyams pa med pa'i phyir/ byang chub kyi sems la gnas pa dang / tshogs kyis mi ngoms pa'i phyir/ pha rol
285a7(phal chen): tu phyin pa la gnas pa dang / shes rab shin tu sbyangs pa'i phyir chos kyi gtam la gnas pa dang / bsam gtan chen po khong du chud par bya ba'i phyir/ bas mtha' dgon pa la gnas
285a8(phal chen): pa dang / bya ba nyung ba'i phyir thams cad mkhyen pa nyid dang 'thun pa'i sbyangs pa'i yon tan dang / chog shes pa dang / 'phags pa'i rgyud la gnas pa dang / chos kyi brtson
285b1(phal chen): 'grus rjes su 'brang bar bya ba'i phyir nan tan la gnas pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi spyod lam yong su rdzogs par bya ba'i phyir/ de bzhin gshegs pa bsnyen bkur ba la gnas pa dang / ye shes
285b2(phal chen): chen po yongasasu rdzogs par bya ba'i phyir/ mngon par shes pas 'byung ba la gnas pa dang / lung bstan pa yongs su rdzogs par bya ba'i phyir/ bzod pa thob pa la gnas pa dang / sangs

285b5(phal chen): sems dpa' rnams kyi stan la 'dug pa ste/ bcu gang / zhe na/ 'di ltar dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam sgrub pa 'i phyir/ 'khor los bsgyur ba'i stan la 'dug pa
285b6(phal chen): dang 'jig rten thams cad sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi dbang phyug la dgod pa'i phyir/ 'jig rten gyi mgon po'i stan la 'dug pa dang / 'gro ba thams cad kyi dbang por 'gyur ba'i phyir/ 
285b7(phal chen): brgya byin gyi stan la 'dug pa dang / rang gi sems dang gzhan gyi sems la dbang sgyur ba'i phyir/ tshangs pa'i stan la 'dug pa dang / chos kyi gtam ma nor bar bya ba'i phyir/ seng ge
285b8(phal chen): stan la 'jug pa dang / gzungs dang spongs pa'i stobs kyis brjod pa'i phyir/ chos kyi stan la 'dug pa dang / dam bcas pa'i mthar phyin par bya ba'i phyir/ yi dam la brtan
286a1(phal chen): pa'i stan la 'dug pa dang / gshe ba dang / sdang ba la byams par bya ba'i phyir/ byams pa chen po'i stan la 'dug pa dang / mi dga' ba thams cad bzod par bya bas mi
286a2(phal chen): bar bya ba'i phyir/ snying rje chen po'i stan la 'dug pa ste/ phas kyi rgol ba dang / bdud kyi sde thams cad bzlog pa'i phyir/ rdo rje'i stan la 'dug pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i
286a3(phal chen): sras bcu po de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi stan la 'dug pa ste/ de dag la gnas shing byang chub sems dpa' rnams de bzhin gshegs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi gdan chen
286a4(phal chen): po bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go// kye rgyal sras bcu po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi/ lam te/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar lus dang sems
286a5(phal chen): dben par bya ba'i phyir/ dben pa'i mal dang tshul bzhin gyi sbyor ba sgrub pa'i phyir/ nang du yang dag par gzhog pa'i mal dang / lus dang sems la su
286a6(phal chen): rung bar bya ba'i phyir/ snyoms par 'jug pa'i mal dang / gzhan dang bdag la gdung ba med par bya ba'i phyir/ tshangs pa'i mal dang / phyis 'gyod pa med par bya ba'i phyir/ 
286a7(phal chen): legs pa'i las kyi mal dang / phyis khro ba med par bya ba'i phyir/ yang dag pa'i nan tan gyi mal dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyis bskul bar bya ba'i phyir/ las kyi
286a8(phal chen): mal dang / yongasu bsngo ba la mkhas pa'i phyir/ shin tu mnyam par bzhag pa'i mal dang / brtsams pa mthar phyin par bya ba'i phyir/ dgos pa thams cad yongs su
286b1(phal chen): sgrub pa'i mal dang / sngon las legs par spyad pa'i phyir/ lhun gyis grub par spyod pa'i malo// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi mal
286b2(phal chen): te/ de dag la gnas shing / byang chub sems dpa' rnams de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos kyi gzims mal chen por rnam par 'tshang rgya ba bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go/
